00127         // Compare two strings
00128         bool strequal(const char_t* src, const char_t* dst)
00129         {
00130                 assert(src && dst);
00131 
00132         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
00133                 return wcscmp(src, dst) == 0;
00134         #else
00135                 return strcmp(src, dst) == 0;
00136         #endif
00137         }
00138 
00139         // Compare lhs with [rhs_begin, rhs_end)
00140         bool strequalrange(const char_t* lhs, const char_t* rhs, size_t count)
00141         {
00142                 for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i)
00143                         if (lhs[i] != rhs[i])
00144                                 return false;
00145         
00146                 return lhs[count] == 0;
00147         }

00152         {
00153                 for (const char* i = source; *i; ++i) *dest++ = *i;
00154                 *dest = 0;
00155         }

00200         {
00201                 static xml_memory_page* construct(void* memory)
00202                 {
00203                         if (!memory) return 0; //$ redundant, left for performance
00204

00211                         result->busy_size = 0;
00212                         result->freed_size = 0;

00236         struct xml_allocator
00237         {
00238                 xml_allocator(xml_memory_page* root): _root(root), _busy_size(root->busy_size)
00239                 {
00240                 }
00241 
00242                 xml_memory_page* allocate_page(size_t data_size)
00243                 {
00244                         size_t size = offsetof(xml_memory_page, data) + data_size;
00245 
00246                         // allocate block with some alignment, leaving memory for worst-case padding
00247                         void* memory = global_allocate(size + xml_memory_page_alignment);
00248                         if (!memory) return 0;
00249 
00250                         // align upwards to page boundary
00251                         void* page_memory = reinterpret_cast<void*>((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(memory) + (xml_memory_page_alignment - 1)) & ~(xml_memory_page_alignment - 1));
00252 
00253                         // prepare page structure
00254                         xml_memory_page* page = xml_memory_page::construct(page_memory);
00255 
00256                         page->memory = memory;
00257                         page->allocator = _root->allocator;
00258 
00259                         return page;
00260                 }
00261 
00262                 static void deallocate_page(xml_memory_page* page)
00263                 {
00264                         global_deallocate(page->memory);
00265                 }
00266 
00267                 void* allocate_memory_oob(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page);
00268 
00269                 void* allocate_memory(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page)
00270                 {
00271                         if (_busy_size + size > xml_memory_page_size) return allocate_memory_oob(size, out_page);
00272 
00273                         void* buf = _root->data + _busy_size;
00274 
00275                         _busy_size += size;
00276 
00277                         out_page = _root;
00278 
00279                         return buf;
00280                 }
00281 
00282                 void deallocate_memory(void* ptr, size_t size, xml_memory_page* page)
00283                 {
00284                         if (page == _root) page->busy_size = _busy_size;
00285 
00286                         assert(ptr >= page->data && ptr < page->data + page->busy_size);
00287                         (void)!ptr;
00288 
00289                         page->freed_size += size;
00290                         assert(page->freed_size <= page->busy_size);
00291 
00292                         if (page->freed_size == page->busy_size)
00293                         {
00294                                 if (page->next == 0)
00295                                 {
00296                                         assert(_root == page);
00297 
00298                                         // top page freed, just reset sizes
00299                                         page->busy_size = page->freed_size = 0;
00300                                         _busy_size = 0;
00301                                 }
00302                                 else
00303                                 {
00304                                         assert(_root != page);
00305                                         assert(page->prev);
00306 
00307                                         // remove from the list
00308                                         page->prev->next = page->next;
00309                                         page->next->prev = page->prev;
00310 
00311                                         // deallocate
00312                                         deallocate_page(page);
00313                                 }
00314                         }
00315                 }
00316 
00317                 char_t* allocate_string(size_t length)
00318                 {
00319                         // allocate memory for string and header block
00320                         size_t size = sizeof(xml_memory_string_header) + length * sizeof(char_t);
00321                         
00322                         // round size up to pointer alignment boundary
00323                         size_t full_size = (size + (sizeof(void*) - 1)) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
00324 
00325                         xml_memory_page* page;
00326                         xml_memory_string_header* header = static_cast<xml_memory_string_header*>(allocate_memory(full_size, page));
00327 
00328                         if (!header) return 0;
00329 
00330                         // setup header
00331                         ptrdiff_t page_offset = reinterpret_cast<char*>(header) - page->data;
00332 
00333                         assert(page_offset >= 0 && page_offset < (1 << 16));
00334                         header->page_offset = static_cast<uint16_t>(page_offset);
00335 
00336                         // full_size == 0 for large strings that occupy the whole page
00337                         assert(full_size < (1 << 16) || (page->busy_size == full_size && page_offset == 0));
00338                         header->full_size = static_cast<uint16_t>(full_size < (1 << 16) ? full_size : 0);
00339 
00340                         return reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(header + 1);
00341                 }
00342 
00343                 void deallocate_string(char_t* string)
00344                 {
00345                         // get header
00346                         xml_memory_string_header* header = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_string_header*>(string) - 1;
00347 
00348                         // deallocate
00349                         size_t page_offset = offsetof(xml_memory_page, data) + header->page_offset;
00350                         xml_memory_page* page = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(reinterpret_cast<char*>(header) - page_offset);
00351 
00352                         // if full_size == 0 then this string occupies the whole page
00353                         size_t full_size = header->full_size == 0 ? page->busy_size : header->full_size;
00354 
00355                         deallocate_memory(header, full_size, page);
00356                 }
00357 
00358                 xml_memory_page* _root;
00359                 size_t _busy_size;
00360         };
00361 
00362         PUGIXML_NO_INLINE void* xml_allocator::allocate_memory_oob(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page)
00363         {
00364                 const size_t large_allocation_threshold = xml_memory_page_size / 4;
00365 
00366                 xml_memory_page* page = allocate_page(size <= large_allocation_threshold ? xml_memory_page_size : size);
00367                 if (!page) return 0;
00368 
00369                 if (size <= large_allocation_threshold)
00370                 {
00371                         _root->busy_size = _busy_size;
00372 
00373                         // insert page at the end of linked list
00374                         page->prev = _root;
00375                         _root->next = page;
00376                         _root = page;
00377 
00378                         _busy_size = size;
00379                 }
00380                 else
00381                 {
00382                         // insert page before the end of linked list, so that it is deleted as soon as possible
00383                         // the last page is not deleted even if it's empty (see deallocate_memory)
00384                         assert(_root->prev);
00385 
00386                         page->prev = _root->prev;
00387                         page->next = _root;
00388 
00389                         _root->prev->next = page;
00390                         _root->prev = page;
00391                 }
00392 
00393                 // allocate inside page
00394                 page->busy_size = size;
00395 
00396                 out_page = page;
00397                 return page->data;
00398         }
00399 }

00483         inline void destroy_attribute(xml_attribute_struct* a, xml_allocator& alloc)
00484         {
00485                 uintptr_t header = a->header;
00486 
00487                 if (header & xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(a->name);
00488                 if (header & xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(a->value);
00489 
00490                 alloc.deallocate_memory(a, sizeof(xml_attribute_struct), reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask));
00491         }
00492 
00493         inline void destroy_node(xml_node_struct* n, xml_allocator& alloc)
00494         {
00495                 uintptr_t header = n->header;
00496 
00497                 if (header & xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(n->name);
00498                 if (header & xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(n->value);
00499 
00500                 for (xml_attribute_struct* attr = n->first_attribute; attr; )
00501                 {
00502                         xml_attribute_struct* next = attr->next_attribute;
00503 
00504                         destroy_attribute(attr, alloc);
00505 
00506                         attr = next;
00507                 }
00508 
00509                 for (xml_node_struct* child = n->first_child; child; )
00510                 {
00511                         xml_node_struct* next = child->next_sibling;
00512 
00513                         destroy_node(child, alloc);
00514 
00515                         child = next;
00516                 }
00517 
00518                 alloc.deallocate_memory(n, sizeof(xml_node_struct), reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask));
00519         }

00521         PUGIXML_NO_INLINE xml_node_struct* append_node(xml_node_struct* node, xml_allocator& alloc, xml_node_type type = node_element)
00522         {
00523                 xml_node_struct* child = allocate_node(alloc, type);
00524                 if (!child) return 0;
00525 
00526                 child->parent = node;
00527 
00528                 xml_node_struct* first_child = node->first_child;
00529                         
00530                 if (first_child)
00531                 {
00532                         xml_node_struct* last_child = first_child->prev_sibling_c;
00533 
00534                         last_child->next_sibling = child;
00535                         child->prev_sibling_c = last_child;
00536                         first_child->prev_sibling_c = child;
00537                 }
00538                 else
00539                 {
00540                         node->first_child = child;
00541                         child->prev_sibling_c = child;
00542                 }
00543                         
00544                 return child;
00545         }

00589         inline uint16_t endian_swap(uint16_t value)
00590         {
00591                 return static_cast<uint16_t>(((value & 0xff) << 8) | (value >> 8));
00592         }
00593 
00594         inline uint32_t endian_swap(uint32_t value)
00595         {
00596                 return ((value & 0xff) << 24) | ((value & 0xff00) << 8) | ((value & 0xff0000) >> 8) | (value >> 24);
00597         }
00598 
00599         struct utf8_counter
00600         {
00601                 typedef size_t value_type;
00602 
00603                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00604                 {
00605                         // U+0000..U+007F
00606                         if (ch < 0x80) return result + 1;
00607                         // U+0080..U+07FF
00608                         else if (ch < 0x800) return result + 2;
00609                         // U+0800..U+FFFF
00610                         else return result + 3;
00611                 }
00612 
00613                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00614                 {
00615                         // U+10000..U+10FFFF
00616                         return result + 4;
00617                 }
00618         };
00619 
00620         struct utf8_writer
00621         {
00622                 typedef uint8_t* value_type;
00623 
00624                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00625                 {
00626                         // U+0000..U+007F
00627                         if (ch < 0x80)
00628                         {
00629                                 *result = static_cast<uint8_t>(ch);
00630                                 return result + 1;
00631                         }
00632                         // U+0080..U+07FF
00633                         else if (ch < 0x800)
00634                         {
00635                                 result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xC0 | (ch >> 6));
00636                                 result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00637                                 return result + 2;
00638                         }
00639                         // U+0800..U+FFFF
00640                         else
00641                         {
00642                                 result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xE0 | (ch >> 12));
00643                                 result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 6) & 0x3F));
00644                                 result[2] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00645                                 return result + 3;
00646                         }
00647                 }
00648 
00649                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00650                 {
00651                         // U+10000..U+10FFFF
00652                         result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xF0 | (ch >> 18));
00653                         result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 12) & 0x3F));
00654                         result[2] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 6) & 0x3F));
00655                         result[3] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00656                         return result + 4;
00657                 }
00658 
00659                 static value_type any(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00660                 {
00661                         return (ch < 0x10000) ? low(result, ch) : high(result, ch);
00662                 }
00663         };
00664 
00665         struct utf16_counter
00666         {
00667                 typedef size_t value_type;
00668 
00669                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t)
00670                 {
00671                         return result + 1;
00672                 }
00673 
00674                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00675                 {
00676                         return result + 2;
00677                 }
00678         };
00679 
00680         struct utf16_writer
00681         {
00682                 typedef uint16_t* value_type;
00683 
00684                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00685                 {
00686                         *result = static_cast<uint16_t>(ch);
00687 
00688                         return result + 1;
00689                 }
00690 
00691                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00692                 {
00693                         uint32_t msh = (uint32_t)(ch - 0x10000) >> 10;
00694                         uint32_t lsh = (uint32_t)(ch - 0x10000) & 0x3ff;
00695 
00696                         result[0] = static_cast<uint16_t>(0xD800 + msh);
00697                         result[1] = static_cast<uint16_t>(0xDC00 + lsh);
00698 
00699                         return result + 2;
00700                 }
00701 
00702                 static value_type any(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00703                 {
00704                         return (ch < 0x10000) ? low(result, ch) : high(result, ch);
00705                 }
00706         };
00707 
00708         struct utf32_counter
00709         {
00710                 typedef size_t value_type;
00711 
00712                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t)
00713                 {
00714                         return result + 1;
00715                 }
00716 
00717                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00718                 {
00719                         return result + 1;
00720                 }
00721         };
00722 
00723         struct utf32_writer
00724         {
00725                 typedef uint32_t* value_type;
00726 
00727                 static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00728                 {
00729                         *result = ch;
00730 
00731                         return result + 1;
00732                 }
00733 
00734                 static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00735                 {
00736                         *result = ch;
00737 
00738                         return result + 1;
00739                 }
00740 
00741                 static value_type any(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00742                 {
00743                         *result = ch;
00744 
00745                         return result + 1;
00746                 }
00747         };
00748 
00749         template <size_t size> struct wchar_selector;
00750 
00751         template <> struct wchar_selector<2>
00752         {
00753                 typedef uint16_t type;
00754                 typedef utf16_counter counter;
00755                 typedef utf16_writer writer;
00756         };
00757 
00758         template <> struct wchar_selector<4>
00759         {
00760                 typedef uint32_t type;
00761                 typedef utf32_counter counter;
00762                 typedef utf32_writer writer;
00763         };
00764 
00765         typedef wchar_selector<sizeof(wchar_t)>::counter wchar_counter;
00766         typedef wchar_selector<sizeof(wchar_t)>::writer wchar_writer;
00767 
00768         template <typename Traits, typename opt_swap = opt_false> struct utf_decoder
00769         {
00770                 static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf8_block(const uint8_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
00771                 {
00772                         const uint8_t utf8_byte_mask = 0x3f;
00773 
00774                         while (size)
00775                         {
00776                                 uint8_t lead = *data;
00777 
00778                                 // 0xxxxxxx -> U+0000..U+007F
00779                                 if (lead < 0x80)
00780                                 {
00781                                         result = Traits::low(result, lead);
00782                                         data += 1;
00783                                         size -= 1;
00784 
00785                                         // process aligned single-byte (ascii) blocks
00786                                         if ((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(data) & 3) == 0)
00787                                         {
00788                                                 while (size >= 4 && (*reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(data) & 0x80808080) == 0)
00789                                                 {
00790                                                         result = Traits::low(result, data[0]);
00791                                                         result = Traits::low(result, data[1]);
00792                                                         result = Traits::low(result, data[2]);
00793                                                         result = Traits::low(result, data[3]);
00794                                                         data += 4;
00795                                                         size -= 4;
00796                                                 }
00797                                         }
00798                                 }
00799                                 // 110xxxxx -> U+0080..U+07FF
00800                                 else if ((unsigned)(lead - 0xC0) < 0x20 && size >= 2 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
00801                                 {
00802                                         result = Traits::low(result, ((lead & ~0xC0) << 6) | (data[1] & utf8_byte_mask));
00803                                         data += 2;
00804                                         size -= 2;
00805                                 }
00806                                 // 1110xxxx -> U+0800-U+FFFF
00807                                 else if ((unsigned)(lead - 0xE0) < 0x10 && size >= 3 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[2] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
00808                                 {
00809                                         result = Traits::low(result, ((lead & ~0xE0) << 12) | ((data[1] & utf8_byte_mask) << 6) | (data[2] & utf8_byte_mask));
00810                                         data += 3;
00811                                         size -= 3;
00812                                 }
00813                                 // 11110xxx -> U+10000..U+10FFFF
00814                                 else if ((unsigned)(lead - 0xF0) < 0x08 && size >= 4 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[2] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[3] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
00815                                 {
00816                                         result = Traits::high(result, ((lead & ~0xF0) << 18) | ((data[1] & utf8_byte_mask) << 12) | ((data[2] & utf8_byte_mask) << 6) | (data[3] & utf8_byte_mask));
00817                                         data += 4;
00818                                         size -= 4;
00819                                 }
00820                                 // 10xxxxxx or 11111xxx -> invalid
00821                                 else
00822                                 {
00823                                         data += 1;
00824                                         size -= 1;
00825                                 }
00826                         }
00827 
00828                         return result;
00829                 }
00830 
00831                 static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf16_block(const uint16_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
00832                 {
00833                         const uint16_t* end = data + size;
00834 
00835                         while (data < end)
00836                         {
00837                                 uint16_t lead = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(*data) : *data;
00838 
00839                                 // U+0000..U+D7FF
00840                                 if (lead < 0xD800)
00841                                 {
00842                                         result = Traits::low(result, lead);
00843                                         data += 1;
00844                                 }
00845                                 // U+E000..U+FFFF
00846                                 else if ((unsigned)(lead - 0xE000) < 0x2000)
00847                                 {
00848                                         result = Traits::low(result, lead);
00849                                         data += 1;
00850                                 }
00851                                 // surrogate pair lead
00852                                 else if ((unsigned)(lead - 0xD800) < 0x400 && data + 1 < end)
00853                                 {
00854                                         uint16_t next = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(data[1]) : data[1];
00855 
00856                                         if ((unsigned)(next - 0xDC00) < 0x400)
00857                                         {
00858                                                 result = Traits::high(result, 0x10000 + ((lead & 0x3ff) << 10) + (next & 0x3ff));
00859                                                 data += 2;
00860                                         }
00861                                         else
00862                                         {
00863                                                 data += 1;
00864                                         }
00865                                 }
00866                                 else
00867                                 {
00868                                         data += 1;
00869                                 }
00870                         }
00871 
00872                         return result;
00873                 }
00874 
00875                 static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf32_block(const uint32_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
00876                 {
00877                         const uint32_t* end = data + size;
00878 
00879                         while (data < end)
00880                         {
00881                                 uint32_t lead = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(*data) : *data;
00882 
00883                                 // U+0000..U+FFFF
00884                                 if (lead < 0x10000)
00885                                 {
00886                                         result = Traits::low(result, lead);
00887                                         data += 1;
00888                                 }
00889                                 // U+10000..U+10FFFF
00890                                 else
00891                                 {
00892                                         result = Traits::high(result, lead);
00893                                         data += 1;
00894                                 }
00895                         }
00896 
00897                         return result;
00898                 }
00899         };
00900 
00901         template <typename T> inline void convert_utf_endian_swap(T* result, const T* data, size_t length)
00902         {
00903                 for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) result[i] = endian_swap(data[i]);
00904         }
00905 
00906         inline void convert_wchar_endian_swap(wchar_t* result, const wchar_t* data, size_t length)
00907         {
00908                 for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) result[i] = static_cast<wchar_t>(endian_swap(static_cast<wchar_selector<sizeof(wchar_t)>::type>(data[i])));
00909         }
00910 }

00987         bool is_little_endian()
00988         {
00989                 unsigned int ui = 1;
00990 
00991                 return *reinterpret_cast<unsigned char*>(&ui) == 1;
00992         }
00993 
00994         xml_encoding get_wchar_encoding()
00995         {
00996                 STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 || sizeof(wchar_t) == 4);
00997 
00998                 if (sizeof(wchar_t) == 2)
00999                         return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01000                 else 
01001                         return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01002         }
01003 
01004         xml_encoding guess_buffer_encoding(uint8_t d0, uint8_t d1, uint8_t d2, uint8_t d3)
01005         {
01006                 // look for BOM in first few bytes
01007                 if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0xfe && d3 == 0xff) return encoding_utf32_be;
01008                 if (d0 == 0xff && d1 == 0xfe && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf32_le;
01009                 if (d0 == 0xfe && d1 == 0xff) return encoding_utf16_be;
01010                 if (d0 == 0xff && d1 == 0xfe) return encoding_utf16_le;
01011                 if (d0 == 0xef && d1 == 0xbb && d2 == 0xbf) return encoding_utf8;
01012 
01013                 // look for <, <? or <?xm in various encodings
01014                 if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0x3c) return encoding_utf32_be;
01015                 if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf32_le;
01016                 if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0x3c && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0x3f) return encoding_utf16_be;
01017                 if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0x3f && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf16_le;
01018                 if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0x3f && d2 == 0x78 && d3 == 0x6d) return encoding_utf8;
01019 
01020                 // look for utf16 < followed by node name (this may fail, but is better than utf8 since it's zero terminated so early)
01021                 if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0x3c) return encoding_utf16_be;
01022                 if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0) return encoding_utf16_le;
01023 
01024                 // no known BOM detected, assume utf8
01025                 return encoding_utf8;
01026         }
01027 
01028         xml_encoding get_buffer_encoding(xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size)
01029         {
01030                 // replace wchar encoding with utf implementation
01031                 if (encoding == encoding_wchar) return get_wchar_encoding();
01032 
01033                 // replace utf16 encoding with utf16 with specific endianness
01034                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01035 
01036                 // replace utf32 encoding with utf32 with specific endianness
01037                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01038 
01039                 // only do autodetection if no explicit encoding is requested
01040                 if (encoding != encoding_auto) return encoding;
01041 
01042                 // skip encoding autodetection if input buffer is too small
01043                 if (size < 4) return encoding_utf8;
01044 
01045                 // try to guess encoding (based on XML specification, Appendix F.1)
01046                 const uint8_t* data = static_cast<const uint8_t*>(contents);
01047 
01048                 DMC_VOLATILE uint8_t d0 = data[0], d1 = data[1], d2 = data[2], d3 = data[3];
01049 
01050                 return guess_buffer_encoding(d0, d1, d2, d3);
01051         }
01052 
01053         bool get_mutable_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01054         {
01055                 if (is_mutable)
01056                 {
01057                         out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(const_cast<void*>(contents));
01058                 }
01059                 else
01060                 {
01061                         void* buffer = global_allocate(size > 0 ? size : 1);
01062                         if (!buffer) return false;
01063 
01064                         memcpy(buffer, contents, size);
01065 
01066                         out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(buffer);
01067                 }
01068 
01069                 out_length = size / sizeof(char_t);
01070 
01071                 return true;
01072         }
01073 
01074 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01075         inline bool need_endian_swap_utf(xml_encoding le, xml_encoding re)
01076         {
01077                 return (le == encoding_utf16_be && re == encoding_utf16_le) || (le == encoding_utf16_le && re == encoding_utf16_be) ||
01078                        (le == encoding_utf32_be && re == encoding_utf32_le) || (le == encoding_utf32_le && re == encoding_utf32_be);
01079         }
01080 
01081         bool convert_buffer_endian_swap(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01082         {
01083                 const char_t* data = static_cast<const char_t*>(contents);
01084         
01085                 if (is_mutable)
01086                 {
01087                         out_buffer = const_cast<char_t*>(data);
01088                 }
01089                 else
01090                 {
01091                         out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate(size > 0 ? size : 1));
01092                         if (!out_buffer) return false;
01093                 }
01094 
01095                 out_length = size / sizeof(char_t);
01096 
01097                 convert_wchar_endian_swap(out_buffer, data, out_length);
01098 
01099                 return true;
01100         }
01101 
01102         bool convert_buffer_utf8(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size)
01103         {
01104                 const uint8_t* data = static_cast<const uint8_t*>(contents);
01105 
01106                 // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01107                 out_length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, 0);
01108 
01109                 // allocate buffer of suitable length
01110                 out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((out_length > 0 ? out_length : 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01111                 if (!out_buffer) return false;
01112 
01113                 // second pass: convert utf8 input to wchar_t
01114                 wchar_writer::value_type out_begin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(out_buffer);
01115                 wchar_writer::value_type out_end = utf_decoder<wchar_writer>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, out_begin);
01116 
01117                 assert(out_end == out_begin + out_length);
01118                 (void)!out_end;
01119 
01120                 return true;
01121         }
01122 
01123         template <typename opt_swap> bool convert_buffer_utf16(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01124         {
01125                 const uint16_t* data = static_cast<const uint16_t*>(contents);
01126                 size_t length = size / sizeof(uint16_t);
01127 
01128                 // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01129                 out_length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, length, 0);
01130 
01131                 // allocate buffer of suitable length
01132                 out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((out_length > 0 ? out_length : 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01133                 if (!out_buffer) return false;
01134 
01135                 // second pass: convert utf16 input to wchar_t
01136                 wchar_writer::value_type out_begin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(out_buffer);
01137                 wchar_writer::value_type out_end = utf_decoder<wchar_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, length, out_begin);
01138 
01139                 assert(out_end == out_begin + out_length);
01140                 (void)!out_end;
01141 
01142                 return true;
01143         }
01144 
01145         template <typename opt_swap> bool convert_buffer_utf32(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01146         {
01147                 const uint32_t* data = static_cast<const uint32_t*>(contents);
01148                 size_t length = size / sizeof(uint32_t);
01149 
01150                 // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01151                 out_length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, length, 0);
01152 
01153                 // allocate buffer of suitable length
01154                 out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((out_length > 0 ? out_length : 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01155                 if (!out_buffer) return false;
01156 
01157                 // second pass: convert utf32 input to wchar_t
01158                 wchar_writer::value_type out_begin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(out_buffer);
01159                 wchar_writer::value_type out_end = utf_decoder<wchar_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, length, out_begin);
01160 
01161                 assert(out_end == out_begin + out_length);
01162                 (void)!out_end;
01163 
01164                 return true;
01165         }
01166 
01167         bool convert_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01168         {
01169                 // get native encoding
01170                 xml_encoding wchar_encoding = get_wchar_encoding();
01171 
01172                 // fast path: no conversion required
01173                 if (encoding == wchar_encoding) return get_mutable_buffer(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01174 
01175                 // only endian-swapping is required
01176                 if (need_endian_swap_utf(encoding, wchar_encoding)) return convert_buffer_endian_swap(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01177 
01178                 // source encoding is utf8
01179                 if (encoding == encoding_utf8) return convert_buffer_utf8(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size);
01180 
01181                 // source encoding is utf16
01182                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
01183                 {
01184                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01185 
01186                         return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01187                                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01188                                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01189                 }
01190 
01191                 // source encoding is utf32
01192                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
01193                 {
01194                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01195 
01196                         return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01197                                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01198                                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01199                 }
01200 
01201                 assert(!"Invalid encoding");
01202                 return false;
01203         }
01204 #else
01205         template <typename opt_swap> bool convert_buffer_utf16(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01206         {
01207                 const uint16_t* data = static_cast<const uint16_t*>(contents);
01208                 size_t length = size / sizeof(uint16_t);
01209 
01210                 // first pass: get length in utf8 units
01211                 out_length = utf_decoder<utf8_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, length, 0);
01212 
01213                 // allocate buffer of suitable length
01214                 out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((out_length > 0 ? out_length : 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01215                 if (!out_buffer) return false;
01216 
01217                 // second pass: convert utf16 input to utf8
01218                 uint8_t* out_begin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(out_buffer);
01219                 uint8_t* out_end = utf_decoder<utf8_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, length, out_begin);
01220 
01221                 assert(out_end == out_begin + out_length);
01222                 (void)!out_end;
01223 
01224                 return true;
01225         }
01226 
01227         template <typename opt_swap> bool convert_buffer_utf32(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01228         {
01229                 const uint32_t* data = static_cast<const uint32_t*>(contents);
01230                 size_t length = size / sizeof(uint32_t);
01231 
01232                 // first pass: get length in utf8 units
01233                 out_length = utf_decoder<utf8_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, length, 0);
01234 
01235                 // allocate buffer of suitable length
01236                 out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((out_length > 0 ? out_length : 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01237                 if (!out_buffer) return false;
01238 
01239                 // second pass: convert utf32 input to utf8
01240                 uint8_t* out_begin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(out_buffer);
01241                 uint8_t* out_end = utf_decoder<utf8_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, length, out_begin);
01242 
01243                 assert(out_end == out_begin + out_length);
01244                 (void)!out_end;
01245 
01246                 return true;
01247         }
01248 
01249         bool convert_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01250         {
01251                 // fast path: no conversion required
01252                 if (encoding == encoding_utf8) return get_mutable_buffer(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01253 
01254                 // source encoding is utf16
01255                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
01256                 {
01257                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01258 
01259                         return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01260                                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01261                                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01262                 }
01263 
01264                 // source encoding is utf32
01265                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
01266                 {
01267                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01268 
01269                         return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01270                                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01271                                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01272                 }
01273 
01274                 assert(!"Invalid encoding");
01275                 return false;
01276         }
01277 #endif
01278 
01279         size_t as_utf8_begin(const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01280         {
01281                 STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 || sizeof(wchar_t) == 4);
01282 
01283                 // get length in utf8 characters
01284                 return sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 ?
01285                         utf_decoder<utf8_counter>::decode_utf16_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint16_t*>(str), length, 0) :
01286                         utf_decoder<utf8_counter>::decode_utf32_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(str), length, 0);
01287     }
01288 
01289     void as_utf8_end(char* buffer, size_t size, const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01290     {
01291                 STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 || sizeof(wchar_t) == 4);
01292 
01293         // convert to utf8
01294         uint8_t* begin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer);
01295         uint8_t* end = sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 ?
01296             utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_utf16_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint16_t*>(str), length, begin) :
01297             utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_utf32_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(str), length, begin);
01298     
01299         assert(begin + size == end);
01300         (void)!end;
01301 
01302                 // zero-terminate
01303                 buffer[size] = 0;
01304         }
01305     
01306 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
01307     std::string as_utf8_impl(const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01308     {
01309                 // first pass: get length in utf8 characters
01310         size_t size = as_utf8_begin(str, length);
01311 
01312                 // allocate resulting string
01313                 std::string result;
01314                 result.resize(size);
01315 
01316                 // second pass: convert to utf8
01317                 if (size > 0) as_utf8_end(&result[0], size, str, length);
01318 
01319                 return result;
01320     }
01321 
01322         std::wstring as_wide_impl(const char* str, size_t size)
01323         {
01324                 const uint8_t* data = reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(str);
01325 
01326                 // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01327                 size_t length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, 0);
01328 
01329                 // allocate resulting string
01330                 std::wstring result;
01331                 result.resize(length);
01332 
01333                 // second pass: convert to wchar_t
01334                 if (length > 0)
01335                 {
01336                         wchar_writer::value_type begin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(&result[0]);
01337                         wchar_writer::value_type end = utf_decoder<wchar_writer>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, begin);
01338 
01339                         assert(begin + length == end);
01340                         (void)!end;
01341                 }
01342 
01343                 return result;
01344         }
01345 #endif
01346 
01347         inline bool strcpy_insitu_allow(size_t length, uintptr_t allocated, char_t* target)
01348         {
01349                 assert(target);
01350                 size_t target_length = strlength(target);
01351 
01352                 // always reuse document buffer memory if possible
01353                 if (!allocated) return target_length >= length;
01354 
01355                 // reuse heap memory if waste is not too great
01356                 const size_t reuse_threshold = 32;
01357 
01358                 return target_length >= length && (target_length < reuse_threshold || target_length - length < target_length / 2);
01359         }
01360 
01361         bool strcpy_insitu(char_t*& dest, uintptr_t& header, uintptr_t header_mask, const char_t* source)
01362         {
01363                 size_t source_length = strlength(source);
01364 
01365                 if (source_length == 0)
01366                 {
01367                         // empty string and null pointer are equivalent, so just deallocate old memory
01368                         xml_allocator* alloc = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask)->allocator;
01369 
01370                         if (header & header_mask) alloc->deallocate_string(dest);
01371                         
01372                         // mark the string as not allocated
01373                         dest = 0;
01374                         header &= ~header_mask;
01375 
01376                         return true;
01377                 }
01378                 else if (dest && strcpy_insitu_allow(source_length, header & header_mask, dest))
01379                 {
01380                         // we can reuse old buffer, so just copy the new data (including zero terminator)
01381                         memcpy(dest, source, (source_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
01382                         
01383                         return true;
01384                 }
01385                 else
01386                 {
01387                         xml_allocator* alloc = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask)->allocator;
01388 
01389                         // allocate new buffer
01390                         char_t* buf = alloc->allocate_string(source_length + 1);
01391                         if (!buf) return false;
01392 
01393                         // copy the string (including zero terminator)
01394                         memcpy(buf, source, (source_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
01395 
01396                         // deallocate old buffer (*after* the above to protect against overlapping memory and/or allocation failures)
01397                         if (header & header_mask) alloc->deallocate_string(dest);
01398                         
01399                         // the string is now allocated, so set the flag
01400                         dest = buf;
01401                         header |= header_mask;
01402 
01403                         return true;
01404                 }
01405         }
01406 
01407         struct gap
01408         {
01409                 char_t* end;
01410                 size_t size;
01411                         
01412                 gap(): end(0), size(0)
01413                 {
01414                 }
01415                         
01416                 // Push new gap, move s count bytes further (skipping the gap).
01417                 // Collapse previous gap.
01418                 void push(char_t*& s, size_t count)
01419                 {
01420                         if (end) // there was a gap already; collapse it
01421                         {
01422                                 // Move [old_gap_end, new_gap_start) to [old_gap_start, ...)
01423                                 assert(s >= end);
01424                                 memmove(end - size, end, reinterpret_cast<char*>(s) - reinterpret_cast<char*>(end));
01425                         }
01426                                 
01427                         s += count; // end of current gap
01428                                 
01429                         // "merge" two gaps
01430                         end = s;
01431                         size += count;
01432                 }
01433                         
01434                 // Collapse all gaps, return past-the-end pointer
01435                 char_t* flush(char_t* s)
01436                 {
01437                         if (end)
01438                         {
01439                                 // Move [old_gap_end, current_pos) to [old_gap_start, ...)
01440                                 assert(s >= end);
01441                                 memmove(end - size, end, reinterpret_cast<char*>(s) - reinterpret_cast<char*>(end));
01442 
01443                                 return s - size;
01444                         }
01445                         else return s;
01446                 }
01447         };
01448         
01449         char_t* strconv_escape(char_t* s, gap& g)
01450         {
01451                 char_t* stre = s + 1;
01452 
01453                 switch (*stre)
01454                 {
01455                         case '#':       // &#...
01456                         {
01457                                 unsigned int ucsc = 0;
01458 
01459                                 if (stre[1] == 'x') // &#x... (hex code)
01460                                 {
01461                                         stre += 2;
01462 
01463                                         char_t ch = *stre;
01464 
01465                                         if (ch == ';') return stre;
01466 
01467                                         for (;;)
01468                                         {
01469                                                 if (static_cast<unsigned int>(ch - '0') <= 9)
01470                                                         ucsc = 16 * ucsc + (ch - '0');
01471                                                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>((ch | ' ') - 'a') <= 5)
01472                                                         ucsc = 16 * ucsc + ((ch | ' ') - 'a' + 10);
01473                                                 else if (ch == ';')
01474                                                         break;
01475                                                 else // cancel
01476                                                         return stre;
01477 
01478                                                 ch = *++stre;
01479                                         }
01480                                         
01481                                         ++stre;
01482                                 }
01483                                 else    // &#... (dec code)
01484                                 {
01485                                         char_t ch = *++stre;
01486 
01487                                         if (ch == ';') return stre;
01488 
01489                                         for (;;)
01490                                         {
01491                                                 if (static_cast<unsigned int>(ch - '0') <= 9)
01492                                                         ucsc = 10 * ucsc + (ch - '0');
01493                                                 else if (ch == ';')
01494                                                         break;
01495                                                 else // cancel
01496                                                         return stre;
01497 
01498                                                 ch = *++stre;
01499                                         }
01500                                         
01501                                         ++stre;
01502                                 }
01503 
01504                         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01505                                 s = reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(wchar_writer::any(reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(s), ucsc));
01506                         #else
01507                                 s = reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(utf8_writer::any(reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(s), ucsc));
01508                         #endif
01509                                         
01510                                 g.push(s, stre - s);
01511                                 return stre;
01512                         }
01513                         case 'a':       // &a
01514                         {
01515                                 ++stre;
01516 
01517                                 if (*stre == 'm') // &am
01518                                 {
01519                                         if (*++stre == 'p' && *++stre == ';') // &amp;
01520                                         {
01521                                                 *s++ = '&';
01522                                                 ++stre;
01523                                                         
01524                                                 g.push(s, stre - s);
01525                                                 return stre;
01526                                         }
01527                                 }
01528                                 else if (*stre == 'p') // &ap
01529                                 {
01530                                         if (*++stre == 'o' && *++stre == 's' && *++stre == ';') // &apos;
01531                                         {
01532                                                 *s++ = '\'';
01533                                                 ++stre;
01534 
01535                                                 g.push(s, stre - s);
01536                                                 return stre;
01537                                         }
01538                                 }
01539                                 break;
01540                         }
01541                         case 'g': // &g
01542                         {
01543                                 if (*++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &gt;
01544                                 {
01545                                         *s++ = '>';
01546                                         ++stre;
01547                                         
01548                                         g.push(s, stre - s);
01549                                         return stre;
01550                                 }
01551                                 break;
01552                         }
01553                         case 'l': // &l
01554                         {
01555                                 if (*++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &lt;
01556                                 {
01557                                         *s++ = '<';
01558                                         ++stre;
01559                                                 
01560                                         g.push(s, stre - s);
01561                                         return stre;
01562                                 }
01563                                 break;
01564                         }
01565                         case 'q': // &q
01566                         {
01567                                 if (*++stre == 'u' && *++stre == 'o' && *++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &quot;
01568                                 {
01569                                         *s++ = '"';
01570                                         ++stre;
01571                                         
01572                                         g.push(s, stre - s);
01573                                         return stre;
01574                                 }
01575                                 break;
01576                         }
01577                 }
01578                 
01579                 return stre;
01580         }
01581 
01582         // Utility macro for last character handling
01583         #define ENDSWITH(c, e) ((c) == (e) || ((c) == 0 && endch == (e)))
01584 
01585         char_t* strconv_comment(char_t* s, char_t endch)
01586         {
01587                 gap g;
01588                 
01589                 while (true)
01590                 {
01591                         while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_comment)) ++s;
01592                 
01593                         if (*s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
01594                         {
01595                                 *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
01596                                 
01597                                 if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
01598                         }
01599                         else if (s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && ENDSWITH(s[2], '>')) // comment ends here
01600                         {
01601                                 *g.flush(s) = 0;
01602                                 
01603                                 return s + (s[2] == '>' ? 3 : 2);
01604                         }
01605                         else if (*s == 0)
01606                         {
01607                                 return 0;
01608                         }
01609                         else ++s;
01610                 }
01611         }
01612 
01613         char_t* strconv_cdata(char_t* s, char_t endch)
01614         {
01615                 gap g;
01616                         
01617                 while (true)
01618                 {
01619                         while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_cdata)) ++s;
01620                         
01621                         if (*s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
01622                         {
01623                                 *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
01624                                 
01625                                 if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
01626                         }
01627                         else if (s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && ENDSWITH(s[2], '>')) // CDATA ends here
01628                         {
01629                                 *g.flush(s) = 0;
01630                                 
01631                                 return s + 1;
01632                         }
01633                         else if (*s == 0)
01634                         {
01635                                 return 0;
01636                         }
01637                         else ++s;
01638                 }
01639         }
01640         
01641         typedef char_t* (*strconv_pcdata_t)(char_t*);
01642                 
01643         template <typename opt_eol, typename opt_escape> struct strconv_pcdata_impl
01644         {
01645                 static char_t* parse(char_t* s)
01646                 {
01647                         gap g;
01648                         
01649                         while (true)
01650                         {
01651                                 while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_pcdata)) ++s;
01652                                         
01653                                 if (*s == '<') // PCDATA ends here
01654                                 {
01655                                         *g.flush(s) = 0;
01656                                         
01657                                         return s + 1;
01658                                 }
01659                                 else if (opt_eol::value && *s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
01660                                 {
01661                                         *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
01662                                         
01663                                         if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
01664                                 }
01665                                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
01666                                 {
01667                                         s = strconv_escape(s, g);
01668                                 }
01669                                 else if (*s == 0)
01670                                 {
01671                                         return s;
01672                                 }
01673                                 else ++s;
01674                         }
01675                 }
01676         };
01677         
01678         strconv_pcdata_t get_strconv_pcdata(unsigned int optmask)
01679         {
01680                 STATIC_ASSERT(parse_escapes == 0x10 && parse_eol == 0x20);
01681 
01682                 switch ((optmask >> 4) & 3) // get bitmask for flags (eol escapes)
01683                 {
01684                 case 0: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_false>::parse;
01685                 case 1: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_true>::parse;
01686                 case 2: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_false>::parse;
01687                 case 3: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_true>::parse;
01688                 default: return 0; // should not get here
01689                 }
01690         }
01691 
01692         typedef char_t* (*strconv_attribute_t)(char_t*, char_t);
01693         
01694         template <typename opt_escape> struct strconv_attribute_impl
01695         {
01696                 static char_t* parse_wnorm(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
01697                 {
01698                         gap g;
01699 
01700                         // trim leading whitespaces
01701                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
01702                         {
01703                                 char_t* str = s;
01704                                 
01705                                 do ++str;
01706                                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space));
01707                                 
01708                                 g.push(s, str - s);
01709                         }
01710 
01711                         while (true)
01712                         {
01713                                 while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_attr_ws | ct_space)) ++s;
01714                                 
01715                                 if (*s == end_quote)
01716                                 {
01717                                         char_t* str = g.flush(s);
01718                                         
01719                                         do *str-- = 0;
01720                                         while (IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space));
01721                                 
01722                                         return s + 1;
01723                                 }
01724                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
01725                                 {
01726                                         *s++ = ' ';
01727                 
01728                                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
01729                                         {
01730                                                 char_t* str = s + 1;
01731                                                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space)) ++str;
01732                                                 
01733                                                 g.push(s, str - s);
01734                                         }
01735                                 }
01736                                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
01737                                 {
01738                                         s = strconv_escape(s, g);
01739                                 }
01740                                 else if (!*s)
01741                                 {
01742                                         return 0;
01743                                 }
01744                                 else ++s;
01745                         }
01746                 }
01747 
01748                 static char_t* parse_wconv(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
01749                 {
01750                         gap g;
01751 
01752                         while (true)
01753                         {
01754                                 while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_attr_ws)) ++s;
01755                                 
01756                                 if (*s == end_quote)
01757                                 {
01758                                         *g.flush(s) = 0;
01759                                 
01760                                         return s + 1;
01761                                 }
01762                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
01763                                 {
01764                                         if (*s == '\r')
01765                                         {
01766                                                 *s++ = ' ';
01767                                 
01768                                                 if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
01769                                         }
01770                                         else *s++ = ' ';
01771                                 }
01772                                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
01773                                 {
01774                                         s = strconv_escape(s, g);
01775                                 }
01776                                 else if (!*s)
01777                                 {
01778                                         return 0;
01779                                 }
01780                                 else ++s;
01781                         }
01782                 }
01783 
01784                 static char_t* parse_eol(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
01785                 {
01786                         gap g;
01787 
01788                         while (true)
01789                         {
01790                                 while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_attr)) ++s;
01791                                 
01792                                 if (*s == end_quote)
01793                                 {
01794                                         *g.flush(s) = 0;
01795                                 
01796                                         return s + 1;
01797                                 }
01798                                 else if (*s == '\r')
01799                                 {
01800                                         *s++ = '\n';
01801                                         
01802                                         if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
01803                                 }
01804                                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
01805                                 {
01806                                         s = strconv_escape(s, g);
01807                                 }
01808                                 else if (!*s)
01809                                 {
01810                                         return 0;
01811                                 }
01812                                 else ++s;
01813                         }
01814                 }
01815 
01816                 static char_t* parse_simple(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
01817                 {
01818                         gap g;
01819 
01820                         while (true)
01821                         {
01822                                 while (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_parse_attr)) ++s;
01823                                 
01824                                 if (*s == end_quote)
01825                                 {
01826                                         *g.flush(s) = 0;
01827                                 
01828                                         return s + 1;
01829                                 }
01830                                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
01831                                 {
01832                                         s = strconv_escape(s, g);
01833                                 }
01834                                 else if (!*s)
01835                                 {
01836                                         return 0;
01837                                 }
01838                                 else ++s;
01839                         }
01840                 }
01841         };
01842 
01843         strconv_attribute_t get_strconv_attribute(unsigned int optmask)
01844         {
01845                 STATIC_ASSERT(parse_escapes == 0x10 && parse_eol == 0x20 && parse_wconv_attribute == 0x40 && parse_wnorm_attribute == 0x80);
01846                 
01847                 switch ((optmask >> 4) & 15) // get bitmask for flags (wconv wnorm eol escapes)
01848                 {
01849                 case 0:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_simple;
01850                 case 1:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_simple;
01851                 case 2:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_eol;
01852                 case 3:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_eol;
01853                 case 4:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wconv;
01854                 case 5:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wconv;
01855                 case 6:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wconv;
01856                 case 7:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wconv;
01857                 case 8:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
01858                 case 9:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
01859                 case 10: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
01860                 case 11: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
01861                 case 12: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
01862                 case 13: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
01863                 case 14: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
01864                 case 15: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
01865                 default: return 0; // should not get here
01866                 }
01867         }
01868 
01869         inline xml_parse_result make_parse_result(xml_parse_status status, ptrdiff_t offset = 0)
01870         {
01871                 xml_parse_result result;
01872                 result.status = status;
01873                 result.offset = offset;
01874 
01875                 return result;
01876         }
01877 
01878         struct xml_parser
01879         {
01880                 xml_allocator alloc;
01881                 char_t* error_offset;
01882                 jmp_buf error_handler;
01883                 
01884                 // Parser utilities.
01885                 #define SKIPWS()                        { while (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space)) ++s; }
01886                 #define OPTSET(OPT)                     ( optmsk & OPT )
01887                 #define PUSHNODE(TYPE)          { cursor = append_node(cursor, alloc, TYPE); if (!cursor) THROW_ERROR(status_out_of_memory, s); }
01888                 #define POPNODE()                       { cursor = cursor->parent; }
01889                 #define SCANFOR(X)                      { while (*s != 0 && !(X)) ++s; }
01890                 #define SCANWHILE(X)            { while ((X)) ++s; }
01891                 #define ENDSEG()                        { ch = *s; *s = 0; ++s; }
01892                 #define THROW_ERROR(err, m)     error_offset = m, longjmp(error_handler, err)
01893                 #define CHECK_ERROR(err, m)     { if (*s == 0) THROW_ERROR(err, m); }
01894                 
01895                 xml_parser(const xml_allocator& alloc): alloc(alloc), error_offset(0)
01896                 {
01897                 }
01898 
01899                 // DOCTYPE consists of nested sections of the following possible types:
01900                 // <!-- ... -->, <? ... ?>, "...", '...'
01901                 // <![...]]>
01902                 // <!...>
01903                 // First group can not contain nested groups
01904                 // Second group can contain nested groups of the same type
01905                 // Third group can contain all other groups
01906                 char_t* parse_doctype_primitive(char_t* s)
01907                 {
01908                         if (*s == '"' || *s == '\'')
01909                         {
01910                                 // quoted string
01911                                 char_t ch = *s++;
01912                                 SCANFOR(*s == ch);
01913                                 if (!*s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
01914 
01915                                 s++;
01916                         }
01917                         else if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '?')
01918                         {
01919                                 // <? ... ?>
01920                                 s += 2;
01921                                 SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && s[1] == '>'); // no need for ENDSWITH because ?> can't terminate proper doctype
01922                                 if (!*s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
01923 
01924                                 s += 2;
01925                         }
01926                         else if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '-' && s[3] == '-')
01927                         {
01928                                 s += 4;
01929                                 SCANFOR(s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && s[2] == '>'); // no need for ENDSWITH because --> can't terminate proper doctype
01930                                 if (!*s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
01931 
01932                                 s += 4;
01933                         }
01934                         else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
01935 
01936                         return s;
01937                 }
01938 
01939                 char_t* parse_doctype_ignore(char_t* s)
01940                 {
01941                         assert(s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '[');
01942                         s++;
01943 
01944                         while (*s)
01945                         {
01946                                 if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '[')
01947                                 {
01948                                         // nested ignore section
01949                                         s = parse_doctype_ignore(s);
01950                                 }
01951                                 else if (s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && s[2] == '>')
01952                                 {
01953                                         // ignore section end
01954                                         s += 3;
01955 
01956                                         return s;
01957                                 }
01958                                 else s++;
01959                         }
01960 
01961                         THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
01962 
01963                         return s;
01964                 }
01965 
01966                 char_t* parse_doctype_group(char_t* s, char_t endch, bool toplevel)
01967                 {
01968                         assert(s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!');
01969                         s++;
01970 
01971                         while (*s)
01972                         {
01973                                 if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] != '-')
01974                                 {
01975                                         if (s[2] == '[')
01976                                         {
01977                                                 // ignore
01978                                                 s = parse_doctype_ignore(s);
01979                                         }
01980                                         else
01981                                         {
01982                                                 // some control group
01983                                                 s = parse_doctype_group(s, endch, false);
01984                                         }
01985                                 }
01986                                 else if (s[0] == '<' || s[0] == '"' || s[0] == '\'')
01987                                 {
01988                                         // unknown tag (forbidden), or some primitive group
01989                                         s = parse_doctype_primitive(s);
01990                                 }
01991                                 else if (*s == '>')
01992                                 {
01993                                         s++;
01994 
01995                                         return s;
01996                                 }
01997                                 else s++;
01998                         }
01999 
02000                         if (!toplevel || endch != '>') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02001 
02002                         return s;
02003                 }
02004 
02005                 char_t* parse_exclamation(char_t* s, xml_node_struct* cursor, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02006                 {
02007                         // parse node contents, starting with exclamation mark
02008                         ++s;
02009 
02010                         if (*s == '-') // '<!-...'
02011                         {
02012                                 ++s;
02013 
02014                                 if (*s == '-') // '<!--...'
02015                                 {
02016                                         ++s;
02017 
02018                                         if (OPTSET(parse_comments))
02019                                         {
02020                                                 PUSHNODE(node_comment); // Append a new node on the tree.
02021                                                 cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
