02022                                         }
02023 
02024                                         if (OPTSET(parse_eol) && OPTSET(parse_comments))
02025                                         {
02026                                                 s = strconv_comment(s, endch);
02027 
02028                                                 if (!s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, cursor->value);
02029                                         }
02030                                         else
02031                                         {
02032                                                 // Scan for terminating '-->'.
02033                                                 SCANFOR(s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02034                                                 CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02035 
02036                                                 if (OPTSET(parse_comments))
02037                                                         *s = 0; // Zero-terminate this segment at the first terminating '-'.
02038 
02039                                                 s += (s[2] == '>' ? 3 : 2); // Step over the '\0->'.
02040                                         }
02041                                 }
02042                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02043                         }
02044                         else if (*s == '[')
02045                         {
02046                                 // '<![CDATA[...'
02047                                 if (*++s=='C' && *++s=='D' && *++s=='A' && *++s=='T' && *++s=='A' && *++s == '[')
02048                                 {
02049                                         ++s;
02050 
02051                                         if (OPTSET(parse_cdata))
02052                                         {
02053                                                 PUSHNODE(node_cdata); // Append a new node on the tree.
02054                                                 cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
02055 
02056                                                 if (OPTSET(parse_eol))
02057                                                 {
02058                                                         s = strconv_cdata(s, endch);
02059 
02060                                                         if (!s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, cursor->value);
02061                                                 }
02062                                                 else
02063                                                 {
02064                                                         // Scan for terminating ']]>'.
02065                                                         SCANFOR(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02066                                                         CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02067 
02068                                                         *s++ = 0; // Zero-terminate this segment.
02069                                                 }
02070                                         }
02071                                         else // Flagged for discard, but we still have to scan for the terminator.
02072                                         {
02073                                                 // Scan for terminating ']]>'.
02074                                                 SCANFOR(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02075                                                 CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02076 
02077                                                 ++s;
02078                                         }
02079 
02080                                         s += (s[1] == '>' ? 2 : 1); // Step over the last ']>'.
02081                                 }
02082                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02083                         }
02084                         else if (s[0] == 'D' && s[1] == 'O' && s[2] == 'C' && s[3] == 'T' && s[4] == 'Y' && s[5] == 'P' && ENDSWITH(s[6], 'E'))
02085                         {
02086                                 s -= 2;
02087 
02088                 if (cursor->parent) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02089 
02090                 char_t* mark = s + 9;
02091 
02092                                 s = parse_doctype_group(s, endch, true);
02093 
02094                 if (OPTSET(parse_doctype))
02095                 {
02096                     while (IS_CHARTYPE(*mark, ct_space)) ++mark;
02097 
02098                     PUSHNODE(node_doctype);
02099 
02100                     cursor->value = mark;
02101 
02102                     assert((s[0] == 0 && endch == '>') || s[-1] == '>');
02103                     s[*s == 0 ? 0 : -1] = 0;
02104 
02105                     POPNODE();
02106                 }
02107                         }
02108                         else if (*s == 0 && endch == '-') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02109                         else if (*s == 0 && endch == '[') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02110                         else THROW_ERROR(status_unrecognized_tag, s);
02111 
02112                         return s;
02113                 }
02114 
02115                 char_t* parse_question(char_t* s, xml_node_struct*& ref_cursor, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02116                 {
02117                         // load into registers
02118                         xml_node_struct* cursor = ref_cursor;
02119                         char_t ch = 0;
02120 
02121                         // parse node contents, starting with question mark
02122                         ++s;
02123 
02124                         // read PI target
02125                         char_t* target = s;
02126 
02127                         if (!IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02128 
02129                         SCANWHILE(IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol));
02130                         CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02131 
02132                         // determine node type; stricmp / strcasecmp is not portable
02133                         bool declaration = (target[0] | ' ') == 'x' && (target[1] | ' ') == 'm' && (target[2] | ' ') == 'l' && target + 3 == s;
02134 
02135                         if (declaration ? OPTSET(parse_declaration) : OPTSET(parse_pi))
02136                         {
02137                                 if (declaration)
02138                                 {
02139                                         // disallow non top-level declarations
02140                                         if (cursor->parent) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02141 
02142                                         PUSHNODE(node_declaration);
02143                                 }
02144                                 else
02145                                 {
02146                                         PUSHNODE(node_pi);
02147                                 }
02148 
02149                                 cursor->name = target;
02150 
02151                                 ENDSEG();
02152 
02153                                 // parse value/attributes
02154                                 if (ch == '?')
02155                                 {
02156                                         // empty node
02157                                         if (!ENDSWITH(*s, '>')) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02158                                         s += (*s == '>');
02159 
02160                                         POPNODE();
02161                                 }
02162                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02163                                 {
02164                                         SKIPWS();
02165 
02166                                         // scan for tag end
02167                                         char_t* value = s;
02168 
02169                                         SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && ENDSWITH(s[1], '>'));
02170                                         CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02171 
02172                                         if (declaration)
02173                                         {
02174                                                 // replace ending ? with / so that 'element' terminates properly
02175                                                 *s = '/';
02176 
02177                                                 // we exit from this function with cursor at node_declaration, which is a signal to parse() to go to LOC_ATTRIBUTES
02178                                                 s = value;
02179                                         }
02180                                         else
02181                                         {
02182                                                 // store value and step over >
02183                                                 cursor->value = value;
02184                                                 POPNODE();
02185 
02186                                                 ENDSEG();
02187 
02188                                                 s += (*s == '>');
02189                                         }
02190                                 }
02191                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02192                         }
02193                         else
02194                         {
02195                                 // scan for tag end
02196                                 SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && ENDSWITH(s[1], '>'));
02197                                 CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02198 
02199                                 s += (s[1] == '>' ? 2 : 1);
02200                         }
02201 
02202                         // store from registers
02203                         ref_cursor = cursor;
02204 
02205                         return s;
02206                 }
02207 
02208                 void parse(char_t* s, xml_node_struct* xmldoc, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02209                 {
02210                         strconv_attribute_t strconv_attribute = get_strconv_attribute(optmsk);
02211                         strconv_pcdata_t strconv_pcdata = get_strconv_pcdata(optmsk);
02212                         
02213                         char_t ch = 0;
02214                         xml_node_struct* cursor = xmldoc;
02215                         char_t* mark = s;
02216 
02217                         while (*s != 0)
02218                         {
02219                                 if (*s == '<')
02220                                 {
02221                                         ++s;
02222 
02223                                 LOC_TAG:
02224                                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) // '<#...'
02225                                         {
02226                                                 PUSHNODE(node_element); // Append a new node to the tree.
02227 
02228                                                 cursor->name = s;
02229 
02230                                                 SCANWHILE(IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol)); // Scan for a terminator.
02231                                                 ENDSEG(); // Save char in 'ch', terminate & step over.
02232 
02233                                                 if (ch == '>')
02234                                                 {
02235                                                         // end of tag
02236                                                 }
02237                                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02238                                                 {
02239                                                 LOC_ATTRIBUTES:
02240                                                     while (true)
02241                                                     {
02242                                                                 SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02243                                                 
02244                                                                 if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) // <... #...
02245                                                                 {
02246                                                                         xml_attribute_struct* a = append_attribute_ll(cursor, alloc); // Make space for this attribute.
02247                                                                         if (!a) THROW_ERROR(status_out_of_memory, s);
02248 
02249                                                                         a->name = s; // Save the offset.
02250 
02251                                                                         SCANWHILE(IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol)); // Scan for a terminator.
02252                                                                         CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s); //$ redundant, left for performance
02253 
02254                                                                         ENDSEG(); // Save char in 'ch', terminate & step over.
02255                                                                         CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s); //$ redundant, left for performance
02256 
02257                                                                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02258                                                                         {
02259                                                                                 SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02260                                                                                 CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s); //$ redundant, left for performance
02261 
02262                                                                                 ch = *s;
02263                                                                                 ++s;
02264                                                                         }
02265                                                                         
02266                                                                         if (ch == '=') // '<... #=...'
02267                                                                         {
02268                                                                                 SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02269 
02270                                                                                 if (*s == '"' || *s == '\'') // '<... #="...'
02271                                                                                 {
02272                                                                                         ch = *s; // Save quote char to avoid breaking on "''" -or- '""'.
02273                                                                                         ++s; // Step over the quote.
02274                                                                                         a->value = s; // Save the offset.
02275 
02276                                                                                         s = strconv_attribute(s, ch);
02277                                                                                 
02278                                                                                         if (!s) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, a->value);
02279 
02280                                                                                         // After this line the loop continues from the start;
02281                                                                                         // Whitespaces, / and > are ok, symbols and EOF are wrong,
02282                                                                                         // everything else will be detected
02283                                                                                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02284                                                                                 }
02285                                                                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02286                                                                         }
02287                                                                         else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02288                                                                 }
02289                                                                 else if (*s == '/')
02290                                                                 {
02291                                                                         ++s;
02292                                                                         
02293                                                                         if (*s == '>')
02294                                                                         {
02295                                                                                 POPNODE();
02296                                                                                 s++;
02297                                                                                 break;
02298                                                                         }
02299                                                                         else if (*s == 0 && endch == '>')
02300                                                                         {
02301                                                                                 POPNODE();
02302                                                                                 break;
02303                                                                         }
02304                                                                         else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02305                                                                 }
02306                                                                 else if (*s == '>')
02307                                                                 {
02308                                                                         ++s;
02309 
02310                                                                         break;
02311                                                                 }
02312                                                                 else if (*s == 0 && endch == '>')
02313                                                                 {
02314                                                                         break;
02315                                                                 }
02316                                                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02317                                                         }
02318 
02319                                                         // !!!
02320                                                 }
02321                                                 else if (ch == '/') // '<#.../'
02322                                                 {
02323                                                         if (!ENDSWITH(*s, '>')) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02324 
02325                                                         POPNODE(); // Pop.
02326 
02327                                                         s += (*s == '>');
02328                                                 }
02329                                                 else if (ch == 0)
02330                                                 {
02331                                                         // we stepped over null terminator, backtrack & handle closing tag
02332                                                         --s;
02333                                                         
02334                                                         if (endch != '>') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02335                                                 }
02336                                                 else THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02337                                         }
02338                                         else if (*s == '/')
02339                                         {
02340                                                 ++s;
02341 
02342                                                 char_t* name = cursor->name;
02343                                                 if (!name) THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02344                                                 
02345                                                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol))
02346                                                 {
02347                                                         if (*s++ != *name++) THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02348                                                 }
02349 
02350                                                 if (*name)
02351                                                 {
02352                                                         if (*s == 0 && name[0] == endch && name[1] == 0) THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02353                                                         else THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02354                                                 }
02355                                                         
02356                                                 POPNODE(); // Pop.
02357 
02358                                                 SKIPWS();
02359 
02360                                                 if (*s == 0)
02361                                                 {
02362                                                         if (endch != '>') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02363                                                 }
02364                                                 else
02365                                                 {
02366                                                         if (*s != '>') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02367                                                         ++s;
02368                                                 }
02369                                         }
02370                                         else if (*s == '?') // '<?...'
02371                                         {
02372                                                 s = parse_question(s, cursor, optmsk, endch);
02373 
02374                                                 assert(cursor);
02375                                                 if ((cursor->header & xml_memory_page_type_mask) + 1 == node_declaration) goto LOC_ATTRIBUTES;
02376                                         }
02377                                         else if (*s == '!') // '<!...'
02378                                         {
02379                                                 s = parse_exclamation(s, cursor, optmsk, endch);
02380                                         }
02381                                         else if (*s == 0 && endch == '?') THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02382                                         else THROW_ERROR(status_unrecognized_tag, s);
02383                                 }
02384                                 else
02385                                 {
02386                                         mark = s; // Save this offset while searching for a terminator.
02387 
02388                                         SKIPWS(); // Eat whitespace if no genuine PCDATA here.
02389 
02390                                         if ((!OPTSET(parse_ws_pcdata) || mark == s) && (*s == '<' || !*s))
02391                                         {
02392                                                 continue;
02393                                         }
02394 
02395                                         s = mark;
02396                                                         
02397                                         if (cursor->parent)
02398                                         {
02399                                                 PUSHNODE(node_pcdata); // Append a new node on the tree.
02400                                                 cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
02401 
02402                                                 s = strconv_pcdata(s);
02403                                                                 
02404                                                 POPNODE(); // Pop since this is a standalone.
02405                                                 
02406                                                 if (!*s) break;
02407                                         }
02408                                         else
02409                                         {
02410                                                 SCANFOR(*s == '<'); // '...<'
02411                                                 if (!*s) break;
02412                                                 
02413                                                 ++s;
02414                                         }
02415 
02416                                         // We're after '<'
02417                                         goto LOC_TAG;
02418                                 }
02419                         }
02420 
02421                         // check that last tag is closed
02422                         if (cursor != xmldoc) THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02423                 }
02424 
02425                 static xml_parse_result parse(char_t* buffer, size_t length, xml_node_struct* root, unsigned int optmsk)
02426                 {
02427                         xml_document_struct* xmldoc = static_cast<xml_document_struct*>(root);
02428 
02429                         // store buffer for offset_debug
02430                         xmldoc->buffer = buffer;
02431 
02432                         // early-out for empty documents
02433                         if (length == 0) return make_parse_result(status_ok);
02434 
02435                         // create parser on stack
02436                         xml_parser parser(*xmldoc);
02437 
02438                         // save last character and make buffer zero-terminated (speeds up parsing)
02439                         char_t endch = buffer[length - 1];
02440                         buffer[length - 1] = 0;
02441                         
02442                         // perform actual parsing
02443                         int error = setjmp(parser.error_handler);
02444 
02445                         if (error == 0)
02446                         {
02447                                 parser.parse(buffer, xmldoc, optmsk, endch);
02448                         }
02449 
02450                         xml_parse_result result = make_parse_result(static_cast<xml_parse_status>(error), parser.error_offset ? parser.error_offset - buffer : 0);
02451                         assert(result.offset >= 0 && static_cast<size_t>(result.offset) <= length);
02452 
02453                         // update allocator state
02454                         *static_cast<xml_allocator*>(xmldoc) = parser.alloc;
02455 
02456                         // since we removed last character, we have to handle the only possible false positive
02457                         if (result && endch == '<')
02458                         {
02459                                 // there's no possible well-formed document with < at the end
02460                                 return make_parse_result(status_unrecognized_tag, length);
02461                         }
02462 
02463                         return result;
02464                 }
02465         };
02466 
02467         // Output facilities
02468         xml_encoding get_write_native_encoding()
02469         {
02470         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
02471                 return get_wchar_encoding();
02472         #else
02473                 return encoding_utf8;
02474         #endif
02475         }
02476 
02477         xml_encoding get_write_encoding(xml_encoding encoding)
02478         {
02479                 // replace wchar encoding with utf implementation
02480                 if (encoding == encoding_wchar) return get_wchar_encoding();
02481 
02482                 // replace utf16 encoding with utf16 with specific endianness
02483                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
02484 
02485                 // replace utf32 encoding with utf32 with specific endianness
02486                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
02487 
02488                 // only do autodetection if no explicit encoding is requested
02489                 if (encoding != encoding_auto) return encoding;
02490 
02491                 // assume utf8 encoding
02492                 return encoding_utf8;
02493         }
02494 
02495 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
02496         size_t get_valid_length(const char_t* data, size_t length)
02497         {
02498                 assert(length > 0);
02499 
02500                 // discard last character if it's the lead of a surrogate pair 
02501                 return (sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 && (unsigned)(static_cast<uint16_t>(data[length - 1]) - 0xD800) < 0x400) ? length - 1 : length;
02502         }
02503 
02504         size_t convert_buffer(char* result, const char_t* data, size_t length, xml_encoding encoding)
02505         {
02506                 // only endian-swapping is required
02507                 if (need_endian_swap_utf(encoding, get_wchar_encoding()))
02508                 {
02509                         convert_wchar_endian_swap(reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(result), data, length);
02510 
02511                         return length * sizeof(char_t);
02512                 }
02513         
02514                 // convert to utf8
02515                 if (encoding == encoding_utf8)
02516                 {
02517                         uint8_t* dest = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(result);
02518 
02519                         uint8_t* end = sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 ?
02520                                 utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_utf16_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint16_t*>(data), length, dest) :
02521                                 utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_utf32_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(data), length, dest);
02522 
02523                         return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest);
02524                 }
02525 
02526                 // convert to utf16
02527                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
02528                 {
02529                         uint16_t* dest = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(result);
02530 
02531                         // convert to native utf16
02532                         uint16_t* end = utf_decoder<utf16_writer>::decode_utf32_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(data), length, dest);
02533 
02534                         // swap if necessary
02535                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
02536 
02537                         if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
02538 
02539                         return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint16_t);
02540                 }
02541 
02542                 // convert to utf32
02543                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
02544                 {
02545                         uint32_t* dest = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(result);
02546 
02547                         // convert to native utf32
02548                         uint32_t* end = utf_decoder<utf32_writer>::decode_utf16_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint16_t*>(data), length, dest);
02549 
02550                         // swap if necessary
02551                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
02552 
02553                         if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
02554 
02555                         return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint32_t);
02556                 }
02557 
02558                 assert(!"Invalid encoding");
02559                 return 0;
02560         }
02561 #else
02562         size_t get_valid_length(const char_t* data, size_t length)
02563         {
02564                 assert(length > 4);
02565 
02566                 for (size_t i = 1; i <= 4; ++i)
02567                 {
02568                         uint8_t ch = static_cast<uint8_t>(data[length - i]);
02569 
02570                         // either a standalone character or a leading one
02571                         if ((ch & 0xc0) != 0x80) return length - i;
02572                 }
02573 
02574                 // there are four non-leading characters at the end, sequence tail is broken so might as well process the whole chunk
02575                 return length;
02576         }
02577 
02578         size_t convert_buffer(char* result, const char_t* data, size_t length, xml_encoding encoding)
02579         {
02580                 if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
02581                 {
02582                         uint16_t* dest = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(result);
02583 
02584                         // convert to native utf16
02585                         uint16_t* end = utf_decoder<utf16_writer>::decode_utf8_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(data), length, dest);
02586 
02587                         // swap if necessary
02588                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
02589 
02590                         if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
02591 
02592                         return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint16_t);
02593                 }
02594 
02595                 if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
02596                 {
02597                         uint32_t* dest = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(result);
02598 
02599                         // convert to native utf32
02600                         uint32_t* end = utf_decoder<utf32_writer>::decode_utf8_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(data), length, dest);
02601 
02602                         // swap if necessary
02603                         xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
02604 
02605                         if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
02606 
02607                         return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint32_t);
02608                 }
02609 
02610                 assert(!"Invalid encoding");
02611                 return 0;
02612         }
02613 #endif
02614 
02615         class xml_buffered_writer
02616         {
02617                 xml_buffered_writer(const xml_buffered_writer&);
02618                 xml_buffered_writer& operator=(const xml_buffered_writer&);
02619 
02620         public:
02621                 xml_buffered_writer(xml_writer& writer, xml_encoding user_encoding): writer(writer), bufsize(0), encoding(get_write_encoding(user_encoding))
02622                 {
02623                 }
02624 
02625                 ~xml_buffered_writer()
02626                 {
02627                         flush();
02628                 }
02629 
02630                 void flush()
02631                 {
02632                         flush(buffer, bufsize);
02633                         bufsize = 0;
02634                 }
02635 
02636                 void flush(const char_t* data, size_t size)
02637                 {
02638                         if (size == 0) return;
02639 
02640                         // fast path, just write data
02641                         if (encoding == get_write_native_encoding())
02642                                 writer.write(data, size * sizeof(char_t));
02643                         else
02644                         {
02645                                 // convert chunk
02646                                 size_t result = convert_buffer(scratch, data, size, encoding);
02647                                 assert(result <= sizeof(scratch));
02648 
02649                                 // write data
02650                                 writer.write(scratch, result);
02651                         }
02652                 }
02653 
02654                 void write(const char_t* data, size_t length)
02655                 {
02656                         if (bufsize + length > bufcapacity)
02657                         {
02658                                 // flush the remaining buffer contents
02659                                 flush();
02660 
02661                                 // handle large chunks
02662                                 if (length > bufcapacity)
02663                                 {
02664                                         if (encoding == get_write_native_encoding())
02665                                         {
02666                                                 // fast path, can just write data chunk
02667                                                 writer.write(data, length * sizeof(char_t));
02668                                                 return;
02669                                         }
02670 
02671                                         // need to convert in suitable chunks
02672                                         while (length > bufcapacity)
02673                                         {
02674                                                 // get chunk size by selecting such number of characters that are guaranteed to fit into scratch buffer
02675                                                 // and form a complete codepoint sequence (i.e. discard start of last codepoint if necessary)
02676                                                 size_t chunk_size = get_valid_length(data, bufcapacity);
02677 
02678                                                 // convert chunk and write
02679                                                 flush(data, chunk_size);
02680 
02681                                                 // iterate
02682                                                 data += chunk_size;
02683                                                 length -= chunk_size;
02684                                         }
02685 
02686                                         // small tail is copied below
02687                                         bufsize = 0;
02688                                 }
02689                         }
02690 
02691                         memcpy(buffer + bufsize, data, length * sizeof(char_t));
02692                         bufsize += length;
02693                 }
02694 
02695                 void write(const char_t* data)
02696                 {
02697                         write(data, strlength(data));
02698                 }
02699 
02700                 void write(char_t d0)
02701                 {
02702                         if (bufsize + 1 > bufcapacity) flush();
02703 
02704                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02705                         bufsize += 1;
02706                 }
02707 
02708                 void write(char_t d0, char_t d1)
02709                 {
02710                         if (bufsize + 2 > bufcapacity) flush();
02711 
02712                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02713                         buffer[bufsize + 1] = d1;
02714                         bufsize += 2;
02715                 }
02716 
02717                 void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2)
02718                 {
02719                         if (bufsize + 3 > bufcapacity) flush();
02720 
02721                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02722                         buffer[bufsize + 1] = d1;
02723                         buffer[bufsize + 2] = d2;
02724                         bufsize += 3;
02725                 }
02726 
02727                 void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3)
02728                 {
02729                         if (bufsize + 4 > bufcapacity) flush();
02730 
02731                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02732                         buffer[bufsize + 1] = d1;
02733                         buffer[bufsize + 2] = d2;
02734                         buffer[bufsize + 3] = d3;
02735                         bufsize += 4;
02736                 }
02737 
02738                 void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3, char_t d4)
02739                 {
02740                         if (bufsize + 5 > bufcapacity) flush();
02741 
02742                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02743                         buffer[bufsize + 1] = d1;
02744                         buffer[bufsize + 2] = d2;
02745                         buffer[bufsize + 3] = d3;
02746                         buffer[bufsize + 4] = d4;
02747                         bufsize += 5;
02748                 }
02749 
02750                 void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3, char_t d4, char_t d5)
02751                 {
02752                         if (bufsize + 6 > bufcapacity) flush();
02753 
02754                         buffer[bufsize + 0] = d0;
02755                         buffer[bufsize + 1] = d1;
02756                         buffer[bufsize + 2] = d2;
02757                         buffer[bufsize + 3] = d3;
02758                         buffer[bufsize + 4] = d4;
02759                         buffer[bufsize + 5] = d5;
02760                         bufsize += 6;
02761                 }
02762 
02763                 // utf8 maximum expansion: x4 (-> utf32)
02764                 // utf16 maximum expansion: x2 (-> utf32)
02765                 // utf32 maximum expansion: x1
02766                 enum { bufcapacity = 2048 };
02767 
02768                 char_t buffer[bufcapacity];
02769                 char scratch[4 * bufcapacity];
02770 
02771                 xml_writer& writer;
02772                 size_t bufsize;
02773                 xml_encoding encoding;
02774         };
02775 
02776         void write_bom(xml_writer& writer, xml_encoding encoding)
02777         {
02778                 switch (encoding)
02779                 {
02780                 case encoding_utf8:
02781                         writer.write("\xef\xbb\xbf", 3);
02782                         break;
02783 
02784                 case encoding_utf16_be:
02785                         writer.write("\xfe\xff", 2);
02786                         break;
02787 
02788                 case encoding_utf16_le:
02789                         writer.write("\xff\xfe", 2);
02790                         break;
02791 
02792                 case encoding_utf32_be:
02793                         writer.write("\x00\x00\xfe\xff", 4);
02794                         break;
02795 
02796                 case encoding_utf32_le:
02797                         writer.write("\xff\xfe\x00\x00", 4);
02798                         break;
02799 
02800                 default:
02801                         assert(!"Invalid encoding");
02802                 }
02803         }
02804 
02805         void text_output_escaped(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s, chartypex_t type)
02806         {
02807                 while (*s)
02808                 {
02809                         const char_t* prev = s;
02810                         
02811                         // While *s is a usual symbol
02812                         while (!IS_CHARTYPEX(*s, type)) ++s;
02813                 
02814                         writer.write(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
02815 
02816                         switch (*s)
02817                         {
02818                                 case 0: break;
02819                                 case '&':
02820                                         writer.write('&', 'a', 'm', 'p', ';');
02821                                         ++s;
02822                                         break;
02823                                 case '<':
02824                                         writer.write('&', 'l', 't', ';');
02825                                         ++s;
02826                                         break;
02827                                 case '>':
02828                                         writer.write('&', 'g', 't', ';');
02829                                         ++s;
02830                                         break;
02831                                 case '"':
02832                                         writer.write('&', 'q', 'u', 'o', 't', ';');
02833                                         ++s;
02834                                         break;
02835                                 default: // s is not a usual symbol
02836                                 {
02837                                         unsigned int ch = static_cast<unsigned int>(*s++);
02838                                         assert(ch < 32);
02839 
02840                                         writer.write('&', '#', static_cast<char_t>((ch / 10) + '0'), static_cast<char_t>((ch % 10) + '0'), ';');
02841                                 }
02842                         }
02843                 }
02844         }
02845 
02846         void text_output_cdata(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s)
02847         {
02848                 do
02849                 {
02850                         writer.write('<', '!', '[', 'C', 'D');
02851                         writer.write('A', 'T', 'A', '[');
02852 
02853                         const char_t* prev = s;
02854 
02855                         // look for ]]> sequence - we can't output it as is since it terminates CDATA
02856                         while (*s && !(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && s[2] == '>')) ++s;
02857 
02858                         // skip ]] if we stopped at ]]>, > will go to the next CDATA section
02859                         if (*s) s += 2;
02860 
02861                         writer.write(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
02862 
02863                         writer.write(']', ']', '>');
02864                 }
02865                 while (*s);
02866         }
02867 
02868         void node_output_attributes(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const xml_node& node)
02869         {
02870                 const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
02871 
02872                 for (xml_attribute a = node.first_attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
02873                 {
02874                         writer.write(' ');
02875                         writer.write(a.name()[0] ? a.name() : default_name);
02876                         writer.write('=', '"');
02877 
02878                         text_output_escaped(writer, a.value(), ctx_special_attr);
02879 
02880                         writer.write('"');
02881                 }
02882         }
02883 
02884         void node_output(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const xml_node& node, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, unsigned int depth)
02885         {
02886                 const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
02887 
02888                 if ((flags & format_indent) != 0 && (flags & format_raw) == 0)
02889                         for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i) writer.write(indent);
02890 
02891                 switch (node.type())
02892                 {
02893                 case node_document:
02894                 {
02895                         for (xml_node n = node.first_child(); n; n = n.next_sibling())
02896                                 node_output(writer, n, indent, flags, depth);
02897                         break;
02898                 }
02899                         
02900                 case node_element:
02901                 {
02902                         const char_t* name = node.name()[0] ? node.name() : default_name;
02903 
02904                         writer.write('<');
02905                         writer.write(name);
02906 
02907                         node_output_attributes(writer, node);
02908 
02909                         if (flags & format_raw)
02910                         {
02911                                 if (!node.first_child())
02912                                         writer.write(' ', '/', '>');
02913                                 else
02914                                 {
02915                                         writer.write('>');
02916 
02917                                         for (xml_node n = node.first_child(); n; n = n.next_sibling())
02918                                                 node_output(writer, n, indent, flags, depth + 1);
02919 
02920                                         writer.write('<', '/');
02921                                         writer.write(name);
02922                                         writer.write('>');
02923                                 }
02924                         }
02925                         else if (!node.first_child())
02926                                 writer.write(' ', '/', '>', '\n');
02927                         else if (node.first_child() == node.last_child() && (node.first_child().type() == node_pcdata || node.first_child().type() == node_cdata))
02928                         {
02929                                 writer.write('>');
02930 
02931                 if (node.first_child().type() == node_pcdata)
02932                     text_output_escaped(writer, node.first_child().value(), ctx_special_pcdata);
02933                 else
02934                     text_output_cdata(writer, node.first_child().value());
02935 
02936                                 writer.write('<', '/');
02937                                 writer.write(name);
02938                                 writer.write('>', '\n');
02939                         }
02940                         else
02941                         {
02942                                 writer.write('>', '\n');
02943                                 
02944                                 for (xml_node n = node.first_child(); n; n = n.next_sibling())
02945                                         node_output(writer, n, indent, flags, depth + 1);
02946 
02947                                 if ((flags & format_indent) != 0 && (flags & format_raw) == 0)
02948                                         for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i) writer.write(indent);
02949                                 
02950                                 writer.write('<', '/');
02951                                 writer.write(name);
02952                                 writer.write('>', '\n');
02953                         }
02954 
02955                         break;
02956                 }
02957                 
02958                 case node_pcdata:
02959                         text_output_escaped(writer, node.value(), ctx_special_pcdata);
02960                         if ((flags & format_raw) == 0) writer.write('\n');
02961                         break;
02962 
02963                 case node_cdata:
02964                         text_output_cdata(writer, node.value());
02965                         if ((flags & format_raw) == 0) writer.write('\n');
02966                         break;
02967 
02968                 case node_comment:
02969                         writer.write('<', '!', '-', '-');
02970                         writer.write(node.value());
02971                         writer.write('-', '-', '>');
02972                         if ((flags & format_raw) == 0) writer.write('\n');
02973                         break;
02974 
02975                 case node_pi:
02976                 case node_declaration:
02977                         writer.write('<', '?');
02978                         writer.write(node.name()[0] ? node.name() : default_name);
02979 
02980                         if (node.type() == node_declaration)
02981                         {
02982                                 node_output_attributes(writer, node);
02983                         }
02984                         else if (node.value()[0])
02985                         {
02986                                 writer.write(' ');
02987                                 writer.write(node.value());
02988                         }
02989 
02990                         writer.write('?', '>');
02991                         if ((flags & format_raw) == 0) writer.write('\n');
02992                         break;
02993 
02994                 case node_doctype:
02995                         writer.write('<', '!', 'D', 'O', 'C');
02996                         writer.write('T', 'Y', 'P', 'E');
02997 
02998             if (node.value()[0])
02999             {
03000                 writer.write(' ');
03001                 writer.write(node.value());
03002             }
03003 
03004             writer.write('>');
03005                         if ((flags & format_raw) == 0) writer.write('\n');
03006                         break;
03007 
03008                 default:
03009                         assert(!"Invalid node type");
03010                 }
03011         }
03012 
03013         inline bool has_declaration(const xml_node& node)
03014         {
03015                 for (xml_node child = node.first_child(); child; child = child.next_sibling())
03016                 {
03017                         xml_node_type type = child.type();
03018 
03019                         if (type == node_declaration) return true;
03020                         if (type == node_element) return false;
03021                 }
03022 
03023                 return false;
03024         }
03025 
03026         inline bool allow_insert_child(xml_node_type parent, xml_node_type child)
03027         {
03028                 if (parent != node_document && parent != node_element) return false;
03029                 if (child == node_document || child == node_null) return false;
03030                 if (parent != node_document && (child == node_declaration || child == node_doctype)) return false;
03031 
03032                 return true;
03033         }
03034 
03035         void recursive_copy_skip(xml_node& dest, const xml_node& source, const xml_node& skip)
03036         {
03037                 assert(dest.type() == source.type());
03038 
03039                 switch (source.type())
03040                 {
03041                 case node_element:
03042                 {
03043                         dest.set_name(source.name());
03044 
03045                         for (xml_attribute a = source.first_attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
03046                                 dest.append_attribute(a.name()).set_value(a.value());
03047 
03048                         for (xml_node c = source.first_child(); c; c = c.next_sibling())
03049                         {
03050                                 if (c == skip) continue;
03051 
03052                                 xml_node cc = dest.append_child(c.type());
03053                                 assert(cc);
03054 
03055                                 recursive_copy_skip(cc, c, skip);
03056                         }
03057 
03058                         break;
03059                 }
03060 
03061                 case node_pcdata:
03062                 case node_cdata:
03063                 case node_comment:
03064         case node_doctype:
03065                         dest.set_value(source.value());
03066                         break;
03067 
03068                 case node_pi:
03069                         dest.set_name(source.name());
03070                         dest.set_value(source.value());
03071                         break;
03072 
03073                 case node_declaration:
03074                 {
03075                         dest.set_name(source.name());
03076 
03077                         for (xml_attribute a = source.first_attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
03078                                 dest.append_attribute(a.name()).set_value(a.value());
03079 
03080                         break;
03081                 }
03082 
03083                 default:
03084                         assert(!"Invalid node type");
03085                 }
03086         }
03087 
03088         // we need to get length of entire file to load it in memory; the only (relatively) sane way to do it is via seek/tell trick
03089         xml_parse_status get_file_size(FILE* file, size_t& out_result)
03090         {
03091         #if defined(_MSC_VER) && _MSC_VER >= 1400
03092                 // there are 64-bit versions of fseek/ftell, let's use them
03093                 typedef __int64 length_type;
03094 
03095                 _fseeki64(file, 0, SEEK_END);
03096                 length_type length = _ftelli64(file);
03097                 _fseeki64(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
03098         #elif defined(__MINGW32__) && !defined(__NO_MINGW_LFS) && !defined(__STRICT_ANSI__)
03099                 // there are 64-bit versions of fseek/ftell, let's use them
03100                 typedef off64_t length_type;
03101 
03102                 fseeko64(file, 0, SEEK_END);
03103                 length_type length = ftello64(file);
03104                 fseeko64(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
03105         #else
03106                 // if this is a 32-bit OS, long is enough; if this is a unix system, long is 64-bit, which is enough; otherwise we can't do anything anyway.
03107                 typedef long length_type;
03108 
03109                 fseek(file, 0, SEEK_END);
03110                 length_type length = ftell(file);
03111                 fseek(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
03112         #endif
03113 
03114                 // check for I/O errors
03115                 if (length < 0) return status_io_error;
03116                 
03117                 // check for overflow
03118                 size_t result = static_cast<size_t>(length);
03119 
03120                 if (static_cast<length_type>(result) != length) return status_out_of_memory;
03121 
03122                 // finalize
03123                 out_result = result;
03124 
03125                 return status_ok;
03126         }
03127 
03128         xml_parse_result load_file_impl(xml_document& doc, FILE* file, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
03129         {
03130                 if (!file) return make_parse_result(status_file_not_found);
03131 
03132                 // get file size (can result in I/O errors)
03133                 size_t size = 0;
03134                 xml_parse_status size_status = get_file_size(file, size);
03135 
03136                 if (size_status != status_ok)
03137                 {
03138                         fclose(file);
03139                         return make_parse_result(size_status);
03140                 }
03141                 
03142                 // allocate buffer for the whole file
03143                 char* contents = static_cast<char*>(global_allocate(size > 0 ? size : 1));
03144 
03145                 if (!contents)
03146                 {
03147                         fclose(file);
03148                         return make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
03149                 }
03150 
03151                 // read file in memory
03152                 size_t read_size = fread(contents, 1, size, file);
03153                 fclose(file);
03154 
03155                 if (read_size != size)
03156                 {
03157                         global_deallocate(contents);
03158                         return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
03159                 }
03160                 
03161                 return doc.load_buffer_inplace_own(contents, size, options, encoding);
03162         }
03163 
03164 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
03165         template <typename T> xml_parse_result load_stream_impl(xml_document& doc, std::basic_istream<T>& stream, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
03166         {
03167                 // get length of remaining data in stream
03168                 typename std::basic_istream<T>::pos_type pos = stream.tellg();
03169                 stream.seekg(0, std::ios::end);
03170                 std::streamoff length = stream.tellg() - pos;
03171                 stream.seekg(pos);
03172 
03173                 if (stream.fail() || pos < 0) return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
03174 
03175                 // guard against huge files
03176                 size_t read_length = static_cast<size_t>(length);
03177 
03178                 if (static_cast<std::streamsize>(read_length) != length || length < 0) return make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
03179 
03180                 // read stream data into memory (guard against stream exceptions with buffer holder)
03181                 buffer_holder buffer(global_allocate((read_length > 0 ? read_length : 1) * sizeof(T)), global_deallocate);
03182                 if (!buffer.data) return make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
03183 
03184                 stream.read(static_cast<T*>(buffer.data), static_cast<std::streamsize>(read_length));
03185 
03186                 // read may set failbit | eofbit in case gcount() is less than read_length (i.e. line ending conversion), so check for other I/O errors
03187                 if (stream.bad()) return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
03188 
03189                 // load data from buffer
03190                 size_t actual_length = static_cast<size_t>(stream.gcount());
03191                 assert(actual_length <= read_length);
03192 
03193                 return doc.load_buffer_inplace_own(buffer.release(), actual_length * sizeof(T), options, encoding);
03194         }
03195 #endif
03196 
03197 #if defined(_MSC_VER) || defined(__BORLANDC__) || defined(__MINGW32__)
03198         FILE* open_file_wide(const wchar_t* path, const wchar_t* mode)
03199         {
03200                 return _wfopen(path, mode);
03201         }
03202 #else
03203         char* convert_path_heap(const wchar_t* str)
03204         {
03205                 assert(str);
03206 
03207                 // first pass: get length in utf8 characters
03208                 size_t length = wcslen(str);
03209         size_t size = as_utf8_begin(str, length);
03210 
03211                 // allocate resulting string
03212                 char* result = static_cast<char*>(global_allocate(size + 1));
03213                 if (!result) return 0;
03214 
03215                 // second pass: convert to utf8
03216         as_utf8_end(result, size, str, length);
03217 
03218                 return result;
03219         }
03220 
03221         FILE* open_file_wide(const wchar_t* path, const wchar_t* mode)
03222         {
03223                 // there is no standard function to open wide paths, so our best bet is to try utf8 path
03224                 char* path_utf8 = convert_path_heap(path);
03225                 if (!path_utf8) return 0;
03226 
03227                 // convert mode to ASCII (we mirror _wfopen interface)
03228                 char mode_ascii[4] = {0};
03229                 for (size_t i = 0; mode[i]; ++i) mode_ascii[i] = static_cast<char>(mode[i]);
03230 
03231                 // try to open the utf8 path
03232                 FILE* result = fopen(path_utf8, mode_ascii);
03233 
03234                 // free dummy buffer
03235                 global_deallocate(path_utf8);
03236 
03237                 return result;
03238         }
03239 #endif
03240 }

03273

03763                 case node_pi:
03764                 case node_cdata:
03765                 case node_pcdata:
03766                 case node_comment:
03767         case node_doctype:
03768                         return strcpy_insitu(_root->value, _root->header, xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask, rhs);

03775         xml_attribute xml_node::append_attribute(const char_t* name)
03776         {
03777                 if (type() != node_element && type() != node_declaration) return xml_attribute();
03778                 
03779                 xml_attribute a(append_attribute_ll(_root, get_allocator(_root)));
03780                 a.set_name(name);
03781                 
03782                 return a;

03784 
03785         xml_attribute xml_node::prepend_attribute(const char_t* name)
03786         {
03787                 if (type() != node_element && type() != node_declaration) return xml_attribute();
03788                 
03789                 xml_attribute a(allocate_attribute(get_allocator(_root)));
03790                 if (!a) return xml_attribute();
03791 
03792                 a.set_name(name);
03793                 
03794         xml_attribute_struct* head = _root->first_attribute;
03795 
03796                 if (head)
03797         {
03798             a._attr->prev_attribute_c = head->prev_attribute_c;
03799             head->prev_attribute_c = a._attr;
03800         }
03801         else
03802             a._attr->prev_attribute_c = a._attr;
03803                 
03804                 a._attr->next_attribute = head;
03805         _root->first_attribute = a._attr;
03806                                 
03807                 return a;
03808         }
03809 
03810         xml_attribute xml_node::insert_attribute_before(const char_t* name, const xml_attribute& attr)
03811         {
03812                 if ((type() != node_element && type() != node_declaration) || attr.empty()) return xml_attribute();
03813                 
03814                 // check that attribute belongs to *this
03815                 xml_attribute_struct* cur = attr._attr;
03816 
03817                 while (cur->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute) cur = cur->prev_attribute_c;
03818 
03819                 if (cur != _root->first_attribute) return xml_attribute();
03820 
03821                 xml_attribute a(allocate_attribute(get_allocator(_root)));
03822                 if (!a) return xml_attribute();
03823 
03824                 a.set_name(name);
03825 
03826                 if (attr._attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute)
03827                         attr._attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute = a._attr;
03828                 else
03829                         _root->first_attribute = a._attr;
03830                 
03831                 a._attr->prev_attribute_c = attr._attr->prev_attribute_c;
03832                 a._attr->next_attribute = attr._attr;
03833                 attr._attr->prev_attribute_c = a._attr;
03834                                 
03835                 return a;
03836         }
03837 
03838         xml_attribute xml_node::insert_attribute_after(const char_t* name, const xml_attribute& attr)
03839         {
03840                 if ((type() != node_element && type() != node_declaration) || attr.empty()) return xml_attribute();
03841                 
03842                 // check that attribute belongs to *this
03843                 xml_attribute_struct* cur = attr._attr;
03844 
03845                 while (cur->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute) cur = cur->prev_attribute_c;
03846 
03847                 if (cur != _root->first_attribute) return xml_attribute();
03848 
03849                 xml_attribute a(allocate_attribute(get_allocator(_root)));
03850                 if (!a) return xml_attribute();
03851 
03852                 a.set_name(name);
03853 
03854                 if (attr._attr->next_attribute)
03855                         attr._attr->next_attribute->prev_attribute_c = a._attr;
03856                 else
03857                         _root->first_attribute->prev_attribute_c = a._attr;
03858                 
03859                 a._attr->next_attribute = attr._attr->next_attribute;
03860                 a._attr->prev_attribute_c = attr._attr;
03861                 attr._attr->next_attribute = a._attr;
03862 
03863                 return a;
03864         }

03906         xml_node xml_node::append_child(xml_node_type type)
03907         {
03908                 if (!allow_insert_child(this->type(), type)) return xml_node();
03909                 
03910                 xml_node n(append_node(_root, get_allocator(_root), type));
03911 
03912                 if (type == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
03913 
03914                 return n;
03915         }
03916 
03917         xml_node xml_node::prepend_child(xml_node_type type)
03918         {
03919                 if (!allow_insert_child(this->type(), type)) return xml_node();
03920                 
03921                 xml_node n(allocate_node(get_allocator(_root), type));
03922                 if (!n) return xml_node();
03923 
03924         n._root->parent = _root;
03925 
03926         xml_node_struct* head = _root->first_child;
03927 
03928                 if (head)
03929         {
03930             n._root->prev_sibling_c = head->prev_sibling_c;
03931             head->prev_sibling_c = n._root;
03932         }
03933         else
03934             n._root->prev_sibling_c = n._root;
03935                 
03936                 n._root->next_sibling = head;
03937         _root->first_child = n._root;
03938                                 
03939                 if (type == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
03940 
03941                 return n;
03942         }
03943 
03944         xml_node xml_node::insert_child_before(xml_node_type type, const xml_node& node)
03945         {
03946                 if (!allow_insert_child(this->type(), type)) return xml_node();
03947                 if (!node._root || node._root->parent != _root) return xml_node();
03948         
03949                 xml_node n(allocate_node(get_allocator(_root), type));
03950                 if (!n) return xml_node();
03951 
03952                 n._root->parent = _root;
03953                 
03954                 if (node._root->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling)
03955                         node._root->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling = n._root;
03956                 else
03957                         _root->first_child = n._root;
03958                 
03959                 n._root->prev_sibling_c = node._root->prev_sibling_c;
03960                 n._root->next_sibling = node._root;
03961                 node._root->prev_sibling_c = n._root;
03962 
03963                 if (type == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
03964 
03965                 return n;
03966         }
03967 
03968         xml_node xml_node::insert_child_after(xml_node_type type, const xml_node& node)
03969         {
03970                 if (!allow_insert_child(this->type(), type)) return xml_node();
03971                 if (!node._root || node._root->parent != _root) return xml_node();
03972         
03973                 xml_node n(allocate_node(get_allocator(_root), type));
03974                 if (!n) return xml_node();
03975 
03976                 n._root->parent = _root;
03977         
03978                 if (node._root->next_sibling)
03979                         node._root->next_sibling->prev_sibling_c = n._root;
03980                 else
03981                         _root->first_child->prev_sibling_c = n._root;
03982                 
03983                 n._root->next_sibling = node._root->next_sibling;
03984                 n._root->prev_sibling_c = node._root;
03985                 node._root->next_sibling = n._root;
03986 
03987                 if (type == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
03988 
03989                 return n;
03990         }
