04064         bool xml_node::remove_attribute(const char_t* name)
04065         {
04066                 return remove_attribute(attribute(name));
04067         }
04068 
04069         bool xml_node::remove_attribute(const xml_attribute& a)
04070         {
04071                 if (!_root || !a._attr) return false;
04072 
04073                 // check that attribute belongs to *this
04074                 xml_attribute_struct* attr = a._attr;
04075 
04076                 while (attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute) attr = attr->prev_attribute_c;
04077 
04078                 if (attr != _root->first_attribute) return false;
04079 
04080                 if (a._attr->next_attribute) a._attr->next_attribute->prev_attribute_c = a._attr->prev_attribute_c;
04081                 else if (_root->first_attribute) _root->first_attribute->prev_attribute_c = a._attr->prev_attribute_c;
04082                 
04083                 if (a._attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute) a._attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute = a._attr->next_attribute;
04084                 else _root->first_attribute = a._attr->next_attribute;
04085 
04086                 destroy_attribute(a._attr, get_allocator(_root));
04087 
04088                 return true;
04089         }
04090 
04091         bool xml_node::remove_child(const char_t* name)
04092         {
04093                 return remove_child(child(name));
04094         }
04095 
04096         bool xml_node::remove_child(const xml_node& n)
04097         {
04098                 if (!_root || !n._root || n._root->parent != _root) return false;
04099 
04100                 if (n._root->next_sibling) n._root->next_sibling->prev_sibling_c = n._root->prev_sibling_c;
04101                 else if (_root->first_child) _root->first_child->prev_sibling_c = n._root->prev_sibling_c;
04102                 
04103                 if (n._root->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling) n._root->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling = n._root->next_sibling;
04104                 else _root->first_child = n._root->next_sibling;
04105         
04106         destroy_node(n._root, get_allocator(_root));
04107 
04108                 return true;
04109         }
04110 
04111         xml_node xml_node::find_child_by_attribute(const char_t* name, const char_t* attr_name, const char_t* attr_value) const
04112         {
04113                 if (!_root) return xml_node();
04114                 
04115                 for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
04116                         if (i->name && strequal(name, i->name))
04117                         {
04118                                 for (xml_attribute_struct* a = i->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
04119                                         if (strequal(attr_name, a->name) && strequal(attr_value, a->value))
04120                                                 return xml_node(i);
04121                         }
04122 
04123                 return xml_node();
04124         }
04125 
04126         xml_node xml_node::find_child_by_attribute(const char_t* attr_name, const char_t* attr_value) const
04127         {
04128                 if (!_root) return xml_node();
04129                 
04130                 for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
04131                         for (xml_attribute_struct* a = i->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
04132                                 if (strequal(attr_name, a->name) && strequal(attr_value, a->value))
04133                                         return xml_node(i);
04134 
04135                 return xml_node();
04136         }
04137 
04138 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
04139         string_t xml_node::path(char_t delimiter) const
04140         {
04141                 string_t path;
04142 
04143                 xml_node cursor = *this; // Make a copy.
04144                 
04145                 path = cursor.name();
04146 
04147                 while (cursor.parent())
04148                 {
04149                         cursor = cursor.parent();
04150                         
04151                         string_t temp = cursor.name();
04152                         temp += delimiter;
04153                         temp += path;
04154                         path.swap(temp);
04155                 }
04156 
04157                 return path;
04158         }
04159 #endif
04160 
04161         xml_node xml_node::first_element_by_path(const char_t* path, char_t delimiter) const
04162         {
04163                 xml_node found = *this; // Current search context.
04164 
04165                 if (!_root || !path || !path[0]) return found;
04166 
04167                 if (path[0] == delimiter)
04168                 {
04169                         // Absolute path; e.g. '/foo/bar'
04170                         found = found.root();
04171                         ++path;
04172                 }
04173 
04174                 const char_t* path_segment = path;
04175 
04176                 while (*path_segment == delimiter) ++path_segment;
04177 
04178                 const char_t* path_segment_end = path_segment;
04179 
04180                 while (*path_segment_end && *path_segment_end != delimiter) ++path_segment_end;
04181 
04182                 if (path_segment == path_segment_end) return found;
04183 
04184                 const char_t* next_segment = path_segment_end;
04185 
04186                 while (*next_segment == delimiter) ++next_segment;
04187 
04188                 if (*path_segment == '.' && path_segment + 1 == path_segment_end)
04189                         return found.first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
04190                 else if (*path_segment == '.' && *(path_segment+1) == '.' && path_segment + 2 == path_segment_end)
04191                         return found.parent().first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
04192                 else
04193                 {
04194                         for (xml_node_struct* j = found._root->first_child; j; j = j->next_sibling)
04195                         {
04196                                 if (j->name && strequalrange(j->name, path_segment, static_cast<size_t>(path_segment_end - path_segment)))
04197                                 {
04198                                         xml_node subsearch = xml_node(j).first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
04199 
04200                                         if (subsearch) return subsearch;
04201                                 }
04202                         }
04203 
04204                         return xml_node();
04205                 }
04206         }
04207 
04208         bool xml_node::traverse(xml_tree_walker& walker)
04209         {
04210                 walker._depth = -1;
04211                 
04212                 xml_node arg_begin = *this;
04213                 if (!walker.begin(arg_begin)) return false;
04214 
04215                 xml_node cur = first_child();
04216                                 
04217                 if (cur)
04218                 {
04219                         ++walker._depth;
04220 
04221                         do 
04222                         {
04223                                 xml_node arg_for_each = cur;
04224                                 if (!walker.for_each(arg_for_each))
04225                                         return false;
04226                                                 
04227                                 if (cur.first_child())
04228                                 {
04229                                         ++walker._depth;
04230                                         cur = cur.first_child();
04231                                 }
04232                                 else if (cur.next_sibling())
04233                                         cur = cur.next_sibling();
04234                                 else
04235                                 {
04236                                         // Borland C++ workaround
04237                                         while (!cur.next_sibling() && cur != *this && (bool)cur.parent())
04238                                         {
04239                                                 --walker._depth;
04240                                                 cur = cur.parent();
04241                                         }
04242                                                 
04243                                         if (cur != *this)
04244                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
04245                                 }
04246                         }
04247                         while (cur && cur != *this);
04248                 }
04249 
04250                 assert(walker._depth == -1);
04251 
04252                 xml_node arg_end = *this;
04253                 return walker.end(arg_end);
04254         }
04255

04258         return static_cast<size_t>(reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(_root) / sizeof(xml_node_struct));
04259     }

04290 
04291         ptrdiff_t xml_node::offset_debug() const
04292         {
04293                 xml_node_struct* r = root()._root;
04294 
04295                 if (!r) return -1;
04296 
04297                 const char_t* buffer = static_cast<xml_document_struct*>(r)->buffer;
04298 
04299                 if (!buffer) return -1;
04300 
04301                 switch (type())
04302                 {
04303                 case node_document:
04304                         return 0;
04305 
04306                 case node_element:
04307                 case node_declaration:
04308                 case node_pi:
04309                         return (_root->header & xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) ? -1 : _root->name - buffer;
04310 
04311                 case node_pcdata:
04312                 case node_cdata:
04313                 case node_comment:
04314                 case node_doctype:
04315                         return (_root->header & xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) ? -1 : _root->value - buffer;
04316 
04317                 default:
04318                         return -1;
04319                 }
04320         }
04321

04329         {

04460     xml_parse_result::operator bool() const
04461     {
04462         return status == status_ok;
04463     }
04464 
04465         const char* xml_parse_result::description() const
04466         {
04467                 switch (status)
04468                 {
04469                 case status_ok: return "No error";
04470 
04471                 case status_file_not_found: return "File was not found";
04472                 case status_io_error: return "Error reading from file/stream";
04473                 case status_out_of_memory: return "Could not allocate memory";
04474                 case status_internal_error: return "Internal error occurred";
04475 
04476                 case status_unrecognized_tag: return "Could not determine tag type";
04477 
04478                 case status_bad_pi: return "Error parsing document declaration/processing instruction";
04479                 case status_bad_comment: return "Error parsing comment";
04480                 case status_bad_cdata: return "Error parsing CDATA section";
04481                 case status_bad_doctype: return "Error parsing document type declaration";
04482                 case status_bad_pcdata: return "Error parsing PCDATA section";
04483                 case status_bad_start_element: return "Error parsing start element tag";
04484                 case status_bad_attribute: return "Error parsing element attribute";
04485                 case status_bad_end_element: return "Error parsing end element tag";
04486                 case status_end_element_mismatch: return "Start-end tags mismatch";
04487 
04488                 default: return "Unknown error";
04489                 }
04490         }
04491 
04492         xml_document::xml_document(): _buffer(0)
04493         {
04494                 create();
04495         }
04496 
04497         xml_document::~xml_document()
04498         {
04499                 destroy();
04500         }
04501 
04502         void xml_document::reset()
04503         {
04504                 destroy();
04505                 create();
04506         }
04507 
04508     void xml_document::reset(const xml_document& proto)
04509     {
04510         reset();
04511 
04512         for (xml_node cur = proto.first_child(); cur; cur = cur.next_sibling())
04513             append_copy(cur);
04514     }
04515 
04516         void xml_document::create()
04517         {
04518                 // initialize sentinel page
04519                 STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(xml_memory_page, data) + sizeof(xml_document_struct) + xml_memory_page_alignment <= sizeof(_memory));
04520 
04521                 // align upwards to page boundary
04522                 void* page_memory = reinterpret_cast<void*>((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(_memory) + (xml_memory_page_alignment - 1)) & ~(xml_memory_page_alignment - 1));
04523 
04524                 // prepare page structure
04525                 xml_memory_page* page = xml_memory_page::construct(page_memory);
04526 
04527                 page->busy_size = xml_memory_page_size;
04528 
04529                 // allocate new root
04530                 _root = new (page->data) xml_document_struct(page);
04531                 _root->prev_sibling_c = _root;
04532 
04533                 // setup sentinel page
04534                 page->allocator = static_cast<xml_document_struct*>(_root);
04535         }
04536 
04537         void xml_document::destroy()
04538         {
04539                 // destroy static storage
04540                 if (_buffer)
04541                 {
04542                         global_deallocate(_buffer);
04543                         _buffer = 0;
04544                 }
04545 
04546                 // destroy dynamic storage, leave sentinel page (it's in static memory)
04547                 if (_root)
04548                 {
04549                         xml_memory_page* root_page = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(_root->header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask);
04550                         assert(root_page && !root_page->prev && !root_page->memory);
04551 
04552                         // destroy all pages
04553                         for (xml_memory_page* page = root_page->next; page; )
04554                         {
04555                                 xml_memory_page* next = page->next;
04556 
04557                                 xml_allocator::deallocate_page(page);
04558 
04559                                 page = next;
04560                         }
04561 
04562                         // cleanup root page
04563                         root_page->allocator = 0;
04564                         root_page->next = 0;
04565                         root_page->busy_size = root_page->freed_size = 0;
04566 
04567                         _root = 0;
04568                 }
04569         }

04616 
04617         xml_parse_result xml_document::load_buffer_impl(void* contents, size_t size, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding, bool is_mutable, bool own)
04618         {
04619                 reset();
04620 
04621                 // check input buffer
04622                 assert(contents || size == 0);
04623 
04624                 // get actual encoding
04625                 xml_encoding buffer_encoding = get_buffer_encoding(encoding, contents, size);
04626 
04627                 // get private buffer
04628                 char_t* buffer = 0;
04629                 size_t length = 0;
04630 
04631                 if (!convert_buffer(buffer, length, buffer_encoding, contents, size, is_mutable)) return make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
04632                 
04633                 // delete original buffer if we performed a conversion
04634                 if (own && buffer != contents && contents) global_deallocate(contents);
04635 
04636                 // parse
04637                 xml_parse_result res = xml_parser::parse(buffer, length, _root, options);
04638 
04639                 // remember encoding
04640                 res.encoding = buffer_encoding;
04641 
04642                 // grab onto buffer if it's our buffer, user is responsible for deallocating contens himself
04643                 if (own || buffer != contents) _buffer = buffer;
04644 
04645                 return res;
04646         }
04647 
04648         xml_parse_result xml_document::load_buffer(const void* contents, size_t size, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
04649         {
04650                 return load_buffer_impl(const_cast<void*>(contents), size, options, encoding, false, false);
04651         }

04663         void xml_document::save(xml_writer& writer, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, xml_encoding encoding) const
04664         {
04665                 if (flags & format_write_bom) write_bom(writer, get_write_encoding(encoding));
04666 
04667                 xml_buffered_writer buffered_writer(writer, encoding);
04668 
04669                 if (!(flags & format_no_declaration) && !has_declaration(*this))
04670                 {
04671                         buffered_writer.write(PUGIXML_TEXT("<?xml version=\"1.0\"?>"));
04672                         if (!(flags & format_raw)) buffered_writer.write('\n');
04673                 }
04674 
04675                 node_output(buffered_writer, *this, indent, flags, 0);
04676         }

04804 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_XPATH
04805 
04806 // STL replacements
04807 namespace
04808 {
04809         struct equal_to
04810         {
04811                 template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
04812                 {
04813                         return lhs == rhs;
04814                 }
04815         };
04816 
04817         struct not_equal_to
04818         {
04819                 template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
04820                 {
04821                         return lhs != rhs;
04822                 }
04823         };
04824 
04825         struct less
04826         {
04827                 template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
04828                 {
04829                         return lhs < rhs;
04830                 }
04831         };
04832 
04833         struct less_equal
04834         {
04835                 template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
04836                 {
04837                         return lhs <= rhs;
04838                 }
04839         };
04840 
04841         template <typename T> void swap(T& lhs, T& rhs)
04842         {
04843                 T temp = lhs;
04844                 lhs = rhs;
04845                 rhs = temp;
04846         }
04847 
04848         template <typename I, typename Pred> I min_element(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred)
04849         {
04850                 I result = begin;
04851 
04852                 for (I it = begin + 1; it != end; ++it)
04853                         if (pred(*it, *result))
04854                                 result = it;
04855 
04856                 return result;
04857         }
04858 
04859         template <typename I> void reverse(I begin, I end)
04860         {
04861                 while (begin + 1 < end) swap(*begin++, *--end);
04862         }
04863 
04864         template <typename I> I unique(I begin, I end)
04865         {
04866                 // fast skip head
04867                 while (begin + 1 < end && *begin != *(begin + 1)) begin++;
04868 
04869                 if (begin == end) return begin;
04870 
04871                 // last written element
04872                 I write = begin++; 
04873 
04874                 // merge unique elements
04875                 while (begin != end)
04876                 {
04877                         if (*begin != *write)
04878                                 *++write = *begin++;
04879                         else
04880                                 begin++;
04881                 }
04882 
04883                 // past-the-end (write points to live element)
04884                 return write + 1;
04885         }
04886 
04887         template <typename I> void copy_backwards(I begin, I end, I target)
04888         {
04889                 while (begin != end) *--target = *--end;
04890         }
04891 
04892         template <typename I, typename Pred, typename T> void insertion_sort(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred, T*)
04893         {
04894                 assert(begin != end);
04895 
04896                 for (I it = begin + 1; it != end; ++it)
04897                 {
04898                         T val = *it;
04899 
04900                         if (pred(val, *begin))
04901                         {
04902                                 // move to front
04903                                 copy_backwards(begin, it, it + 1);
04904                                 *begin = val;
04905                         }
04906                         else
04907                         {
04908                                 I hole = it;
04909 
04910                                 // move hole backwards
04911                                 while (pred(val, *(hole - 1)))
04912                                 {
04913                                         *hole = *(hole - 1);
04914                                         hole--;
04915                                 }
04916 
04917                                 // fill hole with element
04918                                 *hole = val;
04919                         }
04920                 }
04921         }
04922 
04923         // std variant for elements with ==
04924         template <typename I, typename Pred> void partition(I begin, I middle, I end, const Pred& pred, I* out_eqbeg, I* out_eqend)
04925         {
04926                 I eqbeg = middle, eqend = middle + 1;
04927 
04928                 // expand equal range
04929                 while (eqbeg != begin && *(eqbeg - 1) == *eqbeg) --eqbeg;
04930                 while (eqend != end && *eqend == *eqbeg) ++eqend;
04931 
04932                 // process outer elements
04933                 I ltend = eqbeg, gtbeg = eqend;
04934 
04935                 for (;;)
04936                 {
04937                         // find the element from the right side that belongs to the left one
04938                         for (; gtbeg != end; ++gtbeg)
04939                                 if (!pred(*eqbeg, *gtbeg))
04940                                 {
04941                                         if (*gtbeg == *eqbeg) swap(*gtbeg, *eqend++);
04942                                         else break;
04943                                 }
04944 
04945                         // find the element from the left side that belongs to the right one
04946                         for (; ltend != begin; --ltend)
04947                                 if (!pred(*(ltend - 1), *eqbeg))
04948                                 {
04949                                         if (*eqbeg == *(ltend - 1)) swap(*(ltend - 1), *--eqbeg);
04950                                         else break;
04951                                 }
04952 
04953                         // scanned all elements
04954                         if (gtbeg == end && ltend == begin)
04955                         {
04956                                 *out_eqbeg = eqbeg;
04957                                 *out_eqend = eqend;
04958                                 return;
04959                         }
04960 
04961                         // make room for elements by moving equal area
04962                         if (gtbeg == end)
04963                         {
04964                                 if (--ltend != --eqbeg) swap(*ltend, *eqbeg);
04965                                 swap(*eqbeg, *--eqend);
04966                         }
04967                         else if (ltend == begin)
04968                         {
04969                                 if (eqend != gtbeg) swap(*eqbeg, *eqend);
04970                                 ++eqend;
04971                                 swap(*gtbeg++, *eqbeg++);
04972                         }
04973                         else swap(*gtbeg++, *--ltend);
04974                 }
04975         }
04976 
04977         template <typename I, typename Pred> void median3(I first, I middle, I last, const Pred& pred)
04978         {
04979                 if (pred(*middle, *first)) swap(*middle, *first);
04980                 if (pred(*last, *middle)) swap(*last, *middle);
04981                 if (pred(*middle, *first)) swap(*middle, *first);
04982         }
04983 
04984         template <typename I, typename Pred> void median(I first, I middle, I last, const Pred& pred)
04985         {
04986                 if (last - first <= 40)
04987                 {
04988                         // median of three for small chunks
04989                         median3(first, middle, last, pred);
04990                 }
04991                 else
04992                 {
04993                         // median of nine
04994                         size_t step = (last - first + 1) / 8;
04995 
04996                         median3(first, first + step, first + 2 * step, pred);
04997                         median3(middle - step, middle, middle + step, pred);
04998                         median3(last - 2 * step, last - step, last, pred);
04999                         median3(first + step, middle, last - step, pred);
05000                 }
05001         }
05002 
05003         template <typename I, typename Pred> void sort(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred)
05004         {
05005                 // sort large chunks
05006                 while (end - begin > 32)
05007                 {
05008                         // find median element
05009                         I middle = begin + (end - begin) / 2;
05010                         median(begin, middle, end - 1, pred);
05011 
05012                         // partition in three chunks (< = >)
05013                         I eqbeg, eqend;
05014                         partition(begin, middle, end, pred, &eqbeg, &eqend);
05015 
05016                         // loop on larger half
05017                         if (eqbeg - begin > end - eqend)
05018                         {
05019                                 sort(eqend, end, pred);
05020                                 end = eqbeg;
05021                         }
05022                         else
05023                         {
05024                                 sort(begin, eqbeg, pred);
05025                                 begin = eqend;
05026                         }
05027                 }
05028 
05029                 // insertion sort small chunk
05030                 if (begin != end) insertion_sort(begin, end, pred, &*begin);
05031         }
05032 }
05033 
05034 // Allocator used for AST and evaluation stacks
05035 namespace
05036 {
05037         struct xpath_memory_block
05038         {       
05039                 xpath_memory_block* next;
05040 
05041                 char data[4096];
05042         };
05043                 
05044         class xpath_allocator
05045         {
05046                 xpath_memory_block* _root;
05047                 size_t _root_size;
05048 
05049         public:
05050         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
05051                 jmp_buf* error_handler;
05052         #endif
05053 
05054                 xpath_allocator(xpath_memory_block* root, size_t root_size = 0): _root(root), _root_size(root_size)
05055                 {
05056                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
05057                         error_handler = 0;
05058                 #endif
05059                 }
05060                 
05061                 void* allocate_nothrow(size_t size)
05062                 {
05063                         const size_t block_capacity = sizeof(_root->data);
05064 
05065                         // align size so that we're able to store pointers in subsequent blocks
05066                         size = (size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
05067 
05068                         if (_root_size + size <= block_capacity)
05069                         {
05070                                 void* buf = _root->data + _root_size;
05071                                 _root_size += size;
05072                                 return buf;
05073                         }
05074                         else
05075                         {
05076                                 size_t block_data_size = (size > block_capacity) ? size : block_capacity;
05077                                 size_t block_size = block_data_size + offsetof(xpath_memory_block, data);
05078 
05079                                 xpath_memory_block* block = static_cast<xpath_memory_block*>(global_allocate(block_size));
05080                                 if (!block) return 0;
05081                                 
05082                                 block->next = _root;
05083                                 
05084                                 _root = block;
05085                                 _root_size = size;
05086                                 
05087                                 return block->data;
05088                         }
05089                 }
05090 
05091                 void* allocate(size_t size)
05092                 {
05093                         void* result = allocate_nothrow(size);
05094 
05095                         if (!result)
05096                         {
05097                         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
05098                                 assert(error_handler);
05099                                 longjmp(*error_handler, 1);
05100                         #else
05101                                 throw std::bad_alloc();
05102                         #endif
05103                         }
05104 
05105                         return result;
05106                 }
05107 
05108                 void* reallocate(void* ptr, size_t old_size, size_t new_size)
05109                 {
05110                         // align size so that we're able to store pointers in subsequent blocks
05111                         old_size = (old_size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
05112                         new_size = (new_size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
05113 
05114                         // we can only reallocate the last object
05115                         assert(ptr == 0 || static_cast<char*>(ptr) + old_size == _root->data + _root_size);
05116 
05117                         // adjust root size so that we have not allocated the object at all
05118                         bool only_object = (_root_size == old_size);
05119 
05120                         if (ptr) _root_size -= old_size;
05121 
05122                         // allocate a new version (this will obviously reuse the memory if possible)
05123                         void* result = allocate(new_size);
05124                         assert(result);
05125 
05126                         // we have a new block
05127                         if (result != ptr && ptr)
05128                         {
05129                                 // copy old data
05130                                 assert(new_size > old_size);
05131                                 memcpy(result, ptr, old_size);
05132 
05133                                 // free the previous page if it had no other objects
05134                                 if (only_object)
05135                                 {
05136                                         assert(_root->data == result);
05137                                         assert(_root->next);
05138 
05139                                         xpath_memory_block* next = _root->next->next;
05140 
05141                                         if (next)
05142                                         {
05143                                                 // deallocate the whole page, unless it was the first one
05144                                                 global_deallocate(_root->next);
05145                                                 _root->next = next;
05146                                         }
05147                                 }
05148                         }
05149 
05150                         return result;
05151                 }
05152 
05153                 void revert(const xpath_allocator& state)
05154                 {
05155                         // free all new pages
05156                         xpath_memory_block* cur = _root;
05157 
05158                         while (cur != state._root)
05159                         {
05160                                 xpath_memory_block* next = cur->next;
05161 
05162                                 global_deallocate(cur);
05163 
05164                                 cur = next;
05165                         }
05166 
05167                         // restore state
05168                         _root = state._root;
05169                         _root_size = state._root_size;
05170                 }
05171 
05172                 void release()
05173                 {
05174                         xpath_memory_block* cur = _root;
05175                         assert(cur);
05176 
05177                         while (cur->next)
05178                         {
05179                                 xpath_memory_block* next = cur->next;
05180 
05181                                 global_deallocate(cur);
05182 
05183                                 cur = next;
05184                         }
05185                 }
05186         };
05187 
05188         struct xpath_allocator_capture
05189         {
05190                 xpath_allocator_capture(xpath_allocator* alloc): _target(alloc), _state(*alloc)
05191                 {
05192                 }
05193 
05194                 ~xpath_allocator_capture()
05195                 {
05196                         _target->revert(_state);
05197                 }
05198 
05199                 xpath_allocator* _target;
05200                 xpath_allocator _state;
05201         };
05202 
05203         struct xpath_stack
05204         {
05205                 xpath_allocator* result;
05206                 xpath_allocator* temp;
05207         };
05208 
05209         struct xpath_stack_data
05210         {
05211                 xpath_memory_block blocks[2];
05212                 xpath_allocator result;
05213                 xpath_allocator temp;
05214                 xpath_stack stack;
05215 
05216         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
05217                 jmp_buf error_handler;
05218         #endif
05219 
05220                 xpath_stack_data(): result(blocks + 0), temp(blocks + 1)
05221                 {
05222                         blocks[0].next = blocks[1].next = 0;
05223 
05224                         stack.result = &result;
05225                         stack.temp = &temp;
05226 
05227                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
05228                         result.error_handler = temp.error_handler = &error_handler;
05229                 #endif
05230                 }
05231 
05232                 ~xpath_stack_data()
05233                 {
05234                         result.release();
05235                         temp.release();
05236                 }
05237         };
05238 }
05239 
05240 // String class
05241 namespace
05242 {
05243         class xpath_string
05244         {
05245                 const char_t* _buffer;
05246                 bool _uses_heap;
05247 
05248                 static char_t* duplicate_string(const char_t* string, size_t length, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05249                 {
05250                         char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(alloc->allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
05251                         assert(result);
05252 
05253                         memcpy(result, string, length * sizeof(char_t));
05254                         result[length] = 0;
05255 
05256                         return result;
05257                 }
05258 
05259                 static char_t* duplicate_string(const char_t* string, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05260                 {
05261                         return duplicate_string(string, strlength(string), alloc);
05262                 }
05263 
05264         public:
05265                 xpath_string(): _buffer(PUGIXML_TEXT("")), _uses_heap(false)
05266                 {
05267                 }
05268 
05269                 explicit xpath_string(const char_t* str, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05270                 {
05271                         bool empty = (*str == 0);
05272 
05273                         _buffer = empty ? PUGIXML_TEXT("") : duplicate_string(str, alloc);
05274                         _uses_heap = !empty;
05275                 }
05276 
05277                 explicit xpath_string(const char_t* str, bool use_heap): _buffer(str), _uses_heap(use_heap)
05278                 {
05279                 }
05280 
05281                 xpath_string(const char_t* begin, const char_t* end, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05282                 {
05283                         assert(begin <= end);
05284 
05285                         bool empty = (begin == end);
05286 
05287                         _buffer = empty ? PUGIXML_TEXT("") : duplicate_string(begin, static_cast<size_t>(end - begin), alloc);
05288                         _uses_heap = !empty;
05289                 }
05290 
05291                 void append(const xpath_string& o, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05292                 {
05293                         // skip empty sources
05294                         if (!*o._buffer) return;
05295 
05296                         // fast append for constant empty target and constant source
05297                         if (!*_buffer && !_uses_heap && !o._uses_heap)
05298                         {
05299                                 _buffer = o._buffer;
05300                         }
05301                         else
05302                         {
05303                                 // need to make heap copy
05304                                 size_t target_length = strlength(_buffer);
05305                                 size_t source_length = strlength(o._buffer);
05306                                 size_t length = target_length + source_length;
05307 
05308                                 // allocate new buffer
05309                                 char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(alloc->reallocate(_uses_heap ? const_cast<char_t*>(_buffer) : 0, (target_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t), (length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
05310                                 assert(result);
05311 
05312                                 // append first string to the new buffer in case there was no reallocation
05313                                 if (!_uses_heap) memcpy(result, _buffer, target_length * sizeof(char_t));
05314 
05315                                 // append second string to the new buffer
05316                                 memcpy(result + target_length, o._buffer, source_length * sizeof(char_t));
05317                                 result[length] = 0;
05318 
05319                                 // finalize
05320                                 _buffer = result;
05321                                 _uses_heap = true;
05322                         }
05323                 }
05324 
05325                 const char_t* c_str() const
05326                 {
05327                         return _buffer;
05328                 }
05329 
05330                 size_t length() const
05331                 {
05332                         return strlength(_buffer);
05333                 }
05334                 
05335                 char_t* data(xpath_allocator* alloc)
05336                 {
05337                         // make private heap copy
05338                         if (!_uses_heap)
05339                         {
05340                                 _buffer = duplicate_string(_buffer, alloc);
05341                                 _uses_heap = true;
05342                         }
05343 
05344                         return const_cast<char_t*>(_buffer);
05345                 }
05346 
05347                 bool empty() const
05348                 {
05349                         return *_buffer == 0;
05350                 }
05351 
05352                 bool operator==(const xpath_string& o) const
05353                 {
05354                         return strequal(_buffer, o._buffer);
05355                 }
05356 
05357                 bool operator!=(const xpath_string& o) const
05358                 {
05359                         return !strequal(_buffer, o._buffer);
05360                 }
05361 
05362                 bool uses_heap() const
05363                 {
05364                         return _uses_heap;
05365                 }
05366         };
05367 
05368         xpath_string xpath_string_const(const char_t* str)
05369         {
05370                 return xpath_string(str, false);
05371         }
05372 }
05373 
05374 namespace
05375 {
05376         bool starts_with(const char_t* string, const char_t* pattern)
05377         {
05378                 while (*pattern && *string == *pattern)
05379                 {
05380                         string++;
05381                         pattern++;
05382                 }
05383 
05384                 return *pattern == 0;
05385         }
05386 
05387         const char_t* find_char(const char_t* s, char_t c)
05388         {
05389         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
05390                 return wcschr(s, c);
05391         #else
05392                 return strchr(s, c);
05393         #endif
05394         }
05395 
05396         const char_t* find_substring(const char_t* s, const char_t* p)
05397         {
05398         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
05399                 // MSVC6 wcsstr bug workaround (if s is empty it always returns 0)
05400                 return (*p == 0) ? s : wcsstr(s, p);
05401         #else
05402                 return strstr(s, p);
05403         #endif
05404         }
05405 
05406         // Converts symbol to lower case, if it is an ASCII one
05407         char_t tolower_ascii(char_t ch)
05408         {
05409                 return static_cast<unsigned int>(ch - 'A') < 26 ? static_cast<char_t>(ch | ' ') : ch;
05410         }
05411 
05412         xpath_string string_value(const xpath_node& na, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05413         {
05414                 if (na.attribute())
05415                         return xpath_string_const(na.attribute().value());
05416                 else
05417                 {
05418                         const xml_node& n = na.node();
05419 
05420                         switch (n.type())
05421                         {
05422                         case node_pcdata:
05423                         case node_cdata:
05424                         case node_comment:
05425                         case node_pi:
05426                                 return xpath_string_const(n.value());
05427                         
05428                         case node_document:
05429                         case node_element:
05430                         {
05431                                 xpath_string result;
05432 
05433                                 xml_node cur = n.first_child();
05434                                 
05435                                 while (cur && cur != n)
05436                                 {
05437                                         if (cur.type() == node_pcdata || cur.type() == node_cdata)
05438                                                 result.append(xpath_string_const(cur.value()), alloc);
05439 
05440                                         if (cur.first_child())
05441                                                 cur = cur.first_child();
05442                                         else if (cur.next_sibling())
05443                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
05444                                         else
05445                                         {
05446                                                 while (!cur.next_sibling() && cur != n)
05447                                                         cur = cur.parent();
05448 
05449                                                 if (cur != n) cur = cur.next_sibling();
05450                                         }
05451                                 }
05452                                 
05453                                 return result;
05454                         }
05455                         
05456                         default:
05457                                 return xpath_string();
05458                         }
05459                 }
05460         }
05461         
05462         unsigned int node_height(xml_node n)
05463         {
05464             unsigned int result = 0;
05465             
05466             while (n)
05467             {
05468                 ++result;
05469                 n = n.parent();
05470             }
05471             
05472             return result;
05473         }
05474         
05475         bool node_is_before(xml_node ln, unsigned int lh, xml_node rn, unsigned int rh)
05476         {
05477                 // normalize heights
05478                 for (unsigned int i = rh; i < lh; i++) ln = ln.parent();
05479                 for (unsigned int j = lh; j < rh; j++) rn = rn.parent();
05480             
05481                 // one node is the ancestor of the other
05482             if (ln == rn) return lh < rh;
05483             
05484                 // find common ancestor
05485             while (ln.parent() != rn.parent())
05486             {
05487                 ln = ln.parent();
05488                 rn = rn.parent();
05489             }
05490 
05491                 // there is no common ancestor (the shared parent is null), nodes are from different documents
05492                 if (!ln.parent()) return ln < rn;
05493 
05494                 // determine sibling order
05495         for (; ln; ln = ln.next_sibling())
05496             if (ln == rn)
05497                 return true;
05498                 
05499         return false;
05500     }
05501 
05502     bool node_is_ancestor(xml_node parent, xml_node node)
05503     {
05504         while (node && node != parent) node = node.parent();
05505 
05506         return parent && node == parent;
05507     }
05508 
05509     const void* document_order(const xpath_node& xnode)
05510     {
05511         xml_node_struct* node = xnode.node().internal_object();
05512 
05513         if (node)
05514         {
05515             if (node->name && (node->header & xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) == 0) return node->name;
05516             if (node->value && (node->header & xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) == 0) return node->value;
05517             return 0;
05518         }
05519 
05520         xml_attribute_struct* attr = xnode.attribute().internal_object();
05521 
05522         if (attr)
05523         {
05524             if ((attr->header & xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) == 0) return attr->name;
05525             if ((attr->header & xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) == 0) return attr->value;
05526             return 0;
05527         }
05528 
05529                 return 0;
05530     }
05531     
05532         struct document_order_comparator
05533         {
05534                 bool operator()(const xpath_node& lhs, const xpath_node& rhs) const
05535                 {
05536                         // optimized document order based check
05537                         const void* lo = document_order(lhs);
05538                         const void* ro = document_order(rhs);
05539 
05540                         if (lo && ro) return lo < ro;
05541 
05542             // slow comparison
05543                         xml_node ln = lhs.node(), rn = rhs.node();
05544 
05545                         // compare attributes
05546                         if (lhs.attribute() && rhs.attribute())
05547                         {
05548                                 // shared parent
05549                                 if (lhs.parent() == rhs.parent())
05550                                 {
05551                                         // determine sibling order
05552                                     for (xml_attribute a = lhs.attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
05553                                         if (a == rhs.attribute())
05554                                             return true;
05555                                     
05556                                     return false;
05557                                 }
05558                                 
05559                                 // compare attribute parents
05560                                 ln = lhs.parent();
05561                                 rn = rhs.parent();
05562                         }
05563                         else if (lhs.attribute())
05564                         {
05565                                 // attributes go after the parent element
05566                                 if (lhs.parent() == rhs.node()) return false;
05567                                 
05568                                 ln = lhs.parent();
05569                         }
05570                         else if (rhs.attribute())
05571                         {
05572                                 // attributes go after the parent element
05573                                 if (rhs.parent() == lhs.node()) return true;
05574                                 
05575                                 rn = rhs.parent();
05576                         }
05577 
05578                         if (ln == rn) return false;
05579                         
05580                         unsigned int lh = node_height(ln);
05581                         unsigned int rh = node_height(rn);
05582                         
05583                         return node_is_before(ln, lh, rn, rh);
05584                 }
05585         };
05586 
05587         struct duplicate_comparator
05588         {
05589                 bool operator()(const xpath_node& lhs, const xpath_node& rhs) const
05590                 {
05591                         if (lhs.attribute()) return rhs.attribute() ? lhs.attribute() < rhs.attribute() : true;
05592                         else return rhs.attribute() ? false : lhs.node() < rhs.node();
05593                 }
05594         };
05595         
05596         double gen_nan()
05597         {
05598         #if defined(__STDC_IEC_559__) || ((FLT_RADIX - 0 == 2) && (FLT_MAX_EXP - 0 == 128) && (FLT_MANT_DIG - 0 == 24))
05599                 union { float f; int32_t i; } u[sizeof(float) == sizeof(int32_t) ? 1 : -1];
05600                 u[0].i = 0x7fc00000;
05601                 return u[0].f;
05602         #else
05603                 // fallback
05604                 const volatile double zero = 0.0;
05605                 return zero / zero;
05606         #endif
05607         }
05608         
05609         bool is_nan(double value)
05610         {
05611         #if defined(_MSC_VER) || defined(__BORLANDC__)
05612                 return !!_isnan(value);
05613         #elif defined(fpclassify) && defined(FP_NAN)
05614                 return fpclassify(value) == FP_NAN;
05615         #else
05616                 // fallback
05617                 const volatile double v = value;
05618                 return v != v;
05619         #endif
05620         }
05621         
05622         const char_t* convert_number_to_string_special(double value)
05623         {
05624         #if defined(_MSC_VER) || defined(__BORLANDC__)
05625                 if (_finite(value)) return (value == 0) ? PUGIXML_TEXT("0") : 0;
05626                 if (_isnan(value)) return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
05627                 return PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity") + (value > 0);
05628         #elif defined(fpclassify) && defined(FP_NAN) && defined(FP_INFINITE) && defined(FP_ZERO)
05629                 switch (fpclassify(value))
05630                 {
05631                 case FP_NAN:
05632                         return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
05633 
05634                 case FP_INFINITE:
05635                         return PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity") + (value > 0);
05636 
05637                 case FP_ZERO:
05638                         return PUGIXML_TEXT("0");
05639 
05640                 default:
05641                         return 0;
05642                 }
05643         #else
05644                 // fallback
05645                 const volatile double v = value;
05646 
05647                 if (v == 0) return PUGIXML_TEXT("0");
05648                 if (v != v) return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
05649                 if (v * 2 == v) return PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity") + (value > 0);
05650                 return 0;
05651         #endif
05652         }
05653         
05654         bool convert_number_to_boolean(double value)
05655         {
05656                 return (value != 0 && !is_nan(value));
05657         }
05658         
05659         void truncate_zeros(char* begin, char* end)
05660         {
05661                 while (begin != end && end[-1] == '0') end--;
05662 
05663                 *end = 0;
05664         }
05665 
05666         // gets mantissa digits in the form of 0.xxxxx with 0. implied and the exponent
05667 #if defined(_MSC_VER) && _MSC_VER >= 1400
05668         void convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(double value, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size, char** out_mantissa, int* out_exponent)
05669         {
05670                 // get base values
05671                 int sign, exponent;
05672                 _ecvt_s(buffer, buffer_size, value, DBL_DIG + 1, &exponent, &sign);
05673 
05674                 // truncate redundant zeros
05675                 truncate_zeros(buffer, buffer + strlen(buffer));
05676 
05677                 // fill results
05678                 *out_mantissa = buffer;
05679                 *out_exponent = exponent;
05680         }
05681 #else
05682         void convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(double value, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size, char** out_mantissa, int* out_exponent)
05683         {
05684                 // get a scientific notation value with IEEE DBL_DIG decimals
05685                 sprintf(buffer, "%.*e", DBL_DIG, value);
05686                 assert(strlen(buffer) < buffer_size);
05687                 (void)!buffer_size;
05688 
05689                 // get the exponent (possibly negative)
05690                 char* exponent_string = strchr(buffer, 'e');
05691                 assert(exponent_string);
05692 
05693                 int exponent = atoi(exponent_string + 1);
05694 
05695                 // extract mantissa string: skip sign
05696                 char* mantissa = buffer[0] == '-' ? buffer + 1 : buffer;
05697                 assert(mantissa[0] != '0' && mantissa[1] == '.');
05698 
05699                 // divide mantissa by 10 to eliminate integer part
05700                 mantissa[1] = mantissa[0];
05701                 mantissa++;
05702                 exponent++;
05703 
05704                 // remove extra mantissa digits and zero-terminate mantissa
05705                 truncate_zeros(mantissa, exponent_string);
05706 
05707                 // fill results
05708                 *out_mantissa = mantissa;
05709                 *out_exponent = exponent;
05710         }
05711 #endif
05712 
05713         xpath_string convert_number_to_string(double value, xpath_allocator* alloc)
05714         {
05715                 // try special number conversion
05716                 const char_t* special = convert_number_to_string_special(value);
05717                 if (special) return xpath_string_const(special);
05718 
05719                 // get mantissa + exponent form
05720                 char mantissa_buffer[64];
05721 
05722                 char* mantissa;
05723                 int exponent;
05724                 convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(value, mantissa_buffer, sizeof(mantissa_buffer), &mantissa, &exponent);
05725 
05726                 // make the number!
05727                 char_t result[512];
05728                 char_t* s = result;
05729 
05730                 // sign
05731                 if (value < 0) *s++ = '-';
05732 
05733                 // integer part
05734                 if (exponent <= 0)
05735                 {
05736                         *s++ = '0';
05737                 }
05738                 else
05739                 {
05740                         while (exponent > 0)
05741                         {
05742                                 assert(*mantissa == 0 || (unsigned)(*mantissa - '0') <= 9);
05743                                 *s++ = *mantissa ? *mantissa++ : '0';
05744                                 exponent--;
05745                         }
05746                 }
05747 
05748                 // fractional part
05749                 if (*mantissa)
05750                 {
05751                         // decimal point
05752                         *s++ = '.';
05753 
05754                         // extra zeroes from negative exponent
05755                         while (exponent < 0)
05756                         {
05757                                 *s++ = '0';
05758                                 exponent++;
05759                         }
05760 
05761                         // extra mantissa digits
05762                         while (*mantissa)
05763                         {
05764                                 assert((unsigned)(*mantissa - '0') <= 9);
05765                                 *s++ = *mantissa++;
05766                         }
05767                 }
05768 
05769                 // zero-terminate
05770                 assert(s < result + sizeof(result) / sizeof(result[0]));
05771                 *s = 0;
05772 
05773                 return xpath_string(result, alloc);
05774         }
05775         
05776         bool check_string_to_number_format(const char_t* string)
05777         {
05778                 // parse leading whitespace
05779                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*string, ct_space)) ++string;
05780 
05781                 // parse sign
05782                 if (*string == '-') ++string;
05783 
05784                 if (!*string) return false;
05785 
05786                 // if there is no integer part, there should be a decimal part with at least one digit
05787                 if (!IS_CHARTYPEX(string[0], ctx_digit) && (string[0] != '.' || !IS_CHARTYPEX(string[1], ctx_digit))) return false;
05788 
05789                 // parse integer part
05790                 while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*string, ctx_digit)) ++string;
05791 
05792                 // parse decimal part
05793                 if (*string == '.')
05794                 {
05795                         ++string;
05796 
05797                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*string, ctx_digit)) ++string;
05798                 }
05799 
05800                 // parse trailing whitespace
05801                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*string, ct_space)) ++string;
05802 
05803                 return *string == 0;
05804         }
05805 
05806         double convert_string_to_number(const char_t* string)
05807         {
05808                 // check string format
05809                 if (!check_string_to_number_format(string)) return gen_nan();
05810 
05811                 // parse string
05812         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
05813                 return wcstod(string, 0);
05814         #else
05815                 return atof(string);
05816         #endif
05817         }
05818 
05819         bool convert_string_to_number(const char_t* begin, const char_t* end, double* out_result)
05820         {
05821                 char_t buffer[32];
05822 
05823                 size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
05824                 char_t* scratch = buffer;
05825 
05826                 if (length >= sizeof(buffer) / sizeof(buffer[0]))
05827                 {
05828                         // need to make dummy on-heap copy
05829                         scratch = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
05830                         if (!scratch) return false;
05831                 }
05832 
05833                 // copy string to zero-terminated buffer and perform conversion
05834                 memcpy(scratch, begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
05835                 scratch[length] = 0;
05836 
05837                 *out_result = convert_string_to_number(scratch);
05838 
05839                 // free dummy buffer
05840                 if (scratch != buffer) global_deallocate(scratch);
05841 
05842                 return true;
05843         }
05844         
05845         double round_nearest(double value)
05846         {
05847                 return floor(value + 0.5);
05848         }
05849 
05850         double round_nearest_nzero(double value)
05851         {
05852                 // same as round_nearest, but returns -0 for [-0.5, -0]
05853                 // ceil is used to differentiate between +0 and -0 (we return -0 for [-0.5, -0] and +0 for +0)
05854                 return (value >= -0.5 && value <= 0) ? ceil(value) : floor(value + 0.5);
05855         }
05856         
05857         const char_t* qualified_name(const xpath_node& node)
05858         {
05859                 return node.attribute() ? node.attribute().name() : node.node().name();
05860         }
05861         
05862         const char_t* local_name(const xpath_node& node)
05863         {
05864                 const char_t* name = qualified_name(node);
05865                 const char_t* p = find_char(name, ':');
05866                 
05867                 return p ? p + 1 : name;
05868         }
05869 
05870         struct namespace_uri_predicate
05871         {
05872                 const char_t* prefix;
05873                 size_t prefix_length;
05874 
05875                 namespace_uri_predicate(const char_t* name)
05876                 {
05877                         const char_t* pos = find_char(name, ':');
05878 
05879                         prefix = pos ? name : 0;
05880                         prefix_length = pos ? static_cast<size_t>(pos - name) : 0;
05881                 }
05882 
05883                 bool operator()(const xml_attribute& a) const
05884                 {
05885                         const char_t* name = a.name();
05886 
05887                         if (!starts_with(name, PUGIXML_TEXT("xmlns"))) return false;
05888 
05889                         return prefix ? name[5] == ':' && strequalrange(name + 6, prefix, prefix_length) : name[5] == 0;
05890                 }
05891         };
05892 
05893         const char_t* namespace_uri(const xml_node& node)
05894         {
05895                 namespace_uri_predicate pred = node.name();
05896                 
05897                 xml_node p = node;
05898                 
05899                 while (p)
05900                 {
05901                         xml_attribute a = p.find_attribute(pred);
05902                         
05903                         if (a) return a.value();
05904                         
05905                         p = p.parent();
05906                 }
05907                 
05908                 return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
05909         }
05910 
05911         const char_t* namespace_uri(const xml_attribute& attr, const xml_node& parent)
05912         {
05913                 namespace_uri_predicate pred = attr.name();
05914                 
05915                 // Default namespace does not apply to attributes
05916                 if (!pred.prefix) return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
05917                 
05918                 xml_node p = parent;
05919                 
05920                 while (p)
05921                 {
05922                         xml_attribute a = p.find_attribute(pred);
05923                         
05924                         if (a) return a.value();
05925                         
05926                         p = p.parent();
05927                 }
05928                 
05929                 return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
05930         }
05931 
05932         const char_t* namespace_uri(const xpath_node& node)
05933         {
05934                 return node.attribute() ? namespace_uri(node.attribute(), node.parent()) : namespace_uri(node.node());
05935         }
05936 
05937         void normalize_space(char_t* buffer)
05938         {
05939                 char_t* write = buffer;
05940 
05941                 for (char_t* it = buffer; *it; )
05942                 {
05943                         char_t ch = *it++;
05944 
05945                         if (IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
05946                         {
05947                                 // replace whitespace sequence with single space
05948                                 while (IS_CHARTYPE(*it, ct_space)) it++;
05949 
05950                                 // avoid leading spaces
05951                                 if (write != buffer) *write++ = ' ';
05952                         }
05953                         else *write++ = ch;
05954                 }
05955 
05956                 // remove trailing space
05957                 if (write != buffer && IS_CHARTYPE(write[-1], ct_space)) write--;
05958 
05959                 // zero-terminate
05960                 *write = 0;
05961         }
05962 
05963         void translate(char_t* buffer, const char_t* from, const char_t* to)
05964         {
05965                 size_t to_length = strlength(to);
05966 
05967                 char_t* write = buffer;
05968 
05969                 while (*buffer)
05970                 {
05971                         DMC_VOLATILE char_t ch = *buffer++;
05972 
05973                         const char_t* pos = find_char(from, ch);
05974 
05975                         if (!pos)
05976                                 *write++ = ch; // do not process
05977                         else if (static_cast<size_t>(pos - from) < to_length)
05978                                 *write++ = to[pos - from]; // replace
05979                 }
05980 
05981                 // zero-terminate
05982                 *write = 0;
05983         }
05984

06027 
06028         unsigned int hash_string(const char_t* str)
06029         {
06030                 // Jenkins one-at-a-time hash (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jenkins_hash_function#one-at-a-time)
06031                 unsigned int result = 0;
06032 
06033                 while (*str)
06034                 {
06035                         result += static_cast<unsigned int>(*str++);
06036                         result += result << 10;
06037                         result ^= result >> 6;
06038                 }
06039         
06040                 result += result << 3;
06041                 result ^= result >> 11;
06042                 result += result << 15;
06043         
06044                 return result;
06045         }
06046 
06047         template <typename T> T* new_xpath_variable(const char_t* name)
06048         {
06049                 size_t length = strlength(name);
06050                 if (length == 0) return 0; // empty variable names are invalid
06051 
06052                 // $$ we can't use offsetof(T, name) because T is non-POD, so we just allocate additional length characters
06053                 void* memory = global_allocate(sizeof(T) + length * sizeof(char_t));
06054                 if (!memory) return 0;
06055 
06056                 T* result = new (memory) T();
06057 
06058                 memcpy(result->name, name, (length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
06059 
06060                 return result;
06061         }
06062 
06063         xpath_variable* new_xpath_variable(xpath_value_type type, const char_t* name)
06064         {
06065                 switch (type)
06066                 {
06067                 case xpath_type_node_set:
06068                         return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_node_set>(name);
06069 
06070                 case xpath_type_number:
06071                         return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_number>(name);
06072 
06073                 case xpath_type_string:
06074                         return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_string>(name);
06075 
06076                 case xpath_type_boolean:
06077                         return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_boolean>(name);
06078 
06079                 default:
06080                         return 0;
06081                 }
06082         }
06083 
06084         template <typename T> void delete_xpath_variable(T* var)
06085         {
06086                 var->~T();
06087                 global_deallocate(var);
06088         }
06089 
06090         void delete_xpath_variable(xpath_value_type type, xpath_variable* var)
06091         {
06092                 switch (type)
06093                 {
06094                 case xpath_type_node_set:
06095                         delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_node_set*>(var));
06096                         break;
06097 
06098                 case xpath_type_number:
06099                         delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_number*>(var));
06100                         break;
06101 
06102                 case xpath_type_string:
06103                         delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_string*>(var));
06104                         break;
06105 
06106                 case xpath_type_boolean:
06107                         delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_boolean*>(var));
06108                         break;
06109 
06110                 default:
06111                         assert(!"Invalid variable type");
06112                 }
06113         }
06114 
06115         xpath_variable* get_variable(xpath_variable_set* set, const char_t* begin, const char_t* end)
06116         {
06117                 char_t buffer[32];
06118 
06119                 size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
06120                 char_t* scratch = buffer;
06121 
06122                 if (length >= sizeof(buffer) / sizeof(buffer[0]))
06123                 {
06124                         // need to make dummy on-heap copy
06125                         scratch = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
06126                         if (!scratch) return 0;
06127                 }
06128 
06129                 // copy string to zero-terminated buffer and perform lookup
06130                 memcpy(scratch, begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
06131                 scratch[length] = 0;
06132 
06133                 xpath_variable* result = set->get(scratch);
06134 
06135                 // free dummy buffer
06136                 if (scratch != buffer) global_deallocate(scratch);
06137 
06138                 return result;
06139         }
06140 }
06141 
06142 // Internal node set class
06143 namespace
06144 {
06145         xpath_node_set::type_t xpath_sort(xpath_node* begin, xpath_node* end, xpath_node_set::type_t type, bool rev)
06146         {
06147                 xpath_node_set::type_t order = rev ? xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse : xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
06148 
06149                 if (type == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
06150                 {
06151                         sort(begin, end, document_order_comparator());
06152 
06153                         type = xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
06154                 }
06155                 
06156                 if (type != order) reverse(begin, end);
06157                         
06158                 return order;
06159         }
06160 
06161         xpath_node xpath_first(const xpath_node* begin, const xpath_node* end, xpath_node_set::type_t type)
06162         {
06163                 if (begin == end) return xpath_node();
06164 
06165                 switch (type)
06166                 {
06167                 case xpath_node_set::type_sorted:
06168                         return *begin;
06169 
06170                 case xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse:
06171                         return *(end - 1);
06172 
06173                 case xpath_node_set::type_unsorted:
06174                         return *min_element(begin, end, document_order_comparator());
06175 
06176                 default:
06177                         assert(!"Invalid node set type");
06178                         return xpath_node();
06179                 }
06180         }
06181         class xpath_node_set_raw
06182         {
06183                 xpath_node_set::type_t _type;
06184 
06185                 xpath_node* _begin;
06186                 xpath_node* _end;
06187                 xpath_node* _eos;
06188 
06189         public:
06190                 xpath_node_set_raw(): _type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted), _begin(0), _end(0), _eos(0)
06191                 {
06192                 }
06193 
06194                 xpath_node* begin() const
06195                 {
06196                         return _begin;
06197                 }
06198 
06199                 xpath_node* end() const
06200                 {
06201                         return _end;
06202                 }
06203 
06204                 bool empty() const
06205                 {
06206                         return _begin == _end;
06207                 }
06208 
06209                 size_t size() const
06210                 {
06211                         return static_cast<size_t>(_end - _begin);
06212                 }
06213 
06214                 xpath_node first() const
06215                 {
06216                         return xpath_first(_begin, _end, _type);
06217                 }
06218 
06219                 void push_back(const xpath_node& node, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06220                 {
06221                         if (_end == _eos)
06222                         {
06223                                 size_t capacity = static_cast<size_t>(_eos - _begin);
06224 
06225                                 // get new capacity (1.5x rule)
06226                                 size_t new_capacity = capacity + capacity / 2 + 1;
06227 
06228                                 // reallocate the old array or allocate a new one
06229                                 xpath_node* data = static_cast<xpath_node*>(alloc->reallocate(_begin, capacity * sizeof(xpath_node), new_capacity * sizeof(xpath_node)));
06230                                 assert(data);
06231 
06232                                 // finalize
06233                                 _begin = data;
06234                                 _end = data + capacity;
06235                                 _eos = data + new_capacity;
06236                         }
06237 
06238                         *_end++ = node;
06239                 }
06240 
06241                 void append(const xpath_node* begin, const xpath_node* end, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06242                 {
06243                         size_t size = static_cast<size_t>(_end - _begin);
06244                         size_t capacity = static_cast<size_t>(_eos - _begin);
06245                         size_t count = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
06246 
06247                         if (size + count > capacity)
06248                         {
06249                                 // reallocate the old array or allocate a new one
06250                                 xpath_node* data = static_cast<xpath_node*>(alloc->reallocate(_begin, capacity * sizeof(xpath_node), (size + count) * sizeof(xpath_node)));
06251                                 assert(data);
06252 
06253                                 // finalize
06254                                 _begin = data;
06255                                 _end = data + size;
06256                                 _eos = data + size + count;
06257                         }
06258 
06259                         memcpy(_end, begin, count * sizeof(xpath_node));
06260                         _end += count;
06261                 }
06262 
06263                 void sort_do()
06264                 {
06265                         _type = xpath_sort(_begin, _end, _type, false);
06266                 }
06267 
06268                 void truncate(xpath_node* pos)
06269                 {
06270                         assert(_begin <= pos && pos <= _end);
06271 
06272                         _end = pos;
06273                 }
06274 
06275                 void remove_duplicates()
06276                 {
06277                         if (_type == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
06278                                 sort(_begin, _end, duplicate_comparator());
06279                 
06280                         _end = unique(_begin, _end);
06281                 }
06282 
06283                 xpath_node_set::type_t type() const
06284                 {
06285                         return _type;
06286                 }
06287 
06288                 void set_type(xpath_node_set::type_t type)
06289                 {
06290                         _type = type;
06291                 }
06292         };
06293 }

06303                 {
06304                 }

06307         enum lexeme_t
06308         {
06309                 lex_none = 0,
06310                 lex_equal,
06311                 lex_not_equal,
06312                 lex_less,
06313                 lex_greater,
06314                 lex_less_or_equal,
06315                 lex_greater_or_equal,
06316                 lex_plus,
06317                 lex_minus,
06318                 lex_multiply,
06319                 lex_union,
06320                 lex_var_ref,
06321                 lex_open_brace,
06322                 lex_close_brace,
06323                 lex_quoted_string,
06324                 lex_number,
06325                 lex_slash,
06326                 lex_double_slash,
06327                 lex_open_square_brace,
06328                 lex_close_square_brace,
06329                 lex_string,
06330                 lex_comma,
06331                 lex_axis_attribute,
06332                 lex_dot,
06333                 lex_double_dot,
06334                 lex_double_colon,
06335                 lex_eof
06336         };

06338         struct xpath_lexer_string
06339         {
06340                 const char_t* begin;
06341                 const char_t* end;
06342 
06343                 xpath_lexer_string(): begin(0), end(0)
06344                 {
06345                 }
06346 
06347                 bool operator==(const char_t* other) const
06348                 {
06349                         size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
06350 
06351                         return strequalrange(other, begin, length);
06352                 }
06353         };
06354 
06355         class xpath_lexer
06356         {
06357                 const char_t* _cur;
06358                 const char_t* _cur_lexeme_pos;
06359                 xpath_lexer_string _cur_lexeme_contents;
06360 
06361                 lexeme_t _cur_lexeme;
06362 
06363         public:
06364                 explicit xpath_lexer(const char_t* query): _cur(query)
06365                 {
06366                         next();
06367                 }
06368                 
06369                 const char_t* state() const
06370                 {
06371                         return _cur;
06372                 }
06373                 
06374                 void next()
06375                 {
06376                         const char_t* cur = _cur;
06377 
06378                         while (IS_CHARTYPE(*cur, ct_space)) ++cur;
06379
