06380                         // save lexeme position for error reporting
06381                         _cur_lexeme_pos = cur;
06382 
06383                         switch (*cur)
06384                         {
06385                         case 0:
06386                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_eof;
06387                                 break;
06388                         
06389                         case '>':
06390                                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
06391                                 {
06392                                         cur += 2;
06393                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_greater_or_equal;
06394                                 }
06395                                 else
06396                                 {
06397                                         cur += 1;
06398                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_greater;
06399                                 }
06400                                 break;
06401 
06402                         case '<':
06403                                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
06404                                 {
06405                                         cur += 2;
06406                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_less_or_equal;
06407                                 }
06408                                 else
06409                                 {
06410                                         cur += 1;
06411                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_less;
06412                                 }
06413                                 break;
06414 
06415                         case '!':
06416                                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
06417                                 {
06418                                         cur += 2;
06419                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_not_equal;
06420                                 }
06421                                 else
06422                                 {
06423                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
06424                                 }
06425                                 break;
06426 
06427                         case '=':
06428                                 cur += 1;
06429                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_equal;
06430 
06431                                 break;
06432                         
06433                         case '+':
06434                                 cur += 1;
06435                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_plus;
06436 
06437                                 break;
06438 
06439                         case '-':
06440                                 cur += 1;
06441                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_minus;
06442 
06443                                 break;
06444 
06445                         case '*':
06446                                 cur += 1;
06447                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_multiply;
06448 
06449                                 break;
06450 
06451                         case '|':
06452                                 cur += 1;
06453                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_union;
06454 
06455                                 break;
06456                         
06457                         case '$':
06458                                 cur += 1;
06459 
06460                                 if (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_start_symbol))
06461                                 {
06462                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
06463 
06464                                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
06465 
06466                                         if (cur[0] == ':' && IS_CHARTYPEX(cur[1], ctx_symbol)) // qname
06467                                         {
06468                                                 cur++; // :
06469 
06470                                                 while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
06471                                         }
06472 
06473                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
06474                                 
06475                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_var_ref;
06476                                 }
06477                                 else
06478                                 {
06479                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
06480                                 }
06481 
06482                                 break;
06483 
06484                         case '(':
06485                                 cur += 1;
06486                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_open_brace;
06487 
06488                                 break;
06489 
06490                         case ')':
06491                                 cur += 1;
06492                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_close_brace;
06493 
06494                                 break;
06495                         
06496                         case '[':
06497                                 cur += 1;
06498                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_open_square_brace;
06499 
06500                                 break;
06501 
06502                         case ']':
06503                                 cur += 1;
06504                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_close_square_brace;
06505 
06506                                 break;
06507 
06508                         case ',':
06509                                 cur += 1;
06510                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_comma;
06511 
06512                                 break;
06513 
06514                         case '/':
06515                                 if (*(cur+1) == '/')
06516                                 {
06517                                         cur += 2;
06518                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_double_slash;
06519                                 }
06520                                 else
06521                                 {
06522                                         cur += 1;
06523                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_slash;
06524                                 }
06525                                 break;
06526                 
06527                         case '.':
06528                                 if (*(cur+1) == '.')
06529                                 {
06530                                         cur += 2;
06531                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_double_dot;
06532                                 }
06533                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPEX(*(cur+1), ctx_digit))
06534                                 {
06535                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur; // .
06536 
06537                                         ++cur;
06538 
06539                                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
06540 
06541                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
06542                                         
06543                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_number;
06544                                 }
06545                                 else
06546                                 {
06547                                         cur += 1;
06548                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_dot;
06549                                 }
06550                                 break;
06551 
06552                         case '@':
06553                                 cur += 1;
06554                                 _cur_lexeme = lex_axis_attribute;
06555 
06556                                 break;
06557 
06558                         case '"':
06559                         case '\'':
06560                         {
06561                                 char_t terminator = *cur;
06562 
06563                                 ++cur;
06564 
06565                                 _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
06566                                 while (*cur && *cur != terminator) cur++;
06567                                 _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
06568                                 
06569                                 if (!*cur)
06570                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
06571                                 else
06572                                 {
06573                                         cur += 1;
06574                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_quoted_string;
06575                                 }
06576 
06577                                 break;
06578                         }
06579 
06580                         case ':':
06581                                 if (*(cur+1) == ':')
06582                                 {
06583                                         cur += 2;
06584                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_double_colon;
06585                                 }
06586                                 else
06587                                 {
06588                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
06589                                 }
06590                                 break;
06591 
06592                         default:
06593                                 if (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit))
06594                                 {
06595                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
06596 
06597                                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
06598                                 
06599                                         if (*cur == '.')
06600                                         {
06601                                                 cur++;
06602 
06603                                                 while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
06604                                         }
06605 
06606                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
06607 
06608                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_number;
06609                                 }
06610                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_start_symbol))
06611                                 {
06612                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
06613 
06614                                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
06615 
06616                                         if (cur[0] == ':')
06617                                         {
06618                                                 if (cur[1] == '*') // namespace test ncname:*
06619                                                 {
06620                                                         cur += 2; // :*
06621                                                 }
06622                                                 else if (IS_CHARTYPEX(cur[1], ctx_symbol)) // namespace test qname
06623                                                 {
06624                                                         cur++; // :
06625 
06626                                                         while (IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
06627                                                 }
06628                                         }
06629 
06630                                         _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
06631                                 
06632                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_string;
06633                                 }
06634                                 else
06635                                 {
06636                                         _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
06637                                 }
06638                         }
06639 
06640                         _cur = cur;
06641                 }
06642 
06643                 lexeme_t current() const
06644                 {
06645                         return _cur_lexeme;
06646                 }
06647 
06648                 const char_t* current_pos() const
06649                 {
06650                         return _cur_lexeme_pos;
06651                 }
06652 
06653                 const xpath_lexer_string& contents() const
06654                 {
06655                         assert(_cur_lexeme == lex_var_ref || _cur_lexeme == lex_number || _cur_lexeme == lex_string || _cur_lexeme == lex_quoted_string);
06656 
06657                         return _cur_lexeme_contents;
06658                 }
06659         };
06660 
06661         enum ast_type_t
06662         {
06663                 ast_op_or,                                              // left or right
06664                 ast_op_and,                                             // left and right
06665                 ast_op_equal,                                   // left = right
06666                 ast_op_not_equal,                               // left != right
06667                 ast_op_less,                                    // left < right
06668                 ast_op_greater,                                 // left > right
06669                 ast_op_less_or_equal,                   // left <= right
06670                 ast_op_greater_or_equal,                // left >= right
06671                 ast_op_add,                                             // left + right
06672                 ast_op_subtract,                                // left - right
06673                 ast_op_multiply,                                // left * right
06674                 ast_op_divide,                                  // left / right
06675                 ast_op_mod,                                             // left % right
06676                 ast_op_negate,                                  // left - right
06677                 ast_op_union,                                   // left | right
06678                 ast_predicate,                                  // apply predicate to set; next points to next predicate
06679                 ast_filter,                                             // select * from left where right
06680                 ast_filter_posinv,                              // select * from left where right; proximity position invariant
06681                 ast_string_constant,                    // string constant
06682                 ast_number_constant,                    // number constant
06683                 ast_variable,                                   // variable
06684                 ast_func_last,                                  // last()
06685                 ast_func_position,                              // position()
06686                 ast_func_count,                                 // count(left)
06687                 ast_func_id,                                    // id(left)
06688                 ast_func_local_name_0,                  // local-name()
06689                 ast_func_local_name_1,                  // local-name(left)
06690                 ast_func_namespace_uri_0,               // namespace-uri()
06691                 ast_func_namespace_uri_1,               // namespace-uri(left)
06692                 ast_func_name_0,                                // name()
06693                 ast_func_name_1,                                // name(left)
06694                 ast_func_string_0,                              // string()
06695                 ast_func_string_1,                              // string(left)
06696                 ast_func_concat,                                // concat(left, right, siblings)
06697                 ast_func_starts_with,                   // starts_with(left, right)
06698                 ast_func_contains,                              // contains(left, right)
06699                 ast_func_substring_before,              // substring-before(left, right)
06700                 ast_func_substring_after,               // substring-after(left, right)
06701                 ast_func_substring_2,                   // substring(left, right)
06702                 ast_func_substring_3,                   // substring(left, right, third)
06703                 ast_func_string_length_0,               // string-length()
06704                 ast_func_string_length_1,               // string-length(left)
06705                 ast_func_normalize_space_0,             // normalize-space()
06706                 ast_func_normalize_space_1,             // normalize-space(left)
06707                 ast_func_translate,                             // translate(left, right, third)
06708                 ast_func_boolean,                               // boolean(left)
06709                 ast_func_not,                                   // not(left)
06710                 ast_func_true,                                  // true()
06711                 ast_func_false,                                 // false()
06712                 ast_func_lang,                                  // lang(left)
06713                 ast_func_number_0,                              // number()
06714                 ast_func_number_1,                              // number(left)
06715                 ast_func_sum,                                   // sum(left)
06716                 ast_func_floor,                                 // floor(left)
06717                 ast_func_ceiling,                               // ceiling(left)
06718                 ast_func_round,                                 // round(left)
06719                 ast_step,                                               // process set left with step
06720                 ast_step_root                                   // select root node
06721         };
06722 
06723         enum axis_t
06724         {
06725                 axis_ancestor,
06726                 axis_ancestor_or_self,
06727                 axis_attribute,
06728                 axis_child,
06729                 axis_descendant,
06730                 axis_descendant_or_self,
06731                 axis_following,
06732                 axis_following_sibling,
06733                 axis_namespace,
06734                 axis_parent,
06735                 axis_preceding,
06736                 axis_preceding_sibling,
06737                 axis_self
06738         };
06739         
06740         enum nodetest_t
06741         {
06742                 nodetest_none,
06743                 nodetest_name,
06744                 nodetest_type_node,
06745                 nodetest_type_comment,
06746                 nodetest_type_pi,
06747                 nodetest_type_text,
06748                 nodetest_pi,
06749                 nodetest_all,
06750                 nodetest_all_in_namespace
06751         };
06752 
06753         template <axis_t N> struct axis_to_type
06754         {
06755                 static const axis_t axis;
06756         };
06757 
06758         template <axis_t N> const axis_t axis_to_type<N>::axis = N;
06759                 
06760         class xpath_ast_node
06761         {
06762         private:
06763                 // node type
06764                 char _type;
06765                 char _rettype;
06766 
06767                 // for ast_step / ast_predicate
06768                 char _axis;
06769                 char _test;
06770 
06771                 // tree node structure
06772                 xpath_ast_node* _left;
06773                 xpath_ast_node* _right;
06774                 xpath_ast_node* _next;
06775 
06776                 union
06777                 {
06778                         // value for ast_string_constant
06779                         const char_t* string;
06780                         // value for ast_number_constant
06781                         double number;
06782                         // variable for ast_variable
06783                         xpath_variable* variable;
06784                         // node test for ast_step (node name/namespace/node type/pi target)
06785                         const char_t* nodetest;
06786                 } _data;
06787 
06788                 xpath_ast_node(const xpath_ast_node&);
06789                 xpath_ast_node& operator=(const xpath_ast_node&);
06790 
06791                 template <class Comp> static bool compare_eq(xpath_ast_node* lhs, xpath_ast_node* rhs, const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, const Comp& comp)
06792                 {
06793                         xpath_value_type lt = lhs->rettype(), rt = rhs->rettype();
06794 
06795                         if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
06796                         {
06797                                 if (lt == xpath_type_boolean || rt == xpath_type_boolean)
06798                                         return comp(lhs->eval_boolean(c, stack), rhs->eval_boolean(c, stack));
06799                                 else if (lt == xpath_type_number || rt == xpath_type_number)
06800                                         return comp(lhs->eval_number(c, stack), rhs->eval_number(c, stack));
06801                                 else if (lt == xpath_type_string || rt == xpath_type_string)
06802                                 {
06803                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06804 
06805                                         xpath_string ls = lhs->eval_string(c, stack);
06806                                         xpath_string rs = rhs->eval_string(c, stack);
06807 
06808                                         return comp(ls, rs);
06809                                 }
06810                         }
06811                         else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
06812                         {
06813                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06814 
06815                                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06816                                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06817 
06818                                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
06819                                         for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
06820                                         {
06821                                                 xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06822 
06823                                                 if (comp(string_value(*li, stack.result), string_value(*ri, stack.result)))
06824                                                         return true;
06825                                         }
06826 
06827                                 return false;
06828                         }
06829                         else
06830                         {
06831                                 if (lt == xpath_type_node_set)
06832                                 {
06833                                         swap(lhs, rhs);
06834                                         swap(lt, rt);
06835                                 }
06836 
06837                                 if (lt == xpath_type_boolean)
06838                                         return comp(lhs->eval_boolean(c, stack), rhs->eval_boolean(c, stack));
06839                                 else if (lt == xpath_type_number)
06840                                 {
06841                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06842 
06843                                         double l = lhs->eval_number(c, stack);
06844                                         xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06845 
06846                                         for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
06847                                         {
06848                                                 xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06849 
06850                                                 if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
06851                                                         return true;
06852                                         }
06853 
06854                                         return false;
06855                                 }
06856                                 else if (lt == xpath_type_string)
06857                                 {
06858                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06859 
06860                                         xpath_string l = lhs->eval_string(c, stack);
06861                                         xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06862 
06863                                         for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
06864                                         {
06865                                                 xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06866 
06867                                                 if (comp(l, string_value(*ri, stack.result)))
06868                                                         return true;
06869                                         }
06870 
06871                                         return false;
06872                                 }
06873                         }
06874 
06875                         assert(!"Wrong types");
06876                         return false;
06877                 }
06878 
06879                 template <class Comp> static bool compare_rel(xpath_ast_node* lhs, xpath_ast_node* rhs, const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, const Comp& comp)
06880                 {
06881                         xpath_value_type lt = lhs->rettype(), rt = rhs->rettype();
06882 
06883                         if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
06884                                 return comp(lhs->eval_number(c, stack), rhs->eval_number(c, stack));
06885                         else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
06886                         {
06887                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06888 
06889                                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06890                                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06891 
06892                                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
06893                                 {
06894                                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06895 
06896                                         double l = convert_string_to_number(string_value(*li, stack.result).c_str());
06897 
06898                                         for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
06899                                         {
06900                                                 xpath_allocator_capture crii(stack.result);
06901 
06902                                                 if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
06903                                                         return true;
06904                                         }
06905                                 }
06906 
06907                                 return false;
06908                         }
06909                         else if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
06910                         {
06911                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06912 
06913                                 double l = lhs->eval_number(c, stack);
06914                                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06915 
06916                                 for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
06917                                 {
06918                                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06919 
06920                                         if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
06921                                                 return true;
06922                                 }
06923 
06924                                 return false;
06925                         }
06926                         else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
06927                         {
06928                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
06929 
06930                                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack);
06931                                 double r = rhs->eval_number(c, stack);
06932 
06933                                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
06934                                 {
06935                                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
06936 
06937                                         if (comp(convert_string_to_number(string_value(*li, stack.result).c_str()), r))
06938                                                 return true;
06939                                 }
06940 
06941                                 return false;
06942                         }
06943                         else
06944                         {
06945                                 assert(!"Wrong types");
06946                                 return false;
06947                         }
06948                 }
06949 
06950                 void apply_predicate(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, xpath_ast_node* expr, const xpath_stack& stack)
06951                 {
06952                         assert(ns.size() >= first);
06953 
06954                         size_t i = 1;
06955                         size_t size = ns.size() - first;
06956                                 
06957                         xpath_node* last = ns.begin() + first;
06958                                 
06959                         // remove_if... or well, sort of
06960                         for (xpath_node* it = last; it != ns.end(); ++it, ++i)
06961                         {
06962                                 xpath_context c(*it, i, size);
06963                         
06964                                 if (expr->rettype() == xpath_type_number)
06965                                 {
06966                                         if (expr->eval_number(c, stack) == i)
06967                                                 *last++ = *it;
06968                                 }
06969                                 else if (expr->eval_boolean(c, stack))
06970                                         *last++ = *it;
06971                         }
06972                         
06973                         ns.truncate(last);
06974                 }
06975 
06976                 void apply_predicates(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, const xpath_stack& stack)
06977                 {
06978                         if (ns.size() == first) return;
06979                         
06980                         for (xpath_ast_node* pred = _right; pred; pred = pred->_next)
06981                         {
06982                                 apply_predicate(ns, first, pred->_left, stack);
06983                         }
06984                 }
06985 
06986                 void step_push(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, const xml_attribute& a, const xml_node& parent, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06987                 {
06988                         if (!a) return;
06989 
06990                         const char_t* name = a.name();
06991 
06992                         // There are no attribute nodes corresponding to attributes that declare namespaces
06993                         // That is, "xmlns:..." or "xmlns"
06994                         if (starts_with(name, PUGIXML_TEXT("xmlns")) && (name[5] == 0 || name[5] == ':')) return;
06995                         
06996                         switch (_test)
06997                         {
06998                         case nodetest_name:
06999                                 if (strequal(name, _data.nodetest)) ns.push_back(xpath_node(a, parent), alloc);
07000                                 break;
07001                                 
07002                         case nodetest_type_node:
07003                         case nodetest_all:
07004                                 ns.push_back(xpath_node(a, parent), alloc);
07005                                 break;
07006                                 
07007                         case nodetest_all_in_namespace:
07008                                 if (starts_with(name, _data.nodetest))
07009                                         ns.push_back(xpath_node(a, parent), alloc);
07010                                 break;
07011                         
07012                         default:
07013                                 ;
07014                         }
07015                 }
07016                 
07017                 void step_push(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, const xml_node& n, xpath_allocator* alloc)
07018                 {
07019                         if (!n) return;
07020 
07021                         switch (_test)
07022                         {
07023                         case nodetest_name:
07024                                 if (n.type() == node_element && strequal(n.name(), _data.nodetest)) ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07025                                 break;
07026                                 
07027                         case nodetest_type_node:
07028                                 ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07029                                 break;
07030                                 
07031                         case nodetest_type_comment:
07032                                 if (n.type() == node_comment)
07033                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07034                                 break;
07035                                 
07036                         case nodetest_type_text:
07037                                 if (n.type() == node_pcdata || n.type() == node_cdata)
07038                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07039                                 break;
07040                                 
07041                         case nodetest_type_pi:
07042                                 if (n.type() == node_pi)
07043                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07044                                 break;
07045                                                                         
07046                         case nodetest_pi:
07047                                 if (n.type() == node_pi && strequal(n.name(), _data.nodetest))
07048                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07049                                 break;
07050                                 
07051                         case nodetest_all:
07052                                 if (n.type() == node_element)
07053                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07054                                 break;
07055                                 
07056                         case nodetest_all_in_namespace:
07057                                 if (n.type() == node_element && starts_with(n.name(), _data.nodetest))
07058                                         ns.push_back(n, alloc);
07059                                 break;
07060 
07061                         default:
07062                                 assert(!"Unknown axis");
07063                         } 
07064                 }
07065 
07066                 template <class T> void step_fill(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, const xml_node& n, xpath_allocator* alloc, T)
07067                 {
07068                         const axis_t axis = T::axis;
07069 
07070                         switch (axis)
07071                         {
07072                         case axis_attribute:
07073                         {
07074                                 for (xml_attribute a = n.first_attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
07075                                         step_push(ns, a, n, alloc);
07076                                 
07077                                 break;
07078                         }
07079                         
07080                         case axis_child:
07081                         {
07082                                 for (xml_node c = n.first_child(); c; c = c.next_sibling())
07083                                         step_push(ns, c, alloc);
07084                                         
07085                                 break;
07086                         }
07087                         
07088                         case axis_descendant:
07089                         case axis_descendant_or_self:
07090                         {
07091                                 if (axis == axis_descendant_or_self)
07092                                         step_push(ns, n, alloc);
07093                                         
07094                                 xml_node cur = n.first_child();
07095                                 
07096                                 while (cur && cur != n)
07097                                 {
07098                                         step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07099                                         
07100                                         if (cur.first_child())
07101                                                 cur = cur.first_child();
07102                                         else if (cur.next_sibling())
07103                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07104                                         else
07105                                         {
07106                                                 while (!cur.next_sibling() && cur != n)
07107                                                         cur = cur.parent();
07108                                         
07109                                                 if (cur != n) cur = cur.next_sibling();
07110                                         }
07111                                 }
07112                                 
07113                                 break;
07114                         }
07115                         
07116                         case axis_following_sibling:
07117                         {
07118                                 for (xml_node c = n.next_sibling(); c; c = c.next_sibling())
07119                                         step_push(ns, c, alloc);
07120                                 
07121                                 break;
07122                         }
07123                         
07124                         case axis_preceding_sibling:
07125                         {
07126                                 for (xml_node c = n.previous_sibling(); c; c = c.previous_sibling())
07127                                         step_push(ns, c, alloc);
07128                                 
07129                                 break;
07130                         }
07131                         
07132                         case axis_following:
07133                         {
07134                                 xml_node cur = n;
07135 
07136                                 // exit from this node so that we don't include descendants
07137                                 while (cur && !cur.next_sibling()) cur = cur.parent();
07138                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07139 
07140                                 for (;;)
07141                                 {
07142                                         step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07143 
07144                                         if (cur.first_child())
07145                                                 cur = cur.first_child();
07146                                         else if (cur.next_sibling())
07147                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07148                                         else
07149                                         {
07150                                                 while (cur && !cur.next_sibling()) cur = cur.parent();
07151                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07152 
07153                                                 if (!cur) break;
07154                                         }
07155                                 }
07156 
07157                                 break;
07158                         }
07159 
07160                         case axis_preceding:
07161                         {
07162                                 xml_node cur = n;
07163 
07164                                 while (cur && !cur.previous_sibling()) cur = cur.parent();
07165                                 cur = cur.previous_sibling();
07166 
07167                                 for (;;)
07168                                 {
07169                                         if (cur.last_child())
07170                                                 cur = cur.last_child();
07171                                         else
07172                                         {
07173                                                 // leaf node, can't be ancestor
07174                                                 step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07175 
07176                                                 if (cur.previous_sibling())
07177                                                         cur = cur.previous_sibling();
07178                                                 else
07179                                                 {
07180                                                         do 
07181                                                         {
07182                                                                 cur = cur.parent();
07183                                                                 if (!cur) break;
07184 
07185                                                                 if (!node_is_ancestor(cur, n)) step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07186                                                         }
07187                                                         while (!cur.previous_sibling());
07188 
07189                                                         cur = cur.previous_sibling();
07190 
07191                                                         if (!cur) break;
07192                                                 }
07193                                         }
07194                                 }
07195 
07196                                 break;
07197                         }
07198                         
07199                         case axis_ancestor:
07200                         case axis_ancestor_or_self:
07201                         {
07202                                 if (axis == axis_ancestor_or_self)
07203                                         step_push(ns, n, alloc);
07204 
07205                                 xml_node cur = n.parent();
07206                                 
07207                                 while (cur)
07208                                 {
07209                                         step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07210                                         
07211                                         cur = cur.parent();
07212                                 }
07213                                 
07214                                 break;
07215                         }
07216 
07217                         case axis_self:
07218                         {
07219                                 step_push(ns, n, alloc);
07220 
07221                                 break;
07222                         }
07223 
07224                         case axis_parent:
07225                         {
07226                                 if (n.parent()) step_push(ns, n.parent(), alloc);
07227 
07228                                 break;
07229                         }
07230                                 
07231                         default:
07232                                 assert(!"Unimplemented axis");
07233                         }
07234                 }
07235                 
07236                 template <class T> void step_fill(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, const xml_attribute& a, const xml_node& p, xpath_allocator* alloc, T v)
07237                 {
07238                         const axis_t axis = T::axis;
07239 
07240                         switch (axis)
07241                         {
07242                         case axis_ancestor:
07243                         case axis_ancestor_or_self:
07244                         {
07245                                 if (axis == axis_ancestor_or_self && _test == nodetest_type_node) // reject attributes based on principal node type test
07246                                         step_push(ns, a, p, alloc);
07247 
07248                                 xml_node cur = p;
07249                                 
07250                                 while (cur)
07251                                 {
07252                                         step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07253                                         
07254                                         cur = cur.parent();
07255                                 }
07256                                 
07257                                 break;
07258                         }
07259 
07260                         case axis_descendant_or_self:
07261                         case axis_self:
07262                         {
07263                                 if (_test == nodetest_type_node) // reject attributes based on principal node type test
07264                                         step_push(ns, a, p, alloc);
07265 
07266                                 break;
07267                         }
07268 
07269                         case axis_following:
07270                         {
07271                                 xml_node cur = p;
07272                                 
07273                                 for (;;)
07274                                 {
07275                                         if (cur.first_child())
07276                                                 cur = cur.first_child();
07277                                         else if (cur.next_sibling())
07278                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07279                                         else
07280                                         {
07281                                                 while (cur && !cur.next_sibling()) cur = cur.parent();
07282                                                 cur = cur.next_sibling();
07283                                                 
07284                                                 if (!cur) break;
07285                                         }
07286 
07287                                         step_push(ns, cur, alloc);
07288                                 }
07289 
07290                                 break;
07291                         }
07292 
07293                         case axis_parent:
07294                         {
07295                                 step_push(ns, p, alloc);
07296 
07297                                 break;
07298                         }
07299 
07300                         case axis_preceding:
07301                         {
07302                                 // preceding:: axis does not include attribute nodes and attribute ancestors (they are the same as parent's ancestors), so we can reuse node preceding
07303                                 step_fill(ns, p, alloc, v);
07304                                 break;
07305                         }
07306                         
07307                         default:
07308                                 assert(!"Unimplemented axis");
07309                         }
07310                 }
07311                 
07312                 template <class T> xpath_node_set_raw step_do(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, T v)
07313                 {
07314                         const axis_t axis = T::axis;
07315                         bool attributes = (axis == axis_ancestor || axis == axis_ancestor_or_self || axis == axis_descendant_or_self || axis == axis_following || axis == axis_parent || axis == axis_preceding || axis == axis_self);
07316 
07317                         xpath_node_set_raw ns;
07318                         ns.set_type((axis == axis_ancestor || axis == axis_ancestor_or_self || axis == axis_preceding || axis == axis_preceding_sibling) ? xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse : xpath_node_set::type_sorted);
07319 
07320                         if (_left)
07321                         {
07322                                 xpath_node_set_raw s = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07323 
07324                                 // self axis preserves the original order
07325                                 if (axis == axis_self) ns.set_type(s.type());
07326 
07327                                 for (const xpath_node* it = s.begin(); it != s.end(); ++it)
07328                                 {
07329                                         size_t size = ns.size();
07330 
07331                                         // in general, all axes generate elements in a particular order, but there is no order guarantee if axis is applied to two nodes
07332                                         if (axis != axis_self && size != 0) ns.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted);
07333                                         
07334                                         if (it->node())
07335                                                 step_fill(ns, it->node(), stack.result, v);
07336                                         else if (attributes)
07337                                                 step_fill(ns, it->attribute(), it->parent(), stack.result, v);
07338                                                 
07339                                         apply_predicates(ns, size, stack);
07340                                 }
07341                         }
07342                         else
07343                         {
07344                                 if (c.n.node())
07345                                         step_fill(ns, c.n.node(), stack.result, v);
07346                                 else if (attributes)
07347                                         step_fill(ns, c.n.attribute(), c.n.parent(), stack.result, v);
07348                                 
07349                                 apply_predicates(ns, 0, stack);
07350                         }
07351 
07352                         // child, attribute and self axes always generate unique set of nodes
07353                         // for other axis, if the set stayed sorted, it stayed unique because the traversal algorithms do not visit the same node twice
07354                         if (axis != axis_child && axis != axis_attribute && axis != axis_self && ns.type() == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
07355                                 ns.remove_duplicates();
07356 
07357                         return ns;
07358                 }
07359                 
07360         public:
07361                 xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype, const char_t* value):
07362                         _type((char)type), _rettype((char)rettype), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
07363                 {
07364                         assert(type == ast_string_constant);
07365                         _data.string = value;
07366                 }
07367 
07368                 xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype, double value):
07369                         _type((char)type), _rettype((char)rettype), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
07370                 {
07371                         assert(type == ast_number_constant);
07372                         _data.number = value;
07373                 }
07374                 
07375                 xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype, xpath_variable* value):
07376                         _type((char)type), _rettype((char)rettype), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
07377                 {
07378                         assert(type == ast_variable);
07379                         _data.variable = value;
07380                 }
07381                 
07382                 xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype, xpath_ast_node* left = 0, xpath_ast_node* right = 0):
07383                         _type((char)type), _rettype((char)rettype), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(left), _right(right), _next(0)
07384                 {
07385                 }
07386 
07387                 xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_ast_node* left, axis_t axis, nodetest_t test, const char_t* contents):
07388                         _type((char)type), _rettype(xpath_type_node_set), _axis((char)axis), _test((char)test), _left(left), _right(0), _next(0)
07389                 {
07390                         _data.nodetest = contents;
07391                 }
07392 
07393                 void set_next(xpath_ast_node* value)
07394                 {
07395                         _next = value;
07396                 }
07397 
07398                 void set_right(xpath_ast_node* value)
07399                 {
07400                         _right = value;
07401                 }
07402 
07403                 bool eval_boolean(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
07404                 {
07405                         switch (_type)
07406                         {
07407                         case ast_op_or:
07408                                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack) || _right->eval_boolean(c, stack);
07409                                 
07410                         case ast_op_and:
07411                                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack) && _right->eval_boolean(c, stack);
07412                                 
07413                         case ast_op_equal:
07414                                 return compare_eq(_left, _right, c, stack, equal_to());
07415 
07416                         case ast_op_not_equal:
07417                                 return compare_eq(_left, _right, c, stack, not_equal_to());
07418         
07419                         case ast_op_less:
07420                                 return compare_rel(_left, _right, c, stack, less());
07421                         
07422                         case ast_op_greater:
07423                                 return compare_rel(_right, _left, c, stack, less());
07424 
07425                         case ast_op_less_or_equal:
07426                                 return compare_rel(_left, _right, c, stack, less_equal());
07427                         
07428                         case ast_op_greater_or_equal:
07429                                 return compare_rel(_right, _left, c, stack, less_equal());
07430 
07431                         case ast_func_starts_with:
07432                         {
07433                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07434 
07435                                 xpath_string lr = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07436                                 xpath_string rr = _right->eval_string(c, stack);
07437 
07438                                 return starts_with(lr.c_str(), rr.c_str());
07439                         }
07440 
07441                         case ast_func_contains:
07442                         {
07443                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07444 
07445                                 xpath_string lr = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07446                                 xpath_string rr = _right->eval_string(c, stack);
07447 
07448                                 return find_substring(lr.c_str(), rr.c_str()) != 0;
07449                         }
07450 
07451                         case ast_func_boolean:
07452                                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack);
07453                                 
07454                         case ast_func_not:
07455                                 return !_left->eval_boolean(c, stack);
07456                                 
07457                         case ast_func_true:
07458                                 return true;
07459                                 
07460                         case ast_func_false:
07461                                 return false;
07462 
07463                         case ast_func_lang:
07464                         {
07465                                 if (c.n.attribute()) return false;
07466                                 
07467                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07468 
07469                                 xpath_string lang = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07470                                 
07471                                 for (xml_node n = c.n.node(); n; n = n.parent())
07472                                 {
07473                                         xml_attribute a = n.attribute(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml:lang"));
07474                                         
07475                                         if (a)
07476                                         {
07477                                                 const char_t* value = a.value();
07478                                                 
07479                                                 // strnicmp / strncasecmp is not portable
07480                                                 for (const char_t* lit = lang.c_str(); *lit; ++lit)
07481                                                 {
07482                                                         if (tolower_ascii(*lit) != tolower_ascii(*value)) return false;
07483                                                         ++value;
07484                                                 }
07485                                                 
07486                                                 return *value == 0 || *value == '-';
07487                                         }
07488                                 }
07489                                 
07490                                 return false;
07491                         }
07492 
07493                         case ast_variable:
07494                         {
07495                                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
07496 
07497                                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_boolean)
07498                                         return _data.variable->get_boolean();
07499 
07500                                 // fallthrough to type conversion
07501                         }
07502 
07503                         default:
07504                         {
07505                                 switch (_rettype)
07506                                 {
07507                                 case xpath_type_number:
07508                                         return convert_number_to_boolean(eval_number(c, stack));
07509                                         
07510                                 case xpath_type_string:
07511                                 {
07512                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07513 
07514                                         return !eval_string(c, stack).empty();
07515                                 }
07516                                         
07517                                 case xpath_type_node_set:                               
07518                                 {
07519                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07520 
07521                                         return !eval_node_set(c, stack).empty();
07522                                 }
07523 
07524                                 default:
07525                                         assert(!"Wrong expression for return type boolean");
07526                                         return false;
07527                                 }
07528                         }
07529                         }
07530                 }
07531 
07532                 double eval_number(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
07533                 {
07534                         switch (_type)
07535                         {
07536                         case ast_op_add:
07537                                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) + _right->eval_number(c, stack);
07538                                 
07539                         case ast_op_subtract:
07540                                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) - _right->eval_number(c, stack);
07541 
07542                         case ast_op_multiply:
07543                                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) * _right->eval_number(c, stack);
07544 
07545                         case ast_op_divide:
07546                                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) / _right->eval_number(c, stack);
07547 
07548                         case ast_op_mod:
07549                                 return fmod(_left->eval_number(c, stack), _right->eval_number(c, stack));
07550 
07551                         case ast_op_negate:
07552                                 return -_left->eval_number(c, stack);
07553 
07554                         case ast_number_constant:
07555                                 return _data.number;
07556 
07557                         case ast_func_last:
07558                                 return (double)c.size;
07559                         
07560                         case ast_func_position:
07561                                 return (double)c.position;
07562 
07563                         case ast_func_count:
07564                         {
07565                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07566 
07567                                 return (double)_left->eval_node_set(c, stack).size();
07568                         }
07569                         
07570                         case ast_func_string_length_0:
07571                         {
07572                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07573 
07574                                 return (double)string_value(c.n, stack.result).length();
07575                         }
07576                         
07577                         case ast_func_string_length_1:
07578                         {
07579                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07580 
07581                                 return (double)_left->eval_string(c, stack).length();
07582                         }
07583                         
07584                         case ast_func_number_0:
07585                         {
07586                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07587 
07588                                 return convert_string_to_number(string_value(c.n, stack.result).c_str());
07589                         }
07590                         
07591                         case ast_func_number_1:
07592                                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack);
07593 
07594                         case ast_func_sum:
07595                         {
07596                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07597 
07598                                 double r = 0;
07599                                 
07600                                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07601                                 
07602                                 for (const xpath_node* it = ns.begin(); it != ns.end(); ++it)
07603                                 {
07604                                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
07605 
07606                                         r += convert_string_to_number(string_value(*it, stack.result).c_str());
07607                                 }
07608                         
07609                                 return r;
07610                         }
07611 
07612                         case ast_func_floor:
07613                         {
07614                                 double r = _left->eval_number(c, stack);
07615                                 
07616                                 return r == r ? floor(r) : r;
07617                         }
07618 
07619                         case ast_func_ceiling:
07620                         {
07621                                 double r = _left->eval_number(c, stack);
07622                                 
07623                                 return r == r ? ceil(r) : r;
07624                         }
07625 
07626                         case ast_func_round:
07627                                 return round_nearest_nzero(_left->eval_number(c, stack));
07628                         
07629                         case ast_variable:
07630                         {
07631                                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
07632 
07633                                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_number)
07634                                         return _data.variable->get_number();
07635 
07636                                 // fallthrough to type conversion
07637                         }
07638 
07639                         default:
07640                         {
07641                                 switch (_rettype)
07642                                 {
07643                                 case xpath_type_boolean:
07644                                         return eval_boolean(c, stack) ? 1 : 0;
07645                                         
07646                                 case xpath_type_string:
07647                                 {
07648                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07649 
07650                                         return convert_string_to_number(eval_string(c, stack).c_str());
07651                                 }
07652                                         
07653                                 case xpath_type_node_set:
07654                                 {
07655                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07656 
07657                                         return convert_string_to_number(eval_string(c, stack).c_str());
07658                                 }
07659                                         
07660                                 default:
07661                                         assert(!"Wrong expression for return type number");
07662                                         return 0;
07663                                 }
07664                                 
07665                         }
07666                         }
07667                 }
07668                 
07669                 xpath_string eval_string_concat(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
07670                 {
07671                         assert(_type == ast_func_concat);
07672 
07673                         xpath_allocator_capture ct(stack.temp);
07674 
07675                         // count the string number
07676                         size_t count = 1;
07677                         for (xpath_ast_node* nc = _right; nc; nc = nc->_next) count++;
07678 
07679                         // gather all strings
07680                         xpath_string static_buffer[4];
07681                         xpath_string* buffer = static_buffer;
07682 
07683                         // allocate on-heap for large concats
07684                         if (count > sizeof(static_buffer) / sizeof(static_buffer[0]))
07685                         {
07686                                 buffer = static_cast<xpath_string*>(stack.temp->allocate(count * sizeof(xpath_string)));
07687                                 assert(buffer);
07688                         }
07689 
07690                         // evaluate all strings to temporary stack
07691                         xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07692 
07693                         buffer[0] = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07694 
07695                         size_t pos = 1;
07696                         for (xpath_ast_node* n = _right; n; n = n->_next, ++pos) buffer[pos] = n->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07697                         assert(pos == count);
07698 
07699                         // get total length
07700                         size_t length = 0;
07701                         for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) length += buffer[i].length();
07702 
07703                         // create final string
07704                         char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(stack.result->allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
07705                         assert(result);
07706 
07707                         char_t* ri = result;
07708 
07709                         for (size_t j = 0; j < count; ++j)
07710                                 for (const char_t* bi = buffer[j].c_str(); *bi; ++bi)
07711                                         *ri++ = *bi;
07712 
07713                         *ri = 0;
07714 
07715                         return xpath_string(result, true);
07716                 }
07717 
07718                 xpath_string eval_string(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
07719                 {
07720                         switch (_type)
07721                         {
07722                         case ast_string_constant:
07723                                 return xpath_string_const(_data.string);
07724                         
07725                         case ast_func_local_name_0:
07726                         {
07727                                 xpath_node na = c.n;
07728                                 
07729                                 return xpath_string_const(local_name(na));
07730                         }
07731 
07732                         case ast_func_local_name_1:
07733                         {
07734                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07735 
07736                                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07737                                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
07738                                 
07739                                 return xpath_string_const(local_name(na));
07740                         }
07741 
07742                         case ast_func_name_0:
07743                         {
07744                                 xpath_node na = c.n;
07745                                 
07746                                 return xpath_string_const(qualified_name(na));
07747                         }
07748 
07749                         case ast_func_name_1:
07750                         {
07751                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07752 
07753                                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07754                                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
07755                                 
07756                                 return xpath_string_const(qualified_name(na));
07757                         }
07758 
07759                         case ast_func_namespace_uri_0:
07760                         {
07761                                 xpath_node na = c.n;
07762                                 
07763                                 return xpath_string_const(namespace_uri(na));
07764                         }
07765 
07766                         case ast_func_namespace_uri_1:
07767                         {
07768                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
07769 
07770                                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07771                                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
07772                                 
07773                                 return xpath_string_const(namespace_uri(na));
07774                         }
07775 
07776                         case ast_func_string_0:
07777                                 return string_value(c.n, stack.result);
07778 
07779                         case ast_func_string_1:
07780                                 return _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07781 
07782                         case ast_func_concat:
07783                                 return eval_string_concat(c, stack);
07784 
07785                         case ast_func_substring_before:
07786                         {
07787                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07788 
07789                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07790 
07791                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07792                                 xpath_string p = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07793 
07794                                 const char_t* pos = find_substring(s.c_str(), p.c_str());
07795                                 
07796                                 return pos ? xpath_string(s.c_str(), pos, stack.result) : xpath_string();
07797                         }
07798                         
07799                         case ast_func_substring_after:
07800                         {
07801                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07802 
07803                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07804 
07805                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07806                                 xpath_string p = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07807                                 
07808                                 const char_t* pos = find_substring(s.c_str(), p.c_str());
07809                                 if (!pos) return xpath_string();
07810 
07811                                 const char_t* result = pos + p.length();
07812 
07813                                 return s.uses_heap() ? xpath_string(result, stack.result) : xpath_string_const(result);
07814                         }
07815 
07816                         case ast_func_substring_2:
07817                         {
07818                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07819 
07820                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07821 
07822                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07823                                 size_t s_length = s.length();
07824 
07825                                 double first = round_nearest(_right->eval_number(c, stack));
07826                                 
07827                                 if (is_nan(first)) return xpath_string(); // NaN
07828                                 else if (first >= s_length + 1) return xpath_string();
07829                                 
07830                                 size_t pos = first < 1 ? 1 : (size_t)first;
07831                                 assert(1 <= pos && pos <= s_length + 1);
07832 
07833                                 const char_t* rbegin = s.c_str() + (pos - 1);
07834                                 
07835                                 return s.uses_heap() ? xpath_string(rbegin, stack.result) : xpath_string_const(rbegin);
07836                         }
07837                         
07838                         case ast_func_substring_3:
07839                         {
07840                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07841 
07842                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07843 
07844                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07845                                 size_t s_length = s.length();
07846 
07847                                 double first = round_nearest(_right->eval_number(c, stack));
07848                                 double last = first + round_nearest(_right->_next->eval_number(c, stack));
07849                                 
07850                                 if (is_nan(first) || is_nan(last)) return xpath_string();
07851                                 else if (first >= s_length + 1) return xpath_string();
07852                                 else if (first >= last) return xpath_string();
07853                                 else if (last < 1) return xpath_string();
07854                                 
07855                                 size_t pos = first < 1 ? 1 : (size_t)first;
07856                                 size_t end = last >= s_length + 1 ? s_length + 1 : (size_t)last;
07857 
07858                                 assert(1 <= pos && pos <= end && end <= s_length + 1);
07859                                 const char_t* rbegin = s.c_str() + (pos - 1);
07860                                 const char_t* rend = s.c_str() + (end - 1);
07861 
07862                                 return (end == s_length + 1 && !s.uses_heap()) ? xpath_string_const(rbegin) : xpath_string(rbegin, rend, stack.result);
07863                         }
07864 
07865                         case ast_func_normalize_space_0:
07866                         {
07867                                 xpath_string s = string_value(c.n, stack.result);
07868 
07869                                 normalize_space(s.data(stack.result));
07870 
07871                                 return s;
07872                         }
07873 
07874                         case ast_func_normalize_space_1:
07875                         {
07876                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07877 
07878                                 normalize_space(s.data(stack.result));
07879                         
07880                                 return s;
07881                         }
07882 
07883                         case ast_func_translate:
07884                         {
07885                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07886 
07887                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07888 
07889                                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
07890                                 xpath_string from = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07891                                 xpath_string to = _right->_next->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
07892 
07893                                 translate(s.data(stack.result), from.c_str(), to.c_str());
07894 
07895                                 return s;
07896                         }
07897 
07898                         case ast_variable:
07899                         {
07900                                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
07901 
07902                                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_string)
07903                                         return xpath_string_const(_data.variable->get_string());
07904 
07905                                 // fallthrough to type conversion
07906                         }
07907 
07908                         default:
07909                         {
07910                                 switch (_rettype)
07911                                 {
07912                                 case xpath_type_boolean:
07913                                         return xpath_string_const(eval_boolean(c, stack) ? PUGIXML_TEXT("true") : PUGIXML_TEXT("false"));
