07914                                         
07915                                 case xpath_type_number:
07916                                         return convert_number_to_string(eval_number(c, stack), stack.result);
07917                                         
07918                                 case xpath_type_node_set:
07919                                 {
07920                                         xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07921 
07922                                         xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07923 
07924                                         xpath_node_set_raw ns = eval_node_set(c, swapped_stack);
07925                                         return ns.empty() ? xpath_string() : string_value(ns.first(), stack.result);
07926                                 }
07927                                 
07928                                 default:
07929                                         assert(!"Wrong expression for return type string");
07930                                         return xpath_string();
07931                                 }
07932                         }
07933                         }
07934                 }
07935 
07936                 xpath_node_set_raw eval_node_set(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
07937                 {
07938                         switch (_type)
07939                         {
07940                         case ast_op_union:
07941                         {
07942                                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
07943 
07944                                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
07945 
07946                                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = _left->eval_node_set(c, swapped_stack);
07947                                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = _right->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07948                                 
07949                                 // we can optimize merging two sorted sets, but this is a very rare operation, so don't bother
07950                         rs.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted);
07951 
07952                                 rs.append(ls.begin(), ls.end(), stack.result);
07953                                 rs.remove_duplicates();
07954                                 
07955                                 return rs;
07956                         }
07957 
07958                         case ast_filter:
07959                         case ast_filter_posinv:
07960                         {
07961                                 xpath_node_set_raw set = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack);
07962 
07963                                 // either expression is a number or it contains position() call; sort by document order
07964                                 if (_type == ast_filter) set.sort_do();
07965 
07966                                 apply_predicate(set, 0, _right, stack);
07967                         
07968                                 return set;
07969                         }
07970                         
07971                         case ast_func_id:
07972                                 return xpath_node_set_raw();
07973                         
07974                         case ast_step:
07975                         {
07976                                 switch (_axis)
07977                                 {
07978                                 case axis_ancestor:
07979                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_ancestor>());
07980                                         
07981                                 case axis_ancestor_or_self:
07982                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_ancestor_or_self>());
07983 
07984                                 case axis_attribute:
07985                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_attribute>());
07986 
07987                                 case axis_child:
07988                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_child>());
07989                                 
07990                                 case axis_descendant:
07991                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_descendant>());
07992 
07993                                 case axis_descendant_or_self:
07994                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_descendant_or_self>());
07995 
07996                                 case axis_following:
07997                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_following>());
07998                                 
07999                                 case axis_following_sibling:
08000                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_following_sibling>());
08001                                 
08002                                 case axis_namespace:
08003                                         // namespaced axis is not supported
08004                                         return xpath_node_set_raw();
08005                                 
08006                                 case axis_parent:
08007                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_parent>());
08008                                 
08009                                 case axis_preceding:
08010                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_preceding>());
08011 
08012                                 case axis_preceding_sibling:
08013                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_preceding_sibling>());
08014                                 
08015                                 case axis_self:
08016                                         return step_do(c, stack, axis_to_type<axis_self>());
08017                                 }
08018                         }
08019 
08020                         case ast_step_root:
08021                         {
08022                                 assert(!_right); // root step can't have any predicates
08023 
08024                                 xpath_node_set_raw ns;
08025 
08026                                 ns.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_sorted);
08027 
08028                                 if (c.n.node()) ns.push_back(c.n.node().root(), stack.result);
08029                                 else if (c.n.attribute()) ns.push_back(c.n.parent().root(), stack.result);
08030 
08031                                 return ns;
08032                         }
08033 
08034                         case ast_variable:
08035                         {
08036                                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
08037 
08038                                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_node_set)
08039                                 {
08040                                         const xpath_node_set& s = _data.variable->get_node_set();
08041 
08042                                         xpath_node_set_raw ns;
08043 
08044                                         ns.set_type(s.type());
08045                                         ns.append(s.begin(), s.end(), stack.result);
08046 
08047                                         return ns;
08048                                 }
08049 
08050                                 // fallthrough to type conversion
08051                         }
08052 
08053                         default:
08054                                 assert(!"Wrong expression for return type node set");
08055                                 return xpath_node_set_raw();
08056                         }
08057                 }
08058                 
08059                 bool is_posinv()
08060                 {
08061                         switch (_type)
08062                         {
08063                         case ast_func_position:
08064                                 return false;
08065 
08066                         case ast_string_constant:
08067                         case ast_number_constant:
08068                         case ast_variable:
08069                                 return true;
08070 
08071                         case ast_step:
08072                         case ast_step_root:
08073                                 return true;
08074 
08075                         case ast_predicate:
08076                         case ast_filter:
08077                         case ast_filter_posinv:
08078                                 return true;
08079 
08080                         default:
08081                                 if (_left && !_left->is_posinv()) return false;
08082                                 
08083                                 for (xpath_ast_node* n = _right; n; n = n->_next)
08084                                         if (!n->is_posinv()) return false;
08085                                         
08086                                 return true;
08087                         }
08088                 }
08089 
08090                 xpath_value_type rettype() const
08091                 {
08092                         return static_cast<xpath_value_type>(_rettype);
08093                 }
08094         };
08095 
08096         struct xpath_parser
08097         {
08098             xpath_allocator* _alloc;
08099             xpath_lexer _lexer;
08100 
08101                 const char_t* _query;
08102                 xpath_variable_set* _variables;
08103 
08104                 xpath_parse_result* _result;
08105 
08106         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
08107                 jmp_buf _error_handler;
08108         #endif
08109 
08110                 void throw_error(const char* message)
08111                 {
08112                         _result->error = message;
08113                         _result->offset = _lexer.current_pos() - _query;
08114 
08115                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
08116                         longjmp(_error_handler, 1);
08117                 #else
08118                         throw xpath_exception(*_result);
08119                 #endif
08120                 }
08121 
08122                 void throw_error_oom()
08123         {
08124         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
08125             throw_error("Out of memory");
08126         #else
08127             throw std::bad_alloc();
08128         #endif
08129         }
08130 
08131                 void* alloc_node()
08132                 {
08133                         void* result = _alloc->allocate_nothrow(sizeof(xpath_ast_node));
08134 
08135                         if (!result) throw_error_oom();
08136 
08137                         return result;
08138                 }
08139 
08140                 const char_t* alloc_string(const xpath_lexer_string& value)
08141                 {
08142                         if (value.begin)
08143                         {
08144                                 size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(value.end - value.begin);
08145 
08146                                 char_t* c = static_cast<char_t*>(_alloc->allocate_nothrow((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
08147                                 if (!c) throw_error_oom();
08148 
08149                                 memcpy(c, value.begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
08150                                 c[length] = 0;
08151 
08152                                 return c;
08153                         }
08154                         else return 0;
08155                 }
08156 
08157                 xpath_ast_node* parse_function_helper(ast_type_t type0, ast_type_t type1, size_t argc, xpath_ast_node* args[2])
08158                 {
08159                         assert(argc <= 1);
08160 
08161                         if (argc == 1 && args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
08162 
08163                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? type0 : type1, xpath_type_string, args[0]);
08164                 }
08165 
08166                 xpath_ast_node* parse_function(const xpath_lexer_string& name, size_t argc, xpath_ast_node* args[2])
08167                 {
08168                         switch (name.begin[0])
08169                         {
08170                         case 'b':
08171                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("boolean") && argc == 1)
08172                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_boolean, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
08173                                         
08174                                 break;
08175                         
08176                         case 'c':
08177                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("count") && argc == 1)
08178                                 {
08179                                         if (args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
08180                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_count, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08181                                 }
08182                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("contains") && argc == 2)
08183                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_contains, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08184                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("concat") && argc >= 2)
08185                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_concat, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08186                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ceiling") && argc == 1)
08187                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_ceiling, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08188                                         
08189                                 break;
08190                         
08191                         case 'f':
08192                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("false") && argc == 0)
08193                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_false, xpath_type_boolean);
08194                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("floor") && argc == 1)
08195                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_floor, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08196                                         
08197                                 break;
08198                         
08199                         case 'i':
08200                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("id") && argc == 1)
08201                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_id, xpath_type_node_set, args[0]);
08202                                         
08203                                 break;
08204                         
08205                         case 'l':
08206                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("last") && argc == 0)
08207                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_last, xpath_type_number);
08208                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("lang") && argc == 1)
08209                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_lang, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
08210                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("local-name") && argc <= 1)
08211                                         return parse_function_helper(ast_func_local_name_0, ast_func_local_name_1, argc, args);
08212                         
08213                                 break;
08214                         
08215                         case 'n':
08216                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("name") && argc <= 1)
08217                                         return parse_function_helper(ast_func_name_0, ast_func_name_1, argc, args);
08218                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("namespace-uri") && argc <= 1)
08219                                         return parse_function_helper(ast_func_namespace_uri_0, ast_func_namespace_uri_1, argc, args);
08220                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("normalize-space") && argc <= 1)
08221                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_normalize_space_0 : ast_func_normalize_space_1, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08222                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("not") && argc == 1)
08223                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_not, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
08224                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("number") && argc <= 1)
08225                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_number_0 : ast_func_number_1, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08226                         
08227                                 break;
08228                         
08229                         case 'p':
08230                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("position") && argc == 0)
08231                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_position, xpath_type_number);
08232                                 
08233                                 break;
08234                         
08235                         case 'r':
08236                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("round") && argc == 1)
08237                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_round, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08238 
08239                                 break;
08240                         
08241                         case 's':
08242                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("string") && argc <= 1)
08243                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_string_0 : ast_func_string_1, xpath_type_string, args[0]);
08244                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("string-length") && argc <= 1)
08245                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_string_length_0 : ast_func_string_length_1, xpath_type_string, args[0]);
08246                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("starts-with") && argc == 2)
08247                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_starts_with, xpath_type_boolean, args[0], args[1]);
08248                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring-before") && argc == 2)
08249                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_substring_before, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08250                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring-after") && argc == 2)
08251                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_substring_after, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08252                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring") && (argc == 2 || argc == 3))
08253                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 2 ? ast_func_substring_2 : ast_func_substring_3, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08254                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("sum") && argc == 1)
08255                                 {
08256                                         if (args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
08257                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_sum, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
08258                                 }
08259 
08260                                 break;
08261                         
08262                         case 't':
08263                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("translate") && argc == 3)
08264                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_translate, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
08265                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("true") && argc == 0)
08266                                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_true, xpath_type_boolean);
08267                                         
08268                                 break;
08269                         }
08270 
08271                         throw_error("Unrecognized function or wrong parameter count");
08272 
08273                         return 0;
08274                 }
08275 
08276                 axis_t parse_axis_name(const xpath_lexer_string& name, bool& specified)
08277                 {
08278                         specified = true;
08279 
08280                         switch (name.begin[0])
08281                         {
08282                         case 'a':
08283                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ancestor"))
08284                                         return axis_ancestor;
08285                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ancestor-or-self"))
08286                                         return axis_ancestor_or_self;
08287                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("attribute"))
08288                                         return axis_attribute;
08289                                 
08290                                 break;
08291                         
08292                         case 'c':
08293                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("child"))
08294                                         return axis_child;
08295                                 
08296                                 break;
08297                         
08298                         case 'd':
08299                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("descendant"))
08300                                         return axis_descendant;
08301                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("descendant-or-self"))
08302                                         return axis_descendant_or_self;
08303                                 
08304                                 break;
08305                         
08306                         case 'f':
08307                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("following"))
08308                                         return axis_following;
08309                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("following-sibling"))
08310                                         return axis_following_sibling;
08311                                 
08312                                 break;
08313                         
08314                         case 'n':
08315                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("namespace"))
08316                                         return axis_namespace;
08317                                 
08318                                 break;
08319                         
08320                         case 'p':
08321                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("parent"))
08322                                         return axis_parent;
08323                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("preceding"))
08324                                         return axis_preceding;
08325                                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("preceding-sibling"))
08326                                         return axis_preceding_sibling;
08327                                 
08328                                 break;
08329                         
08330                         case 's':
08331                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("self"))
08332                                         return axis_self;
08333                                 
08334                                 break;
08335                         }
08336 
08337                         specified = false;
08338                         return axis_child;
08339                 }
08340 
08341                 nodetest_t parse_node_test_type(const xpath_lexer_string& name)
08342                 {
08343                         switch (name.begin[0])
08344                         {
08345                         case 'c':
08346                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("comment"))
08347                                         return nodetest_type_comment;
08348 
08349                                 break;
08350 
08351                         case 'n':
08352                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("node"))
08353                                         return nodetest_type_node;
08354 
08355                                 break;
08356 
08357                         case 'p':
08358                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("processing-instruction"))
08359                                         return nodetest_type_pi;
08360 
08361                                 break;
08362 
08363                         case 't':
08364                                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("text"))
08365                                         return nodetest_type_text;
08366 
08367                                 break;
08368                         }
08369 
08370                         return nodetest_none;
08371                 }
08372 
08373             // PrimaryExpr ::= VariableReference | '(' Expr ')' | Literal | Number | FunctionCall
08374             xpath_ast_node* parse_primary_expression()
08375             {
08376                 switch (_lexer.current())
08377                 {
08378                 case lex_var_ref:
08379                 {
08380                                 xpath_lexer_string name = _lexer.contents();
08381 
08382                                 if (!_variables)
08383                                         throw_error("Unknown variable: variable set is not provided");
08384 
08385                                 xpath_variable* var = get_variable(_variables, name.begin, name.end);
08386 
08387                                 if (!var)
08388                                         throw_error("Unknown variable: variable set does not contain the given name");
08389 
08390                                 _lexer.next();
08391 
08392                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_variable, var->type(), var);
08393                         }
08394 
08395                         case lex_open_brace:
08396                         {
08397                                 _lexer.next();
08398 
08399                                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_expression();
08400 
08401                                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
08402                                         throw_error("Unmatched braces");
08403 
08404                                 _lexer.next();
08405 
08406                                 return n;
08407                         }
08408 
08409                         case lex_quoted_string:
08410                         {
08411                                 const char_t* value = alloc_string(_lexer.contents());
08412 
08413                                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_string_constant, xpath_type_string, value);
08414                                 _lexer.next();
08415 
08416                                 return n;
08417                         }
08418 
08419                         case lex_number:
08420                         {
08421                                 double value = 0;
08422 
08423                                 if (!convert_string_to_number(_lexer.contents().begin, _lexer.contents().end, &value))
08424                                         throw_error_oom();
08425 
08426                                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_number_constant, xpath_type_number, value);
08427                                 _lexer.next();
08428 
08429                                 return n;
08430                         }
08431 
08432                         case lex_string:
08433                         {
08434                                 xpath_ast_node* args[2] = {0};
08435                                 size_t argc = 0;
08436                                 
08437                                 xpath_lexer_string function = _lexer.contents();
08438                                 _lexer.next();
08439                                 
08440                                 xpath_ast_node* last_arg = 0;
08441                                 
08442                                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_open_brace)
08443                                         throw_error("Unrecognized function call");
08444                                 _lexer.next();
08445 
08446                                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
08447                                         args[argc++] = parse_expression();
08448 
08449                                 while (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
08450                                 {
08451                                         if (_lexer.current() != lex_comma)
08452                                                 throw_error("No comma between function arguments");
08453                                         _lexer.next();
08454                                         
08455                                         xpath_ast_node* n = parse_expression();
08456                                         
08457                                         if (argc < 2) args[argc] = n;
08458                                         else last_arg->set_next(n);
08459 
08460                                         argc++;
08461                                         last_arg = n;
08462                                 }
08463                                 
08464                                 _lexer.next();
08465 
08466                                 return parse_function(function, argc, args);
08467                         }
08468 
08469                 default:
08470                         throw_error("Unrecognizable primary expression");
08471 
08472                         return 0;
08473                 }
08474             }
08475             
08476             // FilterExpr ::= PrimaryExpr | FilterExpr Predicate
08477             // Predicate ::= '[' PredicateExpr ']'
08478             // PredicateExpr ::= Expr
08479             xpath_ast_node* parse_filter_expression()
08480             {
08481                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_primary_expression();
08482 
08483                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_open_square_brace)
08484                 {
08485                         _lexer.next();
08486 
08487                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_expression();
08488 
08489                                 if (n->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Predicate has to be applied to node set");
08490 
08491                                 bool posinv = expr->rettype() != xpath_type_number && expr->is_posinv();
08492 
08493                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(posinv ? ast_filter_posinv : ast_filter, xpath_type_node_set, n, expr);
08494 
08495                         if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_square_brace)
08496                                 throw_error("Unmatched square brace");
08497                 
08498                         _lexer.next();
08499                 }
08500                 
08501                 return n;
08502             }
08503             
08504             // Step ::= AxisSpecifier NodeTest Predicate* | AbbreviatedStep
08505             // AxisSpecifier ::= AxisName '::' | '@'?
08506             // NodeTest ::= NameTest | NodeType '(' ')' | 'processing-instruction' '(' Literal ')'
08507             // NameTest ::= '*' | NCName ':' '*' | QName
08508             // AbbreviatedStep ::= '.' | '..'
08509             xpath_ast_node* parse_step(xpath_ast_node* set)
08510             {
08511                         if (set && set->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set)
08512                                 throw_error("Step has to be applied to node set");
08513 
08514                         bool axis_specified = false;
08515                         axis_t axis = axis_child; // implied child axis
08516 
08517                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_axis_attribute)
08518                         {
08519                                 axis = axis_attribute;
08520                                 axis_specified = true;
08521                                 
08522                                 _lexer.next();
08523                         }
08524                         else if (_lexer.current() == lex_dot)
08525                         {
08526                                 _lexer.next();
08527                                 
08528                                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
08529                         }
08530                         else if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_dot)
08531                         {
08532                                 _lexer.next();
08533                                 
08534                                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis_parent, nodetest_type_node, 0);
08535                         }
08536             
08537                         nodetest_t nt_type = nodetest_none;
08538                         xpath_lexer_string nt_name;
08539                         
08540                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
08541                         {
08542                                 // node name test
08543                                 nt_name = _lexer.contents();
08544                                 _lexer.next();
08545 
08546                                 // was it an axis name?
08547                                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_colon)
08548                                 {
08549                                         // parse axis name
08550                                         if (axis_specified) throw_error("Two axis specifiers in one step");
08551 
08552                                         axis = parse_axis_name(nt_name, axis_specified);
08553 
08554                                         if (!axis_specified) throw_error("Unknown axis");
08555 
08556                                         // read actual node test
08557                                         _lexer.next();
08558 
08559                                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_multiply)
08560                                         {
08561                                                 nt_type = nodetest_all;
08562                                                 nt_name = xpath_lexer_string();
08563                                                 _lexer.next();
08564                                         }
08565                                         else if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
08566                                         {
08567                                                 nt_name = _lexer.contents();
08568                                                 _lexer.next();
08569                                         }
08570                                         else throw_error("Unrecognized node test");
08571                                 }
08572                                 
08573                                 if (nt_type == nodetest_none)
08574                                 {
08575                                         // node type test or processing-instruction
08576                                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_open_brace)
08577                                         {
08578                                                 _lexer.next();
08579                                                 
08580                                                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_close_brace)
08581                                                 {
08582                                                         _lexer.next();
08583 
08584                                                         nt_type = parse_node_test_type(nt_name);
08585 
08586                                                         if (nt_type == nodetest_none) throw_error("Unrecognized node type");
08587                                                         
08588                                                         nt_name = xpath_lexer_string();
08589                                                 }
08590                                                 else if (nt_name == PUGIXML_TEXT("processing-instruction"))
08591                                                 {
08592                                                         if (_lexer.current() != lex_quoted_string)
08593                                                                 throw_error("Only literals are allowed as arguments to processing-instruction()");
08594                                                 
08595                                                         nt_type = nodetest_pi;
08596                                                         nt_name = _lexer.contents();
08597                                                         _lexer.next();
08598                                                         
08599                                                         if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
08600                                                                 throw_error("Unmatched brace near processing-instruction()");
08601                                                         _lexer.next();
08602                                                 }
08603                                                 else
08604                                                         throw_error("Unmatched brace near node type test");
08605 
08606                                         }
08607                                         // QName or NCName:*
08608                                         else
08609                                         {
08610                                                 if (nt_name.end - nt_name.begin > 2 && nt_name.end[-2] == ':' && nt_name.end[-1] == '*') // NCName:*
08611                                                 {
08612                                                         nt_name.end--; // erase *
08613                                                         
08614                                                         nt_type = nodetest_all_in_namespace;
08615                                                 }
08616                                                 else nt_type = nodetest_name;
08617                                         }
08618                                 }
08619                         }
08620                         else if (_lexer.current() == lex_multiply)
08621                         {
08622                                 nt_type = nodetest_all;
08623                                 _lexer.next();
08624                         }
08625                         else throw_error("Unrecognized node test");
08626                         
08627                         xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis, nt_type, alloc_string(nt_name));
08628                         
08629                         xpath_ast_node* last = 0;
08630                         
08631                         while (_lexer.current() == lex_open_square_brace)
08632                         {
08633                                 _lexer.next();
08634                                 
08635                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_expression();
08636 
08637                                 xpath_ast_node* pred = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_predicate, xpath_type_node_set, expr);
08638                                 
08639                                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_square_brace)
08640                                 throw_error("Unmatched square brace");
08641                                 _lexer.next();
08642                                 
08643                                 if (last) last->set_next(pred);
08644                                 else n->set_right(pred);
08645                                 
08646                                 last = pred;
08647                         }
08648                         
08649                         return n;
08650             }
08651             
08652             // RelativeLocationPath ::= Step | RelativeLocationPath '/' Step | RelativeLocationPath '//' Step
08653             xpath_ast_node* parse_relative_location_path(xpath_ast_node* set)
08654             {
08655                         xpath_ast_node* n = parse_step(set);
08656                         
08657                         while (_lexer.current() == lex_slash || _lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
08658                         {
08659                                 lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08660                                 _lexer.next();
08661 
08662                                 if (l == lex_double_slash)
08663                                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
08664                                 
08665                                 n = parse_step(n);
08666                         }
08667                         
08668                         return n;
08669             }
08670             
08671             // LocationPath ::= RelativeLocationPath | AbsoluteLocationPath
08672             // AbsoluteLocationPath ::= '/' RelativeLocationPath? | '//' RelativeLocationPath
08673             xpath_ast_node* parse_location_path()
08674             {
08675                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_slash)
08676                         {
08677                                 _lexer.next();
08678                                 
08679                                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step_root, xpath_type_node_set);
08680 
08681                                 // relative location path can start from axis_attribute, dot, double_dot, multiply and string lexemes; any other lexeme means standalone root path
08682                                 lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08683 
08684                                 if (l == lex_string || l == lex_axis_attribute || l == lex_dot || l == lex_double_dot || l == lex_multiply)
08685                                         return parse_relative_location_path(n);
08686                                 else
08687                                         return n;
08688                         }
08689                         else if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
08690                         {
08691                                 _lexer.next();
08692                                 
08693                                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step_root, xpath_type_node_set);
08694                                 n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
08695                                 
08696                                 return parse_relative_location_path(n);
08697                         }
08698 
08699                         // else clause moved outside of if because of bogus warning 'control may reach end of non-void function being inlined' in gcc 4.0.1
08700                         return parse_relative_location_path(0);
08701             }
08702             
08703             // PathExpr ::= LocationPath
08704             //                          | FilterExpr
08705             //                          | FilterExpr '/' RelativeLocationPath
08706             //                          | FilterExpr '//' RelativeLocationPath
08707             xpath_ast_node* parse_path_expression()
08708             {
08709                         // Clarification.
08710                         // PathExpr begins with either LocationPath or FilterExpr.
08711                         // FilterExpr begins with PrimaryExpr
08712                         // PrimaryExpr begins with '$' in case of it being a variable reference,
08713                         // '(' in case of it being an expression, string literal, number constant or
08714                         // function call.
08715 
08716                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_var_ref || _lexer.current() == lex_open_brace || 
08717                                 _lexer.current() == lex_quoted_string || _lexer.current() == lex_number ||
08718                                 _lexer.current() == lex_string)
08719                 {
08720                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
08721                         {
08722                                 // This is either a function call, or not - if not, we shall proceed with location path
08723                                 const char_t* state = _lexer.state();
08724                                 
08725                                         while (IS_CHARTYPE(*state, ct_space)) ++state;
08726                                 
08727                                 if (*state != '(') return parse_location_path();
08728 
08729                                         // This looks like a function call; however this still can be a node-test. Check it.
08730                                         if (parse_node_test_type(_lexer.contents()) != nodetest_none) return parse_location_path();
08731                         }
08732                         
08733                         xpath_ast_node* n = parse_filter_expression();
08734 
08735                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_slash || _lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
08736                         {
08737                                         lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08738                                 _lexer.next();
08739                                 
08740                                         if (l == lex_double_slash)
08741                                         {
08742                                                 if (n->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Step has to be applied to node set");
08743 
08744                                                 n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
08745                                         }
08746         
08747                                 // select from location path
08748                                 return parse_relative_location_path(n);
08749                         }
08750 
08751                         return n;
08752                 }
08753                 else return parse_location_path();
08754             }
08755 
08756             // UnionExpr ::= PathExpr | UnionExpr '|' PathExpr
08757             xpath_ast_node* parse_union_expression()
08758             {
08759                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_path_expression();
08760 
08761                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_union)
08762                 {
08763                         _lexer.next();
08764 
08765                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_union_expression();
08766 
08767                                 if (n->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set || expr->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set)
08768                                         throw_error("Union operator has to be applied to node sets");
08769 
08770                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_op_union, xpath_type_node_set, n, expr);
08771                 }
08772 
08773                 return n;
08774             }
08775 
08776             // UnaryExpr ::= UnionExpr | '-' UnaryExpr
08777             xpath_ast_node* parse_unary_expression()
08778             {
08779                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_minus)
08780                 {
08781                         _lexer.next();
08782 
08783                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_unary_expression();
08784 
08785                         return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_op_negate, xpath_type_number, expr);
08786                 }
08787                 else return parse_union_expression();
08788             }
08789             
08790             // MultiplicativeExpr ::= UnaryExpr
08791             //                                            | MultiplicativeExpr '*' UnaryExpr
08792             //                                            | MultiplicativeExpr 'div' UnaryExpr
08793             //                                            | MultiplicativeExpr 'mod' UnaryExpr
08794             xpath_ast_node* parse_multiplicative_expression()
08795             {
08796                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_unary_expression();
08797 
08798                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_multiply || (_lexer.current() == lex_string &&
08799                            (_lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("mod") || _lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("div"))))
08800                 {
08801                         ast_type_t op = _lexer.current() == lex_multiply ? ast_op_multiply :
08802                                 _lexer.contents().begin[0] == 'd' ? ast_op_divide : ast_op_mod;
08803                         _lexer.next();
08804 
08805                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_unary_expression();
08806 
08807                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(op, xpath_type_number, n, expr);
08808                 }
08809 
08810                 return n;
08811             }
08812 
08813             // AdditiveExpr ::= MultiplicativeExpr
08814             //                                  | AdditiveExpr '+' MultiplicativeExpr
08815             //                                  | AdditiveExpr '-' MultiplicativeExpr
08816             xpath_ast_node* parse_additive_expression()
08817             {
08818                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_multiplicative_expression();
08819 
08820                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_plus || _lexer.current() == lex_minus)
08821                 {
08822                         lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08823 
08824                         _lexer.next();
08825 
08826                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_multiplicative_expression();
08827 
08828                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(l == lex_plus ? ast_op_add : ast_op_subtract, xpath_type_number, n, expr);
08829                 }
08830 
08831                 return n;
08832             }
08833 
08834             // RelationalExpr ::= AdditiveExpr
08835             //                                    | RelationalExpr '<' AdditiveExpr
08836             //                                    | RelationalExpr '>' AdditiveExpr
08837             //                                    | RelationalExpr '<=' AdditiveExpr
08838             //                                    | RelationalExpr '>=' AdditiveExpr
08839             xpath_ast_node* parse_relational_expression()
08840             {
08841                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_additive_expression();
08842 
08843                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_less || _lexer.current() == lex_less_or_equal || 
08844                            _lexer.current() == lex_greater || _lexer.current() == lex_greater_or_equal)
08845                 {
08846                         lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08847                         _lexer.next();
08848 
08849                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_additive_expression();
08850 
08851                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(l == lex_less ? ast_op_less : l == lex_greater ? ast_op_greater :
08852                                                         l == lex_less_or_equal ? ast_op_less_or_equal : ast_op_greater_or_equal, xpath_type_boolean, n, expr);
08853                 }
08854 
08855                 return n;
08856             }
08857             
08858             // EqualityExpr ::= RelationalExpr
08859             //                                  | EqualityExpr '=' RelationalExpr
08860             //                                  | EqualityExpr '!=' RelationalExpr
08861             xpath_ast_node* parse_equality_expression()
08862             {
08863                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_relational_expression();
08864 
08865                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_equal || _lexer.current() == lex_not_equal)
08866                 {
08867                         lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
08868 
08869                         _lexer.next();
08870 
08871                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_relational_expression();
08872 
08873                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(l == lex_equal ? ast_op_equal : ast_op_not_equal, xpath_type_boolean, n, expr);
08874                 }
08875 
08876                 return n;
08877             }
08878             
08879             // AndExpr ::= EqualityExpr | AndExpr 'and' EqualityExpr
08880             xpath_ast_node* parse_and_expression()
08881             {
08882                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_equality_expression();
08883 
08884                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_string && _lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("and"))
08885                 {
08886                         _lexer.next();
08887 
08888                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_equality_expression();
08889 
08890                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_op_and, xpath_type_boolean, n, expr);
08891                 }
08892 
08893                 return n;
08894             }
08895 
08896             // OrExpr ::= AndExpr | OrExpr 'or' AndExpr
08897             xpath_ast_node* parse_or_expression()
08898             {
08899                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_and_expression();
08900 
08901                 while (_lexer.current() == lex_string && _lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("or"))
08902                 {
08903                         _lexer.next();
08904 
08905                                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_and_expression();
08906 
08907                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_op_or, xpath_type_boolean, n, expr);
08908                 }
08909 
08910                 return n;
08911             }
08912                 
08913                 // Expr ::= OrExpr
08914                 xpath_ast_node* parse_expression()
08915                 {
08916                         return parse_or_expression();
08917                 }
08918 
08919                 xpath_parser(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables, xpath_allocator* alloc, xpath_parse_result* result): _alloc(alloc), _lexer(query), _query(query), _variables(variables), _result(result)
08920                 {
08921                 }
08922 
08923                 xpath_ast_node* parse()
08924                 {
08925                         xpath_ast_node* result = parse_expression();
08926                         
08927                         if (_lexer.current() != lex_eof)
08928                         {
08929                                 // there are still unparsed tokens left, error
08930                                 throw_error("Incorrect query");
08931                         }
08932                         
08933                         return result;
08934                 }
08935 
08936                 static xpath_ast_node* parse(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables, xpath_allocator* alloc, xpath_parse_result* result)
08937                 {
08938                         xpath_parser parser(query, variables, alloc, result);
08939 
08940                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
08941                         int error = setjmp(parser._error_handler);
08942 
08943                         return (error == 0) ? parser.parse() : 0;
08944                 #else
08945                         return parser.parse();
08946                 #endif
08947                 }
08948         };
08949 
08950     struct xpath_query_impl
08951     {
08952                 static xpath_query_impl* create()
08953                 {
08954                         void* memory = global_allocate(sizeof(xpath_query_impl));
08955 
08956             return new (memory) xpath_query_impl();
08957                 }
08958 
08959                 static void destroy(void* ptr)
08960                 {
08961                         if (!ptr) return;
08962                         
08963                         // free all allocated pages
08964                         static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(ptr)->alloc.release();
08965 
08966                         // free allocator memory (with the first page)
08967                         global_deallocate(ptr);
08968                 }
08969 
08970         xpath_query_impl(): root(0), alloc(&block)
08971         {
08972             block.next = 0;
08973         }
08974 
08975         xpath_ast_node* root;
08976         xpath_allocator alloc;
08977         xpath_memory_block block;
08978     };
08979 
08980         xpath_string evaluate_string_impl(xpath_query_impl* impl, const xpath_node& n, xpath_stack_data& sd)
08981         {
08982                 if (!impl) return xpath_string();
08983 
08984         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
08985                 if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return xpath_string();
08986         #endif
08987 
08988                 xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
08989 
08990                 return impl->root->eval_string(c, sd.stack);
08991         }
08992 }

09038         }

09040         xpath_node::operator xpath_node::unspecified_bool_type() const
09041         {
09042                 return (_node || _attribute) ? &xpath_node::_node : 0;
09043         }
09044         
09045         bool xpath_node::operator!() const
09046         {
09047                 return !(_node || _attribute);
09048         }
09049 
09050         bool xpath_node::operator==(const xpath_node& n) const
09051         {
09052                 return _node == n._node && _attribute == n._attribute;
09053         }
09054         
09055         bool xpath_node::operator!=(const xpath_node& n) const
09056         {
09057                 return _node != n._node || _attribute != n._attribute;
09058         }

09060 #ifdef __BORLANDC__
09061         bool operator&&(const xpath_node& lhs, bool rhs)
09062         {
09063                 return (bool)lhs && rhs;
09064         }
09065

09067         {
09068                 return (bool)lhs || rhs;
09069         }

09071 
09072         void xpath_node_set::_assign(const_iterator begin, const_iterator end)
09073         {
09074                 assert(begin <= end);
09075 
09076                 size_t size = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
09077 
09078                 if (size <= 1)
09079                 {
09080                         // deallocate old buffer
09081                         if (_begin != &_storage) global_deallocate(_begin);
09082 
09083                         // use internal buffer
09084                         if (begin != end) _storage = *begin;
09085 
09086                         _begin = &_storage;
09087                         _end = &_storage + size;
09088                 }
09089                 else
09090                 {
09091                         // make heap copy
09092                         xpath_node* storage = static_cast<xpath_node*>(global_allocate(size * sizeof(xpath_node)));
09093 
09094                         if (!storage)
09095                         {
09096                         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
09097                                 return;
09098                         #else
09099                                 throw std::bad_alloc();
09100                         #endif
09101                         }
09102 
09103                         memcpy(storage, begin, size * sizeof(xpath_node));
09104                         
09105                         // deallocate old buffer
09106                         if (_begin != &_storage) global_deallocate(_begin);
09107 
09108                         // finalize
09109                         _begin = storage;
09110                         _end = storage + size;
09111                 }
09112         }
09113 
09114         xpath_node_set::xpath_node_set(): _type(type_unsorted), _begin(&_storage), _end(&_storage)
09115         {
09116         }
09117 
09118         xpath_node_set::xpath_node_set(const_iterator begin, const_iterator end, type_t type): _type(type), _begin(&_storage), _end(&_storage)
09119         {
09120                 _assign(begin, end);
09121         }
09122 
09123         xpath_node_set::~xpath_node_set()
09124         {
09125                 if (_begin != &_storage) global_deallocate(_begin);
09126         }
09127                 
09128         xpath_node_set::xpath_node_set(const xpath_node_set& ns): _type(ns._type), _begin(&_storage), _end(&_storage)
09129         {
09130                 _assign(ns._begin, ns._end);
09131         }
09132         
09133         xpath_node_set& xpath_node_set::operator=(const xpath_node_set& ns)
09134         {
09135                 if (this == &ns) return *this;
09136                 
09137                 _type = ns._type;
09138                 _assign(ns._begin, ns._end);
09139 
09140                 return *this;
09141         }
09142 
09143         xpath_node_set::type_t xpath_node_set::type() const
09144         {
09145                 return _type;
09146         }
09147                 
09148         size_t xpath_node_set::size() const
09149         {
09150                 return _end - _begin;
09151         }
09152                 
09153         bool xpath_node_set::empty() const
09154         {
09155                 return _begin == _end;
09156         }
09157                 
09158         const xpath_node& xpath_node_set::operator[](size_t index) const
09159         {
09160                 assert(index < size());
09161                 return _begin[index];
09162         }
09163 
09164         xpath_node_set::const_iterator xpath_node_set::begin() const
09165         {
09166                 return _begin;
09167         }
09168                 
09169         xpath_node_set::const_iterator xpath_node_set::end() const
09170         {
09171                 return _end;
09172         }
09173         
09174         void xpath_node_set::sort(bool reverse)
09175         {
09176                 _type = xpath_sort(_begin, _end, _type, reverse);
09177         }
09178 
09179         xpath_node xpath_node_set::first() const
09180         {
09181                 return xpath_first(_begin, _end, _type);
09182         }

09184     xpath_parse_result::xpath_parse_result(): error("Internal error"), offset(0)
09185     {
09186     }
09187 
09188     xpath_parse_result::operator bool() const
09189     {
09190         return error == 0;
09191     }
09192         const char* xpath_parse_result::description() const
09193         {
09194                 return error ? error : "No error";

09201         const char_t* xpath_variable::name() const
09202         {
09203                 switch (_type)
09204                 {
09205                 case xpath_type_node_set:
09206                         return static_cast<const xpath_variable_node_set*>(this)->name;
09207 
09208                 case xpath_type_number:
09209                         return static_cast<const xpath_variable_number*>(this)->name;
09210 
09211                 case xpath_type_string:
09212                         return static_cast<const xpath_variable_string*>(this)->name;
09213 
09214                 case xpath_type_boolean:
09215                         return static_cast<const xpath_variable_boolean*>(this)->name;
09216 
09217                 default:
09218                         assert(!"Invalid variable type");
09219                         return 0;
09220                 }
09221         }

09265         bool xpath_variable::set(const char_t* value)
09266         {
09267                 if (_type != xpath_type_string) return false;
09268 
09269                 xpath_variable_string* var = static_cast<xpath_variable_string*>(this);
09270 
09271                 // duplicate string
09272                 size_t size = (strlength(value) + 1) * sizeof(char_t);
09273 
09274                 char_t* copy = static_cast<char_t*>(global_allocate(size));
09275                 if (!copy) return false;
09276 
09277                 memcpy(copy, value, size);
09278 
09279                 // replace old string
09280                 if (var->value) global_deallocate(var->value);
09281                 var->value = copy;
09282 
09283                 return true;
09284         }

09294         xpath_variable_set::xpath_variable_set()
09295         {
09296                 for (size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]); ++i) _data[i] = 0;
09297         }

09299         xpath_variable_set::~xpath_variable_set()
09300         {
09301                 for (size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]); ++i)
09302                 {
09303                         xpath_variable* var = _data[i];
09304 
09305                         while (var)
09306                         {
09307                                 xpath_variable* next = var->_next;
09308 
09309                                 delete_xpath_variable(var->_type, var);
09310 
09311                                 var = next;
09312                         }
09313                 }
09314         }
09315 
09316         xpath_variable* xpath_variable_set::find(const char_t* name) const
09317         {
09318                 const size_t hash_size = sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]);
09319                 size_t hash = hash_string(name) % hash_size;
09320 
09321                 // look for existing variable
09322                 for (xpath_variable* var = _data[hash]; var; var = var->_next)
09323                         if (strequal(var->name(), name))
09324                                 return var;
09325 
09326                 return 0;
09327         }
09328 
09329         xpath_variable* xpath_variable_set::add(const char_t* name, xpath_value_type type)
09330         {
09331                 const size_t hash_size = sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]);
09332                 size_t hash = hash_string(name) % hash_size;
09333 
09334                 // look for existing variable
09335                 for (xpath_variable* var = _data[hash]; var; var = var->_next)
09336                         if (strequal(var->name(), name))
09337                                 return var->type() == type ? var : 0;
09338 
09339                 // add new variable
09340                 xpath_variable* result = new_xpath_variable(type, name);
09341 
09342                 if (result)
09343                 {
09344                         result->_type = type;
09345                         result->_next = _data[hash];
09346 
09347                         _data[hash] = result;
09348                 }
09349 
09350                 return result;
09351         }

09387         xpath_query::xpath_query(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables): _impl(0)
09388         {
09389                 xpath_query_impl* impl = xpath_query_impl::create();
09390 
09391                 if (!impl)
09392                 {
09393                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
09394                         _result.error = "Out of memory";
09395         #else
09396                         throw std::bad_alloc();
09397                 #endif
09398                 }
09399                 else
09400                 {
09401                         buffer_holder impl_holder(impl, xpath_query_impl::destroy);
09402 
09403                         impl->root = xpath_parser::parse(query, variables, &impl->alloc, &_result);
09404 
09405                         if (impl->root)
09406                         {
09407                 _impl = static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(impl_holder.release());
09408                                 _result.error = 0;
09409                         }
09410                 }
09411         }
09412 
09413         xpath_query::~xpath_query()
09414         {
09415                 xpath_query_impl::destroy(_impl);
09416         }

09419         {
09420                 if (!_impl) return xpath_type_none;
09421 
09422                 return static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(_impl)->root->rettype();
09423         }

09425         bool xpath_query::evaluate_boolean(const xpath_node& n) const
09426         {
09427                 if (!_impl) return false;
09428                 
09429                 xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
09430                 xpath_stack_data sd;
09431 
09432         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
09433                 if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return false;
09434         #endif
09435                 
09436                 return static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(_impl)->root->eval_boolean(c, sd.stack);
09437         }

09453 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
09454         string_t xpath_query::evaluate_string(const xpath_node& n) const
09455         {

09461 
09462         size_t xpath_query::evaluate_string(char_t* buffer, size_t capacity, const xpath_node& n) const
09463         {
09464                 xpath_stack_data sd;
09465 
09466                 xpath_string r = evaluate_string_impl(static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(_impl), n, sd);
09467 
09468                 size_t full_size = r.length() + 1;
09469                 
09470                 if (capacity > 0)
09471         {
09472             size_t size = (full_size < capacity) ? full_size : capacity;
09473             assert(size > 0);
09474 
09475             memcpy(buffer, r.c_str(), (size - 1) * sizeof(char_t));
09476             buffer[size - 1] = 0;
09477         }
09478                 
09479                 return full_size;
09480         }
09481 
09482         xpath_node_set xpath_query::evaluate_node_set(const xpath_node& n) const
09483         {
09484                 if (!_impl) return xpath_node_set();
09485 
09486         xpath_ast_node* root = static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(_impl)->root;
09487 
09488                 if (root->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set)
09489                 {
09490                 #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
09491                         return xpath_node_set();
09492                 #else
09493                         xpath_parse_result result;
09494                         result.error = "Expression does not evaluate to node set";
09495 
09496                         throw xpath_exception(result);
09497                 #endif
09498                 }
09499                 
09500                 xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
09501                 xpath_stack_data sd;
09502 
09503         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
09504                 if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return xpath_node_set();
09505         #endif
09506 
09507                 xpath_node_set_raw r = root->eval_node_set(c, sd.stack);
09508 
09509                 return xpath_node_set(r.begin(), r.end(), r.type());
09510         }
